# CloudPOS SDK

This comprehensive documentation aims to guide Android application developers for the Smart POS. It covers EMV payment specifications, barcode scanning, the Device Java API, API details, samples, a quick start guide, and additional resources.

For more details, please refer to the provided links and sections.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk#emv-payment)

EMV Payment

The EMV Payment SDK is designed to facilitate the development of payment applications (APPs).

*   [EMV Develop Spec](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/emv-develop-spec)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk#barcode-scanning)

Barcode Scanning

*   [Scanning Service Usage](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/scanning-service-usage)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk#device-java-api)

Device Java API

The Device Java API simplifies development by being packaged as an AAR library file, providing Android developers with easy integration. This API includes functionalities such as Printer, PINPad, MSR, SmartCard, RFCard, SerialPort, LED, Fingerprint, and HSM.

*   [API Specificationsarrow-up-right](http://sdkwiki.wizarpos.com/wizarposapi/)
    
*   [API Specifications Downloadarrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/device/java/javadoc_20250527.zip)
    
*   [CloudPOS SDK AAR](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/cloudpos-sdk-aar)
    
*   [Samples](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/java-api-samples)
    
*   [Permissions Definition](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/permissions)
    
*   [Error Code](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/error-code)
    
*   [Printer Technical Manualarrow-up-right](http://ftp.wizarpos.com/device/CloudPOSPrinter_TechnicalManual_20231222_en.pdf)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk#mdb-interface)

MDB Interface

*   [MDB Communication Protocal](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk#quick-start-guide)

Quick Start Guide

*   [USB Driver Download](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/usb-serial-port/install-terminal-usb-drivers)
    
*   [Install App](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/other-development/install-pos-applications)
    
*   [Apply App Certificate](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/certificate/apply-app-certificates)
    
*   [Sign App](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/other-development/app-signing-process)
    
*   [Apply TMS Account](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/apply-wizarview-account)
    
*   [TMS Manualarrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/device/TMSManual.pdf)
    

[NextEMV Develop Specchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/emv-develop-spec)

Last updated 3 days ago

*   [EMV Payment](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk#emv-payment)
    
*   [Barcode Scanning](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk#barcode-scanning)
    
*   [Device Java API](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk#device-java-api)

# Catering Online Store User Guide | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-online-store-user-guide#toc14333)

1.Login


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After the customer scans the ordering QR code, he will be prompted to log in, and then enter the correct account number and password to log in. If there is no account then he has to register first.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FKTXVABBYEHVcLOZi7z5v%252F0.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c87498b0&sv=2)

07bfdc8416055f9512ab8efe5c842d6

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FxEi6mhbsE69HZlqiHAaZ%252F1.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f280894&sv=2)

f8cc39e7a4266e7a8a2b8bb75716679

You can enter your email address to create a new account, and you can reset your password if you forget it.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FgsHSw8m1abNH3a2qjye6%252F2.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c48fc48f&sv=2)

2b7f5c2a9b78fea70622e0005ce64ac

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQGW36UoyndfCTU5wlAAZ%252F3.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88e27639&sv=2)

976f0aff6a8c142ea4648319b91fcf3

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-online-store-user-guide#toc17206)

2.Home


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The home page shows customers the business name and address, as well as dine-in, take-out, dish recommendations, orders and recommended dishes.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FBEeDDBK6ciq41FFTdPBg%252F4.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1ee2f2b1&sv=2)

5085a312fe1b1cc1f137e2190ee8f50

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-online-store-user-guide#toc3235)

3.Dine in


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After scanning the table QR code enter the home page, click Dine in, you will enter the table and order food. There are various specifications of dishes to choose from depending on the restaurant.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F4QkzwiUYthjVJDvjrM9E%252F5.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f78c1523&sv=2)

ba163212cab967f4811f920c1167219

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FD25v5YQw4LVbfZYAtQGP%252F6.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=be2a4b24&sv=2)

3cb62891bc2468f9b18d418d5218d8e

After ordering, you can view, modify and delete the number of dishes in the shopping cart and then you can check out.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FordEIldwYxyLBjlYJdAS%252F7.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea2186f&sv=2)

24d9c45ba671cf11ac40a1cd31303ab

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrTGqw0jDhaAudvqOl4Lm%252F8.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4f6babc&sv=2)

24c58452660919e22b7151d250ddab7

When check out, you can choose whether you want to pay by yourself or split the bill, you can choose the tip ratio, or you can customize the tip amount.

You can choose to pay by membership card or bank card.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FxI4v7dlC3MRPKwPZkOAC%252F9.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec57ba31&sv=2)

a6dd3d23ff3b46722d6ea7743bd2bb6

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F4vXA16fEMzhUvmMe80YF%252F10.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d964a7f9&sv=2)

6f6f29a910a0436f20a158ebd092dba

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FyveKvKnoSCy9xCt629bf%252F11.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b2140a96&sv=2)

02c9be9d8d37e44a3a46baa091e47fb

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-online-store-user-guide#toc30275)

4.Takeout


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Takeaway, the same as dine-in process, the difference between takeaway and dine-in is that there is a packing fee, you can also choose the address, choose whether to pick up or deliver

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F8N8oDXAAWttQNCeZVnwJ%252F12.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4095fa3c&sv=2)

cb30a02354bff5b95dd0382e71b9423

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FLAeJ8TH6vPzEOs4efPqb%252F13.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=320bd808&sv=2)

e8c2a3ab9479bde28e2979a4c5761d3

Choose delivery method or self-pickup

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FCc8RW3p4OaHPDb5YYJXV%252F14.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c1810409&sv=2)

ac9a0ee6ab0a4cd2efd6e3fc85e8231

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FF1Vd18Rwq2da2UEuCwII%252F15.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8fa6b85&sv=2)

5.Recommand


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click More on the home page to enter the list of recommended dishes. You can order food and add it to the shopping cart directly to place an order and checkout

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FRjwZOIKvBxFWkuccftII%252F16.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f47350b&sv=2)

7226c12abdf0f0eeb92a84bbda39d6c

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F60q7FaaJPPS57VxSo6xm%252F17.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3fba05d7&sv=2)

69e44fd9cbf899f5a8e8fe7973dff38

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-online-store-user-guide#toc24936)

6.Orders


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Orders to display all by type, unpaid, refunded, and completed 4 types of orders. Click an order to view the details.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FUhCPTYc2sIVuWx7nqdvn%252F18.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e3d4798&sv=2)

490ee3691c852b767c5ca2d133bfbee

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FAMQ93bFpgXlVglsSDjLZ%252F19.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ab7f6a48&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-online-store-user-guide#toc9850)

7.Mine


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Mine to display my page, which needs to be displayed after the user logs in.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjnnlXKd2z5OVMnndtxGU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b670f5b-a439-4508-aab8-101d3bc13333&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7f9ccd7d&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FkAyhRNcKdlIxeHivD5No%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4f9ba51-5c73-4616-9175-67e1b42d5d83&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dae4f01&sv=2)

After logging in, you can view member information, membership code, point mall, and modify your member information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FwWylOkeKGe3YiovMB8QO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85c78e43-fdbe-42e5-80b7-195fd9a6468b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d70b84a5&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FUxbjfDQPEKd1t5AnE5gq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97c48962-8aa3-40f7-ab62-2ee9441e118c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=74522d9d&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FG9RwqYnMQ0Thv1a9eQC5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a31fa9b-94ef-4c5f-9fa6-15cfebdd26e6&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b353a57b&sv=2)

You can also view your membership balance, consumption records, recharge records

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQnsN3ULcR3b8XHaHnwRV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D330147e2-c7c4-42ae-b016-f728e82f1735&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ad5abde&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FbDzIRnEXRc7vm7HoGCI0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7e20c06-90fe-4103-b511-757edbeb5752&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=184fad15&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0WEVqi3Petfs9chumxhR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1447477b-b8e5-4f12-a5d1-7920d947bf9d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d4d00f5&sv=2)

Points Mall, where you can choose the product you want to exchange by using points.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FxnrNV6dboZqEcuWzZ2ix%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2cecd403-cf60-4c76-875e-b1c27b64ebc2&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fa2a0443&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0qgcmaIlCglET5kNp0DX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c91e3ef-10d9-4c9a-862c-517903ea8628&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64632d5f&sv=2)

Click on Exchange Records, you can redeem the products with your own points, click on the exchanged QR code, go to the store and ask the waiter to scan the code to exchange products.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F7GYzRJD8gmFk1WlXecyT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c14f625-aa49-4970-8717-c4fe9c321362&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a8789e21&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FRBEMeB8QfAXwNkhcFEdv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D382e2a3e-1bbf-4d81-a59a-1739063f99c1&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bab29490&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FVRnFNKwPXWrjFpeCW226%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0eccd0df-cafc-4eaa-bad2-1021ee91b2bb&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=461e60d1&sv=2)

# Catering Terminal APP User Guide | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc18639)

1\. Function overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WizarPOS handheld ordering app is an ordering system for Android POS terminals. Waiters at catering merchants use handheld devices to provide ordering services to customers. The main functions provided by the system are as follows:

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#menu)

**Menu**

The merchant uploads various types of dishes, hot dishes, cold dishes, Western food, dim sum, snacks, etc. And displays all the dishes in the menu. When ordering, the dishes can be customized according to the specifications, tastes, methods, and toppings.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#promotions)

**Promotions**

Merchants can set up various types of marketing activities through the merchant portal, including discounts, full discounts, special offers, points malls, coupons for consumption and other activities, which can provide great dining experiences.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#membership)

**Membership**

Each catering merchant can use the table QR code or takeout QR code to allow customers to scan the QR to register and become a member of the merchant. The waiter can use terminal to recharge for the members, and the member balance can be used when order and pay. Members can get coupons through consumption.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#payment)

**Payment**

Handheld ordering can support cash, bank cards, membership payment, membership coupons and other payment methods.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#points)

**Points**

Merchants can configure goods for exchange in the merchant portal, such as 100 points to exchange for a bottle of Coke, 500 points to exchange for a dish. The waiter uses a terminal to scan the customer's redemption code and redeem the goods for the customer.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc11376)

2\. Login


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to log in to the terminal, you need to enter the merchant ID, username and password.

The merchant ID is when the service provider onboarding the merchant. An assigned merchant ID can be obtained from the email after the merchant is successfully onboarded. At the same time, the merchant administrator account and initial password will be given. The merchant administrator must log in to the merchant backend for the first time, change the initial password, and create an operator account in System Settings -> Account Management. The created operator account can be used to log in to the terminal catering application.

circle-info

**Note:** **The administrator account of the merchant received by email cannot be used to log in to the terminal application.**

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F3NQxfjin2BIrVzAlDHG0%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59e9210e&sv=2)

1dc914aa645d6c4157ad7768a7923bc

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc14554)

3\. Home


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The merchant’s name, merchant number, merchant logo and settings are displayed at the top of the homepage.

**Function list:**

1.  **Dine-In**: In store order.
    
2.  **Takeout**: Takeout food
    
3.  **Bill**: Business report
    
4.  **Report**: Daily summary
    
5.  **Sales Order**: Sales order list
    
6.  **Today Sum**: Dish statistics
    
7.  **Print**: Receipt printing
    
8.  **Tips**: Tips report
    
9.  **Member**: Membership manager
    
10.  **Points**: Points redeem
    
11.  **Reservation**: Wait for a table
    
12.  **Takeout Man**: Takeout order management
    
13.  **Notification**: Message notification
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FF0s9hKUNGn9w8UJY9IvG%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=62a1be61&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc4239)

4\. Dine-in


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Merchants click on Dine-in to the table selection page.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#step-1-choose-table)

Step 1: Choose Table

The table displays the table name, maximum customer of the table allowed and status. The table status is divided into idle and occupied. (Table can be managed at the merchant portal.) Select the table which customer is sitting at to enter the menu.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FBhdqKqp3cfySoQakovRh%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1652718&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#step-2-order)

Step 2: Order

At the menu, you can select dishes according to their types. For the dishes, you can select specifications, flavors, toppings, and cooking methods.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fa9VFcKYOaLprGIt7n2Cx%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=efc9233c&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FK2RAEHfZKEjLxMEqsj3G%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e507cad5&sv=2)

Select the dishes and dish specifications and add them to the cart. You can review the selected dishes in the cart. The dishes in the cart can be added or deleted.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F8cQyY9dsLzM7Mm3Ly0PE%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8cd0bf5e&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FxyAH3aBYR9esq0PL6v1T%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59ab2d3c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#step-3-confirm-order)

Step 3: Confirm Order

Click the Order button to jump to the order confirmation page. If customer has special needs then fill in the remark, choose whether to package, and check the total amount of the order. After confirmation, click confirm order. The order is successfully placed and terminal will print the receipt. The table is occupied at this time.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjjEe6mq3OrPS9lhgvDFd%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f04931f6&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FpWPE8qrFvllMYYa1wNtx%252F8.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=54c60242&sv=2)

7b55a2d39c107240cf8f7b624eb8b63

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#step-4-payment)

Step 4: Payment

Click on the dining table to jump to the order details. On this page, waiters can add dishes Order More or modify order Modify.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F5wadTIIyLPI9qiZaVMKH%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98cf67d8&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FLOl5TkrzbrKqi1DhHeIU%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=770fa5e5&sv=2)

Click Checkout to jump to the payment page. The cashier displays the payment amount, taxes, discount information and the total order amount. Customer can choose to split the payment (multiple payments), and the customer can also select the tip ratio or directly enters the tip amount.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FXdKwvnzbYZd4rzQHoITL%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=63df3816&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FJaNbfy8aVOZhRe6MuiI5%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fd68fe11&sv=2)

circle-info

**Note: Click Split to split orders, up to 10p. Click Tip Ratio to choose the rate. The default is 10%, 15%, and 20%. It can also be customized in the system settings.**

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FFaz1zgJ2g5wJUUeAZrCx%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2fa570fb&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FNritzPBqMlW3Ad9cfF3x%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6e126458&sv=2)

Payment methods include cash, bank card, membership payment or other payment. Among them, member payments need to identify membership QR code first. Click on the upper right member icon to identify members.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FxCO61TAusISxl2zGlO42%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=93687b7c&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FoUFlMzapw2JlCs6SGaC0%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6825d47c&sv=2)

circle-info

**Note: After identifying the member, if the customer has coupons then click on the coupon to select the member's coupon for discount.**

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjjTpD3nyb2ipPByOGTTm%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7fb9b085&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FzDWYXxxD6P4BLCg7Au4w%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=abe19707&sv=2)

You can also use other payment methods customized by the merchant to record other types of transactions.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FWW1lfwKHmV7LN7khqyW7%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8579f96b&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F6KR8aoYzvBZO7wvFOrdZ%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69a3bc7e&sv=2)

After the payment is successful, the terminal prints the receipt. Click View Orders to view the orders, and click Back To Home to return to the HOME.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjSdpQ3ekWY1ruBflEteK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c952152-c5a8-4091-a405-1ed394d31e52&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a0cfdcd8&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F2Vg48VPYxyOKJkmPqTu0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0c62a5a-7e4d-48fc-82fb-dde26257bf64&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebfb7b08&sv=2)

5\. Takeout


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Takeout on the homepage to enter the takeout ordering process. Takeout scenario is the same as dine-in. The difference is that when placing an order, the Takeout switch will be turned on by default, and the packaging fee will be calculated for the order automatically.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FwLhdxTVajamURbORJFN3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39041373-5e02-4851-88a4-d2478f0e7769&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9358dcc6&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F53aQnQWlQRDJK6SFxRby%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D778ba741-c698-48f4-9788-a8c2a83fbe7a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c38a0ff&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fz7Kx3RfwMlFzpvYqdOK3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b54d1c2-bf5d-480d-9186-42a9155bfe7d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5b7ce8cc&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc12691)

6\. Bills


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on the Bill to enter the order list. All dine-in and mobile orders are displayed here.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F9FAS96U4PQfw3psFFLgy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddc766936-82a8-45cd-b8f0-2504bb0fc2dc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=62d5cf5c&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F4cDWJUmQafXDwqgt6GKy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db483c28f-fc48-4369-8921-45b735623e5e&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d10e3e88&sv=2)

Click on the order to view the order details, including amount, payment time, payment method, discount information, etc.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FEhZnwjh9hzZV98lRO9Bk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2525be77-083a-40be-be85-da4745de7e75&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43f66cfc&sv=2)

7\. Business Report


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Report on the home page to enter the report page. The sales report displays all income, discounts, refunds, etc. based on date. Click Print icon in the upper right corner to print out the report receipt.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fa03rVceNK43leYG7puwC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3fa2aea5-110b-41c3-8eec-7de7a090aac0&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f353db9e&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrSgyfYzuz1NUv2yEc3vx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daae98ec6-d9f1-48e8-a173-1c3816aa604c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f2007d56&sv=2)

8\. Sales Orders


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Sales Order to display the sales order list, which can include all mobile and dine-in orders.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FtcHjvw8xqBBQl0im99np%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8bda004-5c18-4f68-8618-9f3374b8df63&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d9328e10&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FebbEC4SY3Dc5bSl3Y0Nq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e00e67c-9f4c-40fc-b53b-6647bbd2b89a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c82ddf35&sv=2)

Click on the order details to print and refund the order. When refund, you need to enter the manager password. The manager password is set in the merchant's portal.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FOzm0qgwRroPq8uLuPXLV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e19f40e-7c94-4ff0-8dc7-ceac0e85ca47&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b195ce31&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQSBolB8BMhNohzxbq293%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65a08cf7-17bf-4083-bc55-5a00055e95a1&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3be93c0&sv=2)

Entering the password to perform the refund operation, a refund receipt will be printed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQ0HmuJdpsTfdX26Q1VTN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc194a5e0-f3a7-428a-904c-6e1bfe6cd2ad&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a3a5f266&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FpY1BXlA9qcNqCiedlk38%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90dd2050-9ce5-41c5-adcb-a23f590e5757&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20a5d0d5&sv=2)

9\. Summary of the day


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Today Sum to enter the day's summary, view the dishes sold on the day, and print the day's summary of the dishes.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F8ZRF1muBtscfbwcCguez%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5ebbb15-0e05-4ee8-acf6-66061f25e66a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0cb09a2&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FnzT4MKjlg1ty5Ak4X7Qz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4bb90060-9baf-4169-9724-cd71edb7d22c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1128702a&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc28164)

10\. Print


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Print on the home page to enter the network printing list. The page displays the receipts printed successfully and failed by the network printer (for kitchen use). If the receipt fails to print, it will be displayed in the Not Printed column, and the merchant clicks Reprint to reprint. Click the icon in the upper right corner to view the configuration of the current merchant's network printers. If you want to configure a network printer, you can configure it in the merchant's portal. The terminal can only enable and disable network printers.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FtGmeNLkhClaiilcwMISB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9268d19d-c3bb-4695-91ad-d9e7b3f45501&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=524d521b&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fx2DGH5jyNWOFDX2v5d3X%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75435b6b-5fed-4499-9ba4-aee59285ca5f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bbb6c241&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc17955)

11\. Tip Report


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Tips to enter tip report. You can check the tip amount and number of orders based on employees and time.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FPTPWIyWahDUcgGsqiSFf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7551ef0-95c3-4945-be3a-cedf4c06adfd&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d55627ba&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FiJUTMFE1f4ua76BoEhkW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd7111f50-e5eb-4ca4-a77e-c888986d2965&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f04292e9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc22811)

12\. Membership


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Member to enter the member management. You can enter the member ID or scan the member QR ID. After identifying the member, his balance, points and coupons will be showed. You can recharge for the customer, and you can also view recharge details and transaction details.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FOKcFit6rBxthAlb2tpXA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D950776b0-10e7-4454-8b10-fddc7c9d45be&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c384293e&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FSQkYv5NqB47QdtgnROBv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5cc1a2c-26c6-402b-a86a-627461c03711&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=105cafed&sv=2)

Click on Member Details - > Rechange enters the recharge page. The payment method supports cash and bank card. After the payment is successful, the balance will be credited immediately. Member accounts can also view points and coupons.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fc4Nj2AGBt9PIwx4ttnNd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3738e27e-b87f-461f-b5a6-febaf15e0d23&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ee84ff0d&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FKjgskBLrMUk02K0fEQAt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3315e4b6-88fb-4c15-9e49-c7eb996f5d06&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3476889d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc1061)

13\. Points


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on Member Details - > Point, enter the points redemption function, and the items currently redeemed and to be redeemed will be displayed. The waiter can use the scan function in the upper right corner to scan the customer's points redemption QR code to redeem items.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FVLAAOZu5MWxIEiT0zeyg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93f9668e-14d9-4269-b720-ff1c0433c749&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5165caf&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FvYzv4uFftVKyySdJrsNh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70f093b8-8050-467b-8b1a-5b4c2d839158&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ad4bb49&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc30049)

14\. Takeout Management


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Takeout Man on the homepage to enter the takeout list. The takeout page displays two lists: Taken and Untaken.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FsPjOEtLtOXBQnk1NAPGM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f86d336-34dc-40c5-82dc-0eb4522930d8&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea3d0dd4&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fld6KGfrH0qKxUrv6NIZn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df96dccda-2b00-4311-b52e-844794740b6c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2aa05c60&sv=2)

Click Untaken on the unpicked meal list, click on the order, and click on Confirm Pickup to pick up the meal. After clicking, the status of the order changes to (Finished).

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F1LvkZZ52GQ2JbyIO0Et5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De25a2f5e-1ded-40f2-941a-555152824c9b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90d96230&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F1tBpy377qb6CWSfhnxLk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa495f15-c5c8-426c-9ed2-a8ac78871642&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d9fc6d7a&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc12302)

15\. Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the settings icon in the upper right corner of the homepage to enter the system settings page, which will display relevant information such as the current merchant number and merchant name. You can turn on or off the message notification function as needed, and choose whether to automatically receive orders. By default, these two functions are turned off. When turned off, you need to manually receive orders and print operations. When turned on, the terminal will automatically print new orders. Merchants can also set different tip ratios according to needs.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FPofYWbaOKbmmEiyN40mG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7800e3a8-533c-442c-84bb-68d9b335977e&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95979c5d&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FFqYjcXwyHSxYKsegwUzJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bd4d832-fb82-4954-80c0-98050deebe87&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec4e9325&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc25752)

16\. Notifications


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There is a notification area at the bottom of the homepage, which can receive order notifications from customers who order online. The green icon represents a dine-in order. If a customer places an order but does not pay yet, they will receive a corresponding order notification and the waiter can click to place the order and print it. The yellow icon represents a takeout order. After the customer places the order and completes the payment, the order notification will be received in the message notification bar, and the waiter can click to take the order and print it. If the kitchen network printer has been configured , the kitchen receipt will be automatically printed .

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdGqVAbKrfjk9mg0gLZ2f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0de330cc-5694-4f0c-a69d-5ba70dddec26&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17cc1dc1&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FZAisjyQlPuiEYISKf4Ri%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b271803-265a-4c20-914d-0d0fb907daf8&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fdc2c8f6&sv=2)

Click Notification - More to view more messages. Click to enter the order details page, where you can accept or reject the order. After placing the order, receipt will be printed. If the order is rejected, a refund will be processed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FAcF5ADnEe5aFenJka19r%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daaaa6d99-4348-46ab-9ee0-a283b1b40328&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4a7fb3b&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FCD5VaBMCWJsuEMu3JB36%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D131ad85f-a7c8-4454-a729-6658b75eea0b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=202ee3d0&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-terminal-app-user-guide#toc10812)

17\. Reservation


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Reservation on the home page to enter the queuing page. On the page, you can check the queuing status of the table, such as the number of people at the table, waiting time, etc. The waiter can click on the three icons in the list to perform voice announcements, customer dining and queuing invalidation. Click the icon in the upper right corner to view expired historical queue information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FsdRMy7ZzgaMkKqOZaHkP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D10726662-deec-4199-96c7-256a151a14b6&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3da40834&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F9uiUSBQ1VUZLJQ6h1kwy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e08ba04-fd5c-4b79-b038-e84afc66e395&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c686496e&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FHN5echBCsFYBYbz36uCG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d30f9e0-012c-4af2-a1ad-9eade7a90891&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5b65937&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F7zeCbdEBQwLK0jRLEgTm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3fa8b97a-34e7-4b78-91df-a12e691a7eca&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d1a0912&sv=2)

Click the Reservation - Reserve button, select the table, and the terminal will print a receipt to the customer. Customers can use their mobile phone browser to scan the QR code on the receipt to check the queue information in real time to prevent overdue.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FwkFwpqkNdnVwL31zRzGz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b3eee16-7246-4ad9-a01c-8ba51640dd8f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c821621f&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0R8qrknGogOcFALowwMB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d3f0a0d-2d3d-43f7-814b-420ff41f68a3&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1036a68b&sv=2)

After scanning the QR code, customer can check the current dining queue status on your mobile browser.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FuShvh3Y2FwLjoY6zWoFY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57a156d2-af74-4181-be84-a23164bf1bf8&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6913c72f&sv=2)

# Retail Online Store User Guide | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-online-store-user-guide#toc18639)

1\. Function Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WizarPOS retail online store is a mall system based on HTML5. Customer use mobile phone scan function to scan the online store QR code of the retail merchant to enter the mall for shopping or direct click the store URL. The system provides the following functions:

**1\. Goods**

Merchants upload various types of products in the merchant portal and display all products in the product list. They can also select several of the products as hot-selling products and display them in the recommendation bar on the homepage.

**2\. Promotions**

Merchants can set up various types of marketing activities through the merchant portal, including discounts, full discounts , special offers , points malls, coupons for consumption and other activities, which can better provide users with better shopping experiences.

**3\. Membership**

Each retail merchant can recommend the merchant's online store to the customer through links or QR code. Customers scan the QR code to register and become a member of the merchant. The staff can use the terminal to recharge the balance. The member's balance can be used at checkout. Members can receive coupons for consumption, which can be deducted when making purchases.

**4\. Payment**

Retail online store membership card balance, bank cards, coupons and other payment methods.

**5\. Points Mall**

Merchants can configure points redemption activities in the merchant portal, such as 100 points redeeming a bottle of Coke, 200 points redeeming a pack of snacks, etc.

**6\. Chain stores**

If a merchant has multiple stores and supports the chain store function, you can switch to the store list on the mall page, view all stores under the merchant, and then enter one of the stores for shopping in the mall.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-online-store-user-guide#toc20911)

2\. Login


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Customer need to register as a member to log in for the first time.

Enter email address and password. After successful registration, you can log in with your registered email address and password.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FPY5PfwEzo6I4x2XjXz9Q%252F0.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a2077c7f&sv=2)

If you forget your password or want to reset it, you can click Forgot Password to reset your login password.

3\. Home


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After successfully logging in, the product recommendation images and lists displayed on the homepage can be set in the merchant portal. You can quickly find the products you want through search. Click on the product list below to see all products. You can also click on Me to view personal information status.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdcMKgNW6LSaPqMzmgAxV%252F4.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3367541&sv=2)

f20b2347cd7a37425755277a2098bca

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FEAW0Pi5Md4jfLQpt87uF%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=52226fea&sv=2)

1675332857509

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-online-store-user-guide#toc19015)

4\. Product Categories


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Menu to see all the product lists. You can also quickly find products through search, and you can also click on the sort order to arrange the products. For example, click on the price, and the products will be presented from low to high, or from high to low. The category supports up to level 2. Click on the product to view the product details. The taste, price and other parameters of the product can be set in the background.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FSMOSBTj1LMAbvFdKoibU%252F6.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ffab28fc&sv=2)

5\. Shopping Cart


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After you select the product, add the product to the shopping cart. You can choose delivery or self-pickup. To choose delivery, you need to enter your address, mobile phone number and other personal information before submitting the order.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fuqb16LlOPjohTnPyeBQ8%252F8.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=10bc1d03&sv=2)

On the payment page, you can choose various payment methods such as membership card, bank card, etc. After a successful payment, wait for delivery or pick up at the store according to the method you selected previously.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-online-store-user-guide#id-6.-me)

6\. Me


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the avatar, you can fill in or edit your member information, such as mobile phone number, name, birthday, gender and other information. Click Confirm to submit, and the modifications are completed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FGXEgNo85uviZKrKJKd7d%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bd7c66a0&sv=2)

Click on the QR code icon. Your membership QR code will be displayed. With this membership QR code, you can show it to the terminal to recharge, identify membership, and other operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FXDeGqK55knj76XMHXvfR%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31c84ebd&sv=2)

Click Me to enter my page, where you can see the user's own membership information, balance, points, membership coupons, membership codes, orders and other information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjV1zNuUQ97BUldJHM5vm%252F20.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ae45c8bf&sv=2)

c4ba99daf639906596b582146927140

Click Balance to view your member's balance. Click Recharge Record to view the member's recharge record. You can select a time to view the recharge record for a specific date.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fo7XPQDbXh2vqs6uV0y8Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5daacad4-bce0-43a6-8eb1-cdccbed9c49f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ee6e128&sv=2)

Members can receive coupons after their purchase meets the amount set for the promotions. Next time when your purchase amount reaches a certain amount, you can use the coupon, the used coupon and Expired coupons will become invalid

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F8u6r3brm0iGCp32qtZo4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D045d83be-bb2b-4626-80a6-dc177b23934b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c63183bb&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FgbzF0bqBhbtF8YsJqeGN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D980b2101-1f2b-4a4a-b228-5267d3b1806b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94a5c3ac&sv=2)

Click ALL in My Order to enter my order list and view orders with pending payment, pending shipment, picked up, and completed status.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FumhdKFJApc8fe1hCwqbt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46e26c88-14ca-41da-8946-0083c5de3663&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61dc3cb7&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FfoYe8xAlnvkIwTmjXh2W%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ffd3b40-27f5-4737-8924-da25fb9f1b5f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1cd7943c&sv=2)

For unpaid orders, you can choose to cancel or pay. For orders that have been shipped, the customer can confirm receipt after receiving the goods and they will be converted into completed orders.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fxtj8Zs4B6UwFZYVisufc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df51650e5-4ed1-461b-9038-36e03f1764d7&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1ba97fc1&sv=2)

For completed orders, if you want to purchase again, you can click to view the details and place an order again.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FzammhfTAUPccTkTkwemL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D495cec37-c56d-464a-86d5-cae83eecbd0b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=132531d1&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F6xEHUmQ3zH50qxdztZJL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4174b58-df5a-4d9d-9e3c-df565c52ea31&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59d990cc&sv=2)

If you want to know the merchant's information, you can click Store profile to view the merchant's profile, and click Store address to view the merchant's address.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdrG8kvt4Msb4N23M4fJy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D368213de-9ab7-4312-b028-d97c52f5bcd5&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca118fe4&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F63dobqc0VBVpsYhLDsmd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f81d047-971a-4b7b-a3f2-c1357cf75589&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b9682a2&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-online-store-user-guide#toc17650)

7\. Points Redeem


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On Me page, click Points to enter the redemption page of the points mall. The products and points redemption displayed here are set by the merchant portal. You can click Redeem to use existing points to redeem the product. Click Exchange Records, you can see the redeemed products, click to apply, a QR code will appear, and then use the terminal to scan and redeem.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQXQswOPhjj0k5KaTBCEh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2261f4e3-4a21-4f01-a320-4e32c14c7d33&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=acda0a66&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FE56Oehe3rJg46luVuGaw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D055fce85-b767-4625-a3e5-ab486073434e&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b54b75a8&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FDAgnc9VMuPdmYRQGPrjm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De51bdbde-d833-4809-85dd-bbc55da262ea&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=56b65ca&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FfdsI4oRMIdPk8WWTx018%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D058f8f4c-900f-4af1-a6a0-aa8cc10ac85c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=53bf6566&sv=2)

8\. Store List


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If a merchant has multiple stores, you can enter the list of all stores under the merchant on the homepage of the mall and switch stores for shopping.
