# Retail Terminal APP User Guide | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc18639)

1\. Function Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WizarPOS terminal retail app is a retail cashier system for Android terminal. It is used in retail stores. The main functions provided by the system are as follows:

**Goods**

Merchants upload various types of goods in the merchant portal and save all products in the product list. When customers shopping, the waiter scans the barcode of the goods to checkout.

**Promotions**

Merchants can set up various types of marketing activities through the merchant portal, including discounts, full discounts, special offers, points malls, coupons for consumption and other activities, which can provide a better shopping experience.

**Membership**

Each retail merchant can recommend the merchant's online store to the customer through links or QR code. Customers scan the QR code to register and become a member of the merchant. The staff can use the terminal to recharge the balance. The member's balance can be used at checkout. Members can receive coupons for consumption, which can be deducted when making purchases.

**Payment**

Retail APP support cash, bank cards, membership cards, membership coupons and other payment methods.

**Points**

Merchants can configure points redemption activities in the merchant portal, such as 100 points redeeming a bottle of Coke, 200 points redeeming a pack of snacks, etc. The waiter uses terminal to scan the customer's redemption code and redeem the product for the customer.

**Chain stores**

If a merchant has multiple stores, it supports the chain store function. Customers can register as a member at any store under the merchant. The membership balance can be used across all stores. The membership coupons obtained through consumption can also be used at any store.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc22756)

2\. Login


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please check the email of the merchant’s account. For accounts with operator roles, enter the merchant ID, username, and password to log in to the app. Check auto login will let you automatically log in next time.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FaJF9d6xAhGsif7vZjbS3%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=79f32a3&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc5448)

3\. Home


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The search bar allows you to search for products.

Scan function support 3 types of code:

1.Product barcode

2.Membership QR code

3.Pickup code

Stuff can place pending orders (unchecked orders are temporarily suspended), membership identify.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FejVjHhyqiM2QWntMAjGT%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39300553&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F3w1xVAZhpBTFrjLITm8W%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61b3a107&sv=2)

Click the Scan icon to scan the barcode of the product package with terminal and add it to the product list.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc20898)

4\. Pending Order


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The cashier can temporarily held the orders, for customers who want to postpone the checkout, so that the next customers can checkout first, and then select unchecked orders from the pending order list to perform checkout operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrwlkNtAn1QnGhbq5rmc6%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=84d94c67&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjpWMREA8FNUIzdxjELkU%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9750ce89&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc10489)

5\. Checkout


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Check out on the home page to enter the checkout page. You can use cash or bank cards to pay.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FfDxKuV9WjgfeN9HyZI48%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46a26ba&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FTAYpOdqCijSqvxcMIeMd%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2fc7415&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#identify-membership)

Identify Membership

The customer can present the membership QR code before checkout. The cashier clicks Membership to identify the membership, and the current member's info and balance will be displayed. At this time, the membership card icon and coupon icon will be available at checkout page. Checkout supports multiple payments with any payment method.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F9OydYp3XtCVsDCnaac1r%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ffe0ee42&sv=2)

6\. Search


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can search for products at the top of the homepage. By manually entering part of the product name or barcode number.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdTq34BD1zk3cSNukNCRb%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f7c3daff&sv=2)

7\. Online Order


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Online order on the left menu to enter the mall order page. You can view the orders to be shipped, shipped, pending payment, completed, and canceled. The orders are divided into delivery and self-pickup. You can enter the order details. Click Delivery. For self-pickup orders, customers can show the delivery code, then scan the code to quickly locate the order and perform delivery operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FLYCYlTwHXz05Mflm880B%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3735f9e5&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FGYVthIMQzWobkKZMFJew%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8af459fb&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FKHSjUKrm37aQvktZY1lt%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=de2d2fde&sv=2)

For shipped orders, you can view details and reprint the order receipt.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F2OlqepumMPKSgs1fHGQ1%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b27e248&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc6897)

8\. Member


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Gift card on the left menu to enter the member identification page. You can identify members by scanning the QR code and entering the membership card number manually..

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FYDFTk6lcNAFqusbOdLOU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d65d32f-88e0-4cb8-8883-4ab7530608bd&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8f703ce8&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FfpMXlWLYUICMUJ2RvkLV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5175d946-b722-4aa1-bb72-5709ce359c68&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8763b43b&sv=2)

After the identification is successful, you can check the members info such as membership number, balance, and other information. Customer can recharge their membership card with cash or bank card. Also, can check the member's transaction history and the member's coupons.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fc6gsC2jZy7NkvUi5oIlv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e801117-bdcc-4bec-a6fc-40c660429d20&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17a6f14d&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FBkWtanT9vXwQVYXSNvSH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d3b0288-8241-4907-b528-e32e13c7f7d1&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64f29d0c&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FXWu6zpOgRNqPWqTxUn6C%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0ba0b41-b1f6-4c13-a18d-84e92786f8dc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86fa29d0&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FXTTW8ekYfnp0JNL0nbNy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2f0098d-9c1b-4782-94cc-592b21736e4a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=793d3142&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#id-9.-points-mall)

9\. Points Mall


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Points on the left menu to enter the points redemption function. Items currently redeemed and to be redeemed will be displayed. The cashier can use the scan function to scan the customer's points redemption QR code to redeem items.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQlc8sqwU5sCv0AjJzyKZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8917b380-ee31-433f-896e-554af9b3c5b6&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=af212af2&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc7772)

10\. Sales Report


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Sale report to enter the sales report, which displays the sales summary of the day. Click Print to print the report receipt.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdxomLdUCPVyvhUrh9jcR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9178880-8e06-4e4c-8975-9602df15044a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2634a698&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F7NOwxT5pLxv22NOIKKtJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa919f84-5770-4943-9839-82b53f69280d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1497cb9a&sv=2)

11\. Product Categories


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Goods & Categories to enter the category list. Click a category to enter the product list under that category. You can view product prices and de tails, add products, and edit and delete products.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FAAvknhlnECy7tQVOopHe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7899e31-8f0c-44fe-aa98-1aee1fff05ab&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=405df801&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FlNEQE125YpOgpAif8wRU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D947df6bc-b36f-4e71-afaf-af86af306dca&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7507c33d&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FwjNjO54VPnwM7iIDhW6c%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db371a522-d9e0-4941-a024-7ce469c08f25&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72569e33&sv=2)

Click + to add new products.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FalEcbw0F6MKceGIFE5aM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D062fa678-5b64-4e60-8505-e27a6c4193ab&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e38f1419&sv=2)

12\. Sales Order


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Sales Order to view all sales orders. Click on an order to view details. For sales orders, you can refund the order. After entering the manager password, you can perform refund operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQLL1jCV2wbsaDos8MFy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded53d234-8cc4-4467-98e8-98c5f5b6912d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5df9471&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrA2imSKwplu5KXBkVuqW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6692a5a-2a91-4331-98cb-001ac6de7dbf&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2551806&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FiduWdJXJLPg9qJqzYBgk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9194330b-1bf3-4abe-a4c2-897dcaef6256&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b74dff8&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc21954)

13\. Inventory Manage


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Inventory Manage to enter warehouse management.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fiu17U8oGB2780QeVribl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D842eaab5-181b-466a-bc4b-f1ac72e5c6dd&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31baf6c1&sv=2)

Click Stockin to enter the stock in process. You can scan the QR code and manually select the product. After confirming, the process is completed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdoiIwnNSSedNAkIHSkej%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D179cdbbd-71fc-432a-9761-de2068772943&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64980f3f&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FCRKA0aNMZBzzTzQ23cuD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D172f2790-0a77-4c4a-aa05-cf952ab8702a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4368f970&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fw8HisZQBVaaIlT7Vq30l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D959d9141-06f9-4d7f-bfda-7df67571f81d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=41f3eb2&sv=2)

Click Stockout to enter the stock in process. You can scan the QR code and manually select the product. After confirming, the process is completed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FYNI0JSipSAjkU0VUT6zi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9526459c-c15d-4384-8541-38947e0cbdee&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14da6d81&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FpvfK00HhhIc1Yijo1Cfl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe5279a4-6af7-4ea9-9287-d3804567b323&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73b09305&sv=2)

Click Inventory to enter the inventory count page. You can scan the QR code and manually select the product, then enter the inventory quantity of the product, and complete the count process.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FyYuGNgvAQf2JHNTbICEN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D721144df-092c-470d-99e7-6b626db96498&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e1e16eb&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fwkgh5mXDOM5IuELdAFkw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D778bb396-cd5d-4acb-a417-21d7a91ba177&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3ba22875&sv=2)

Click Stock query to enter the inventory query.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FcQg7gUfzVdHU4x9qEo14%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29879079-36d2-4221-ba86-2110ac0387fc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=458dce3c&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FI3H0S1RwsWPbzn7H2Zc5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D36890d68-b204-483c-b50c-f5fd741b2abc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48c48b0e&sv=2)

Click Stockin query to enter the stockin query. The list displays all stockin orders. Select a stockin order to enter and query the stockin details.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FimKPFcaCraLloLOk8h7O%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34e7e2e3-538e-4077-96bf-06f0e0ade02b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d9962ba&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FGpkPPafesAGRyZMej61J%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f5822ae-ad64-4960-b6a7-e50d2a03196c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=efab1c7d&sv=2)

Click Stockout query to enter the stockout query. The list displays all stockout orders. Select a certain stockout order to enter and query the stockout details.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FJKYPIGYpNAmGhOu610TV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ee7a797-2bb7-49b0-8959-dac618c62c31&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=af5a8d5d&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FFJ0FitQRwxlTwcdyOwku%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bfc6d5d-9f3c-4069-918f-6188a4e45428&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2c8b643&sv=2)

Click Inventory query to enter the inventory query and display all inventory orders. Click to view the details of a certain inventory order. You can also filter the inventory orders within a certain time period based on time to view.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FMRnJhjXbHo8qieUFyg5y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ea5938d-00e3-4b9c-8808-5624e4f18cd9&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0f89d5b&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F6LbYuAakOP8IwZOCwiHz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd79156c3-f5a1-469c-afb2-b5b1c848156a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b6ca891&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F8icNzIVL7EguNWUmghx1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b5e2068-b462-44c1-b6b8-fee0406b0f01&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f49d876b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc1778)

14\. Parameter settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the parameter setting page, you can view the quantity of the current order receipt. You can turn on/off message notifications. After turning it on, the order placed by the customer in the mall will be notified to the handheld retail store. You can clear the cache and data below.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0SC4ONn3COZmj2IH6QZC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D598bc107-1887-4e54-a85b-4c3e2d3c0e0f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2da0ba4&sv=2)

# Catering Smart ECR User Guide | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

WizarPOS Catering Solution

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508823)

1\. Function Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WizarPOS Smart ECR Catering is a professional ordering system based on Android devices, providing efficient services and convenient ordering experience to catering merchants. The system has the following functions:

**1\. Menu**

The merchant uploads various types of dishes, hot dishes, cold dishes, Western food, dim sum, snacks, etc. And displays all the dishes in the menu. When ordering, the dishes can be customized according to the specifications, tastes, methods, and toppings.

**2\. Promotions**

Merchants can set up various types of marketing activities through the merchant portal, including discounts, full discounts, special offers, points malls, coupons for consumption and other activities, which can provide great dining experiences.

**3\. Membership**

Each catering merchant can use the table QR code or takeout QR code to allow customers to scan the QR to register and become a member of the merchant. The waiter can use terminal to recharge for the members, and the member balance can be used when order and pay. Members can get coupons through consumption.

**4\. Payment**

Handheld ordering can support cash, bank cards, membership payment, membership coupons and other payment methods.

**5\. Points**

Merchants can configure goods for exchange in the merchant portal, such as 100 points to exchange for a bottle of Coke, 500 points to exchange for a dish. The waiter uses a terminal to scan the customer's redemption code and redeem the goods for the customer.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508824)

2\. Login


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to log in to the terminal, you need to enter the merchant ID, username and password.

The merchant ID is when the service provider onboarding the merchant. An assigned merchant ID can be obtained from the email after the merchant is successfully onboarded. At the same time, the merchant administrator account and initial password will be given. The merchant administrator must log in to the merchant backend for the first time, change the initial password, and create an operator account in System Settings -> Account Management. The created operator account can be used to log in to the terminal catering application.

**Note:** **The administrator account of the merchant received by email cannot be used to log in to the terminal application.**

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FfTx0rK0jd1SV4HHICf3l%252F0.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b4da7a91&sv=2)

Enter the MID, username, and password, and click Login to enter the homepage.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FTY5zLG7yuxLpHg1PmAog%252F1.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69df1a30&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508825)

3\. Home


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The home page is divided into three areas, function area on the left, display area in the middle, and the checkout area below.

The function area has the following functions:

Dine-in, reservations, reports, membership, points, takeout, notifications, menu management and settings.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FX1KpWMpYAg3aVWCxFla6%252F2.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=afedd7c1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508826)

4\. Dine-in


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The merchant clicks on the dine-in to choose the table, and the table displays the table name, maximum customer and status. The table status is divided into free and dining. The table is set in the merchant portal. Click the table to enter the menu.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FOmTBcEQ0dAIvQtkTfVvX%252F3.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=655f41db&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdjyIrhPHU4ARJSvMqHfj%252F4.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=286dd5ec&sv=2)

In the menu, you can select dishes according to the category of the dishes, and you can choose the specifications, tastes, toppings, and methods of the dishes.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Flz2R29CQBOGcX10MkgWK%252F5.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e668761a&sv=2)

Select dishes and dish specifications to add to the ordering list on the right. You can view the selected dishes in the ordering list, and support modify dishes. Click Remarks below to fill in the remark information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FLgAm26m4hshMDPykePk5%252F6.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=65c5d7cc&sv=2)

Click Order to place an order. The table status changes to dining, the printer print receipts and kitchen receipts, and the kitchen prepares dishes according to the order.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F5B826E47zOp9QtUJv0zZ%252F7.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db3e2381&sv=2)

Select the table and click the dining button on the lower right to jump to the ordering list. On this page, waiter can modify dishes .

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F3mtXMRQBoTUucJRSkFcW%252F8.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d9d4cc9&sv=2)

Select the dining table and click the bill button to jump to the payment. The cashier displays the payment amount, taxes, discount information on the total order amount, etc. You can choose the payment method, such as split payment (multiple payments), and the customer selects the tip ratio or directly enters the tip amount.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fw8USFIPnfLM4RchTqLXo%252F9.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc4e09d0&sv=2)

Click on the number of people to split the order, up to 10 orders; click on the tipping ratio, the default is 10%, 15%, 20%, which can also be customized in the system settings.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FckU5SG5Izf5Fv4kYz8l0%252F10.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c895f85d&sv=2)

Payment methods include cash payment, bank card payment, membership payment or other payment. Among them, bank cards need to be connected to payment channels, and membership payments need to identify membership QR code. Click on the lower right corner for member identification.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FoG6B0yhUoo9jTm6d5Akx%252F11.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e07b8a60&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FPWvRlZ0Xu0jNCacLeLJK%252F12.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b43e34a7&sv=2)

After identifying the member, you can choose a membership card or coupon to pay. You can also use other payment methods customized by the merchant to record other types of transactions.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQBCo8YFFWVu1dO6toAyr%252F13.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96b7a44&sv=2)

After a success payment, you will be redirected to the home page, the table will be changed to idle, and the label machine will print the receipt.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrxVY12xegAZRyMsUrNSG%252F14.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e94f2a05&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508827)

5\. Reservations


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Book to enter the table reservation list. The page can manage customers' reservation table information. Make reservations for customers based on table. Reservation information includes date, reservation time, number of diners, etc.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrWQQBfZa9zcX2FY3hKly%252F15.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88990721&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508828)

6\. Reports


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the report menu, and the page displays business reports, sales orders, today's summary and tip reports. These reports are summary queries that can query order information based on time period and type.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508829)

6.1 Sales Reports

The business report displays the revenue, discounts, refunds and other information of the day's business, and supports printing of business report documents.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FS9qLWUejIWnrKjzbubix%252F16.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c3f7fe5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508830)

6.2 Sales Order

Sales reports can query order details based on time range and type.

Sales Orders display all online and dine-in orders.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FEBEnYXVV0deh8CLW9imQ%252F17.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e3938081&sv=2)

Select an order and click to view details. In the pop-up window, you can view all the details of the order, and you can print or return the order. Refund requires entering the manager password, which is set in the merchant's portal.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FmOYrK0IeDZjO4PpQ94eR%252F18.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ee37ede8&sv=2)

After entering the password to perform the refund operation, a refund receipt will be printed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0KbteBPU1u6YMEIIltvU%252F19.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a5c7d96&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508831)

6.3 Today’s Summary

You can view all the dishes sold today on today's summary page.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FEJOJAy502qBlv7DI0oZE%252F20.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40ee55d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508832)

6.4 Tip Report

Click Tips Report to enter tip statistics. You can check the tip amount and number of orders based on employees and time.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0RqTmlhvjzupGT7aUnly%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1465079e-1ac6-4eaa-b771-2be6a7433992&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=23810904&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508833)

7\. Membership


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the member menu to enter the member inquiry page. You can enter the member ID or scan the QR code. After identifying the member, its balance, number of points, and number of coupons will be displayed. You can recharge for the members, and you can also view recharge details and transaction details.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F31wXy6NYqx3wM8JFPgnq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5740209-b8d7-4bc0-b921-107c94d8e1d1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=10959a34&sv=2)

Click Recharge to enter the recharge page. The payment method supports cash and bank card. Enter the recharge amount. After the payment is successful, the balance will be credited immediately. Member accounts can also view coupons.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F40cENA1T1k7ei5h3zrQa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e1c9af4-1f19-4776-bcac-e1d81e043ba6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c2a58a57&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FNC3YUJcbw25A0HMIjB9k%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3865f0ed-cfa3-4e43-a302-caa078c45368&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b7b3cdc&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FDtQOvg7t2rx2fi5Ihn1j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd86c694-a2f1-4abc-970a-a65fe53b7b4d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3829ac68&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508834)

8\. Points


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the points menu to enter the points redemption function. The page displays the redemption records, including items used and to be used. The waiter can use the scanner to scan the customer's points redemption QR code to redeem items.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fdu4akabzKHIfY4wNg4U8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8b677fa-3c80-4993-a733-f24099560ac2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13e9eca9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508835)

9\. Delivery


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on Delivery to enter the takeout list. The page displays two lists of picked up and unpicked meals. Select the unpicked meal list, click on the order and click on the lower right corner to pick up the meal, then the status of the order will change to Completed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F4MCvqKU09VM153RXH4JC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbba05c0c-ce92-4419-8aaa-b863d690e2b7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61f06c6a&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508836)

10\. Queue


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter the queuing page. On the page, you can check the queuing status of the table, such as the number of people at the table, waiting time, etc. The waiter can click the three icons in the list to perform voice announcements, customer dining and queuing invalidation. Click on the number transfer information at the bottom right to view the historical queue details that have expired.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F1BflCb6XkfewxZLEtLIT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D107ee1be-2cd1-45d3-a36a-6e9d77ae412c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=847efca3&sv=2)

Click the pick up number button, select the type of the table, and the terminal will print a receipt to the customer. Customers can use their mobile phone browser to scan the QR code on the ticket to check the queue information in real time to prevent passing the number.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F2gcKLGUJyDkjMcxUeigQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1fbabe79-8239-4be1-a5c3-58e18eaf6d9c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f01dd9f&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FeglOuOixjCZSXl6jLAmP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d52cb49-c085-4a01-ac6d-5cfd935f0557&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b20e6f4e&sv=2)

After scanning the QR code, check the current dining queue status on your mobile browser.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fm1bPzOuXfFcYqlqMYiL6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D429e2fdc-7bf1-4025-a9f4-e47ee2dbe7cb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=560eee6f&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508837)

11\. Menu Management


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The menu management page supports the operations of adding, modifying, and deleting dishes. You can modify the sold out status of a dish.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FEdJaxfB75JMnIcgZRHwn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D643ad5a7-a2c2-4cb3-bdd9-83c485465e24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cebdd44d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508838)

12\. Category Management


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In category management, you can create categories for dishes to make it easier to manage dishes.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FHiGLV2KKdEUr9GF2oWgQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded9b0bda-6a72-45e6-9042-4e78b0d602f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bf36b094&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508839)

13\. Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the settings menu to enter the system settings page, which displays basic parameters, printing parameters, and other payment settings. The basic parameters display relevant information such as the current merchant number and merchant name. You can turn on or off the message notification function as needed, and choose whether to automatically receive orders. By default, these two functions are turned off. When turned off, you need to manually receive orders and print operations. When turned on, the terminal will automatically print new orders. Merchants can also set different tip ratios according to needs.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FCGVZqjPrDwcFlpVnIigs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f772d03-6be8-4022-8a57-07c9f0187043&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=19a97153&sv=2)

In the printing parameters, you can configure the parameters related to the back kitchen and front desk cashier printing.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FJhVFEqcLUFiPoEsGDs3t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac56efc3-5371-4b12-888d-0a6894288c30&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26895001&sv=2)

Other payments are to configure payment methods other than mainstream payment methods.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508840)

14\. Notification


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the notification menu, you can receive order notifications for customers' online orders on their mobile phones. The green icon represents a dine-in order. If a customer places an order but does not pay, they will receive a corresponding order notification and the waiter can click to take the order and print it. The yellow icon represents a takeout order. After the customer places the order and completes the payment, the order notification will be received in the message notification bar, and the waiter can click to take the order and print it. If the kitchen network printer has been configured , the kitchen receipt will be automatically printed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fuk2sgyxJSerpZYcuH5GX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b62251e-f53b-411f-a4d2-6af85ca46d72&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8494e039&sv=2)

# Permissions | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/permissions#permissions)

Permissions

In order to interact with various devices on the terminal, your application needs to declare the relevant permissions for each device. Below is the list of permissions along with their descriptions:

Permission

Description

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_PRINTER

Access the printer

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_MSR

Access the mega stripe reader (MSR)

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_CONTACTLESS\_CARD

Access the contactless card reader (RF card reader)

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_SMARTCARD

Access the smart card reader

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_SERIAL

Access the serial port (RS232)

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_LED

Access the LED device

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_CUSTOMER\_DISPLAY

Access the second display device

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_CLONESCREEN

Access the HDMI device

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_MONEYBOX

Access the cash drawer

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_FINGERPRINT

Access the fingerprint device

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_PIN\_GET\_PIN\_BLOCK

Retrieve the encrypted PIN block by PINPad

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_PIN\_MAC

Calculate the MAC by the MAC key in PINPad

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_PIN\_ENCRYPT\_DATA

Encrypt data by the data key in PINPad

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_PIN\_UPDATE\_USER\_KEY

Update the session (user) key of MasterKey/SessionKey schema

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_SIGNATURE

Access the signature board

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_SAFE\_MODULE

Access HSM

android.permission.SYSTEM\_ALERT\_WINDOW

Used when printing HTML

android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_EXT\_USB\_CTRL

Access the double USB control

Ensure that your application requests and is granted these permissions appropriately to enable seamless interaction with the CloudPOS SDK. For more detailed information, refer to the documentation sections related to each device API and consult the POS Spec, FAQs, or device-specific manuals.

Explore the CloudPOS SDK resources using the quick links provided, including Device API, Device Samples, EMV Development, BarCode Scan, Printer Manual, and TMS Manual.

Thank you for using wizarPOS, and if you have any questions, feel free to explore the available resources or contact our support team.

[PreviousJava API Sampleschevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/java-api-samples)
[NextError codechevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/error-code)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Scanning Service Usage | CloudPOS SDK

This documentation is crafted to aid Android application developers for the Smart POS. It clarifies the functionality of the scanning service and provides details on the released SDKs, testing applications, and features for quickly launching the scan application. For specific downloads and further information, refer to the provided links and sections.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/scanning-service-usage#overview)

Overview

The scanning service enables Android devices equipped with imaging hardware, such as cameras, to scan barcodes or QR codes, retrieving encoded data. This encoded information typically includes a web address, geographic coordinates, small text excerpts, and commercial product codes.

###

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/scanning-service-usage#quickly-launch-the-scan-application-in-q2-q3)

Quickly Launch the Scan Application in Q2/Q3

Physical Action: Double-click the power button or long press Volumn+.

This feature enables the swift launch of the scan application. Upon clicking, the system searches for all installed applications and launches the one with the scan intent-filter. If multiple applications exist, the system presents a list for users to choose from, initiating the selected application. The code for the scan intent-filter is as follows:

If no application in the system defines the scan intent-filter, pressing will not work. For instance, to use the scan button effectively, the application must define the scan intent-filter in its Android manifest file, with the category and action defined as follows:

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/scanning-service-usage#cloudpos-scan-service-in-q1-android-4.4)

CloudPOS Scan Service in Q1 Android 4.4

[CloudposScannerService-v3.12.28arrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/advanceSDK/CloudposScannerService-v3.12.28-r35144-q1_releasekey_forQ1android4.4.apk)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/scanning-service-usage#faq)

FAQ

*   How to not show the scan window?
    

Set window\_width=0 and window\_height=0 in ScanParameter.

Generally, physical scanner don't need show the scanner window.

Copy

    <action android:name="android.intent.action.SCAN" />
    <category android:name="android.intent.category.DEFAULT" />

Copy

    <activity
      android:name="com.XX.activity.MainActivity"
      android:label="@string/app_name" >
       <intent-filter>      
         <action android:name="android.intent.action.SCAN" />
         <category android:name="android.intent.category.DEFAULT" />
       </intent-filter>
    </activity>
