# Retail Smart ECR User Guide | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

V1.2

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc22979)

1\. Function overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WizarPOS Smart ECR retail app is a retail cashier system for Android big screen devices. It is used by cashiers in retail stores who use smart ECR machines to perform cashier operations on customers. The main functions provided by the system are as follows:

**1\. Goods**

Merchants upload various types of goods in the merchant portal and save all products in the product list. When customers shopping, the waiter scans the barcode of the goods to checkout.

**2\. Promotions**

Merchants can set up various types of marketing activities through the merchant portal, including discounts, full discounts, special offers, points malls, coupons for consumption and other activities, which can provide a better shopping experience.

**3\. Membership**

Each retail merchant can recommend the merchant's online store to the customer through links or QR code. Customers scan the QR code to register and become a member of the merchant. The staff can use the terminal to recharge the balance. The member's balance can be used at checkout. Members can receive coupons for consumption, which can be deducted when making purchases.

**4\. Payment**

Retail APP support cash, bank cards, membership cards, membership coupons and other payment methods.

**5\. Points**

Merchants can configure points redemption activities in the merchant portal, such as 100 points redeeming a bottle of Coke, 200 points redeeming a pack of snacks, etc. The waiter uses terminal to scan the customer's redemption code and redeem the product for the customer.

**6\. Chain stores**

If a merchant has multiple stores, it supports the chain store function. Customers can register as a member at any store under the merchant. The membership balance can be used across all stores. The membership coupons obtained through consumption can also be used at any store.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680710)

2\. Login


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter the merchant number, user name, and password and click Login to enter the homepage.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0XEwpeGP7Gn7OXcm8NfC%252F0.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=276aaf64&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fc3iP3CJKP9jTcUVNRzFF%252F1.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2861ac9d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680711)

3\. Home


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The home page is the home page of the cashier, with a function bar at the top and various functions displayed on the left side of the function bar, such as selecting members, clearing the entire order, pending orders, and online store orders. On the right side are the product search function and operation panel (function aggregation bar), which displays all retail functions.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FcyadWoImDHdCAmtIbqVb%252F2.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=886958f&sv=2)

On this page, the cashier can use a scanner to scan the barcode of the product package and add the product to the product list. He or she can also select the product classification menu on the left to select the product to add to the product list. Of course, it also supports product search and purchase.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FxipmDncd1UNAcfxoOYMf%252F3.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c77579e5&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680712)

4\. Pending Order


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The cashier can temporarily suspend the items that are already in the pending order list, which is convenient for some customers who want to postpone the checkout, so that next customers can checkout first, and then select unchecked orders from the pending order list to perform checkout operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F7hFQFr4bRQCnX36qgesQ%252F4.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=146c3e81&sv=2)

Click on the pending order to place the item on hold.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FlXX5lH2PJPjyAXHJNIi8%252F5.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7840e36f&sv=2)

Click the left and right arrows under Actions to add items to your shopping cart and check out.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F8sKwpEFPGNGEPCKNnK2u%252F6.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca10cb08&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680713)

5\. Checkout


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Checkout in the lower right corner to enter the checkout page. The payment amount, taxes, discounts and other payment information are displayed on the left side of the page. The right side is the payment method. Customers can choose different methods to pay, such as cash, bank card, membership card, etc.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fo6uRsZAKK90UCjMcQvbF%252F7.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c771c494&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrsSnVGwjF8Ge4jJnbeyP%252F8.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b85a56dd&sv=2)

On the home page, customers have several ways to identify themselves as members. First, customers can show their membership code QR code to the cashier, and the cashier can scan the QR code presented by the customer for identification. In addition, if necessary, the cashier can also manually enter the customer's membership code for binding. Once the binding is successful, the customer's membership information will be displayed in the upper left corner of the top.

At checkout, the system will display a membership card button, and customers can use their membership card balance to pay. In addition, the checkout function also supports the combination of different payment methods to pay multiple amounts, and coupons can also be used for deductions.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F4h5aolJ1y81bp5vj06P6%252F9.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e09321f&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F5Ev9SKDQ9PhvwrMnr0Te%252F10.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=537a1f94&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FwXd1OaNv1GEKOQ5brWx9%252F11.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=37828e1c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680714)

6\. Online Orders


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the online store order above the checkout counter to enter the online store order page. You can view orders to be shipped, shipped, pending payment, completed, and canceled. Orders are divided into door-to-door delivery and self-pickup. You can enter for order details. For self-pickup orders, customers can show the delivery code and then scan the code to quickly locate the order and proceed with delivery. For shipped orders, you can view details and print the order receipt repeatedly.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fpg1SLRubot5HLtegClGT%252F12.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67d6c5be&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680715)

7\. Membership


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Member Query on the operation panel, enter the membership id or scan the membership QR code for member identification.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FI9xBe9axddLCu5zZjgVR%252F13.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=792d9a52&sv=2)

After the member is identified, enter the member management page. On this page, you can view the member's detailed information and recharge for the customer. In addition, members’ recharge records and consumption records can also be viewed on the page at any time.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FTOyuQbxdzNEn7lVQ0JuG%252F14.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ce1ce241&sv=2)

Click Recharge, enter the recharge amount, and select the payment method to complete the recharge operation.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FgraRc3mBCYdDvSKvT1aK%252F15.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b4a7e8b5&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FmincZl2Bnx2aF4R9PWk1%252F16.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dddcd066&sv=2)

Open the recharge record to query the member's recharge record.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FtsHDMp4XcTLar41QjQjN%252F17.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6e9cdb68&sv=2)

Open the consumption record to query the member's consumption record.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F7pvGMYJaGyKAmSaADQf3%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17d188f6&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680716)

8\. Goods Management


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the Product and Category button in the operation panel to enter the product management page. Click the category to select its product, and the product information will be displayed on the right. Click the lower right corner to modify or delete the product. You can also add new products under this category.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F2VNP3LxstphWjPQ7hS15%252F19.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c52a0df&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FXY5mAcpx6hFKOViB6vvd%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5c034eaa&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680717)

9\. Sales Order


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on the sales order in the operation panel to view the sales orders of all transactions. Click on one of the orders to view the order details and support refund operations. If the customer pays in cash, the merchant will refund the cash. If the customer pays with a membership card, the payment amount will be Automatically returned to the customer's membership card.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FThgIdXSHeN95NHPkPZxX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a1fdaa9-2743-45dc-8a57-b822a6d97373&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28f21aca&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FaJsiNgfi32ba9sfJLX7j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbb50083-e96f-48f3-ac44-8ad12840e39f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cc966e8f&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680718)

10\. Stock-in and Stock-out


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Stock-in and Stock-out in the operation panel to enter the merchandise inbound and outbound page. The page has functions such as warehousing, warehousing, warehousing records, and warehousing records.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FbG5IzzAvU19fsxK0PgVt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D296f8b3a-cef2-4292-8f28-898c4dd893cd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81332c9e&sv=2)

Click on the category of the product and select the product. You can fill in the quantity of the product on the right side. Click on the lower right corner to enter the warehouse. If the warehouse is successfully entered, click on the outbound warehouse to complete the outbound operation. You can also view the incoming and outgoing records.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FESJn1ijTOoNFPbJ2DIsd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3474c8b-1bb8-43f2-93b2-c166ad26cf53&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d474a413&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FZcYYmUEulPM5WTqbWNds%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f7faf8c-a2ad-4be8-b085-e7d3701a9532&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b8381695&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FUA9XUtrduyGDbLwGkiOx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55851f43-c024-40b0-9e6a-2e5f8fe6c94d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e49a4abb&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680719)

11\. Inventory


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the inventory button in the operation panel to open the inventory page. Fill in the counted quantity according to the product, and display the profit and loss status.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FLGIRLKQEEGCSqkTSqxbh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2774dfa0-469c-4790-b670-56e6790bfb46&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90e2b412&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680720)

12\. Business Report


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The business report can view the total sales amount of the day, full discounts and other information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FAfqiXLwoZGJi2E3Atmv6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f830c18-ea18-451e-bc22-e69da56d4595&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a6a3f4a0&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680721)

13\. Stock Query


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Inventory inquiry can check the current quantity of goods in stock.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FTYRY6c0I8QT8SJByWAgV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf40f129-56c1-4ea9-962a-026281b0abef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=30cfdf5b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680722)

14\. Points


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The points page displays the member's points redemption details, as well as the currently redeemed and pending items. The waiter can use the scanner function to scan the customer's point redemption QR code to redeem the items.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fp11FimlivuJ5UYkLyRQC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a9ec79d-b47a-46ee-bb98-a502b52c1315&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=293caf3b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680723)

15\. Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the parameter setting page, you can configure printer parameters. Such as printer IP , print size, whether printing is enabled, etc.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FGcIRLKM0weXoF2pnFau2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D855302f1-241c-4154-81a8-414f5eeb9d09&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90fb658d&sv=2)

# Manual for Maintenance Management Portal | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-1-service-provider-portal)

**1** Service Provider Portal


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc26390)

1.1 Function Overview

Wizarpos service provider portal, mainly provides functions for service providers to manage merchants. It allows adding and modifying one or more merchants under this service provider. The merchant types supported are retail and catering. It is possible to view the transaction records of each merchant, as well as the terminal information and quantity bound to each merchant.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc5715)

1.2 Login

Enter the account password to log in to the backend. Before logging in, you can choose the language

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FWBBBWfKV1Jx9n5VmhB6b%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd6987df&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc16686)

1.3 Merchant Management - Settlement Records

Click on Settlement Results to access the settlement records, where you can view the transaction data of all merchants under this service provider, including member transactions and bank card transactions

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FTAvrkLP2Qt1jRUVjLIs2%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=54ded094&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc24981)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-1.4-merchant-management-merchant-information-management)

1.4 Merchant Management - Merchant Information Management

Click on MerchantList to enter the merchant list, where you can add new merchants (retail or catering), search and edit merchant information, configure payment methods, set payment parameters, resend emails, view bound terminals, enable merchants, disable merchants, etc

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FHDEjBTUxke8IWyYMAm1p%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8e0655e0&sv=2)

Click "Add Merchant" to add a new merchant. After filling in the merchant information, complete the account opening process. The merchant will receive an account opening email and can log in to the merchant portal using the initial account and password to perform operations

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FyTATeVI9hHFAlZxh0UQP%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7ab4d92d&sv=2)

Clicking on "more" allows you to configure payments, edit merchants, and manage terminals

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FJQtZKDGQpDjOYxstUqME%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=149fdc1&sv=2)

Terminal Management Click on Payment Setting to configure the existing payment methods, whether to enable or disable online and offline

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FhsuGBdTp8gzU9RTRU37M%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=24fe0ac1&sv=2)

Clicking on Payment Setting allows you to configure payment parameters according to the actual payment integration needs. After configuration, you can proceed with actual payment transactions

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FCvPCNegGqSqjxNkkgWvn%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=100663fc&sv=2)

You can make actual payments and transactions. Click "Add" to set up payment methods, transaction fees, and maximum transaction fees

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FY0SfVtaLp2jzDM3di7ad%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e75aeb2d&sv=2)

Click on "Resend Email" to resend the email. If the customer forgets their password, clicking on "Resend Email" will send the new password to the email address provided during registration

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fu3KyC4wRgJp7MgHioSEY%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c67008f1&sv=2)

Click to resend emai

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fx3Xptob5LSQTe7sEKZrE%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=23d252fa&sv=2)

Will send the new password to the email address filled in during registration. Click on "Terminal Manage" to view the terminal information bound to the merchant, and you can edit the terminal type and delete the terminal

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc32108)

1.5 Merchant Management - Terminal Management

Clicking on Terminal Manage allows you to view terminal information for all merchants, and perform actions such as adding, editing, and deleting

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FX08iz7bT8yvC0Tqy7Ye7%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13f2c71d&sv=2)

Can edit terminal information

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQFRniSQiuGvIkm3B0kPp%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a7dfea92&sv=2)

Clicking on "Add" allows you to add a new terminal for a specific merchant. The terminal can only be logged in and used after it is bound to the merchant

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FW1XgDEFAEq93PO6l5bNG%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f9e058b1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-1.6-agent-management)

1.6 Agent Management

Clicking on the Agent Manage page displays agents. Agents are subordinates of service providers and can onboard merchants

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FwO16Km1EQC3oXLbGr3o2%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c56da38&sv=2)

Click Add to add an agent, fill in the information, click the confirm button, and the agent will be created. The initial password will be sent to the entered email

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F9m6VoqGIZenloZrETu3p%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c881d79a&sv=2)

Clicking on Payment Setting allows you to configure payment settings

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F9K7I5pKWebIjbNFj27ky%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc3ede26&sv=2)

You can configure the payment methods and commission rates for agents, with a maximum commission cap

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FCdcEie6NTbEPANIPqxfX%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3aa8f9ae&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-1.7-payment-methods)

1.7 Payment methods

Click on Payment Method to view and create payment methods

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fo87RvY1knPVOSuDEOiiP%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e4823ba4&sv=2)

Click on Edit to view detailed configuration methods

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fki1cRFnnQbvxaPpGOBgC%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a35f1e3&sv=2)

Clicking on Add allows you to create a payment method

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjED0QTNGkSbiBxIYR7QI%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=53830859&sv=2)

1.8 Service Fee

Clicking on Handing Fee Details will allow you to view a summary of the fees

1.9 Service Fee Summary

Click Service Fee Summary

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FOisERiS6ygLsDLMCy3d5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9af22698-2b28-434b-ac9d-ae3da9d81def&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=891e1b83&sv=2)

1.10 System Settings - Role Settings

Click on Role Manage to enter and view the currently available roles. Currently, there is only one type of role, which is the employee role, and it allows for menu authorization

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FY4VViKXYLKc9bCJFUU6P%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b36bcb1-bda5-498f-ba9a-19452d043324&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c6640a17&sv=2)

You can authorize the menu. Click on "Role resources" to edit the menu authorization. The checked menus will only be visible when logging into the system

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FwhrPpbYSo39W2iPyUKp8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D912ea72a-c1f2-470c-babf-331f6bfe913f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=233fb60a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc13971)

1.11 System Settings - User Management

Click on "User Manage" to enter user management. You can view all current account information, add new users, edit existing users, enable/disable accounts, and reset passwords

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Ff1nLga0IHCy4UOShIn0r%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24baa51d-1134-4b5a-a619-e732a15c3dfe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e1a69f3a&sv=2)

Click Add to create a new user

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FmLciRUS4SUm5ntpINkya%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d37e94e-c9fc-406c-8473-3e06f43effb1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d464f908&sv=2)

Click Edit to edit the user

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrrvhPljnRaxfzbdm1xti%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D60c8430e-ff1b-41e9-a02c-0771b3396a87&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c918c6a2&sv=2)

Click Disable or Enable to activate or deactivate the user

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrNsVZGVKeAZuXtBQlcSm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0c65508-1b7a-4898-b7c0-1dee74fab582&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20d438e8&sv=2)

Click on "Reset Password" to reset the user's login password

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fg1gyYidSvhEHCDswRzYY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db35be808-14aa-45ef-8342-aaa0aafe2a7a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a3384a50&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-1.12-merchant-onboarding-announcement)

**1.12** Merchant Onboarding Announcement

Click on "Merchant entry notice" to view the merchant entry announcement. This page displays the information that users need to know when applying for the free version of the POS machine

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FUFI1Kqcq14pY2PdhVZff%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcaa84b8c-ffd8-4a52-abeb-2f990213912b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba3fd6ee&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-1.13-parameter-setting)

**1.13** Parameter Setting

Clicking on Parameter Setting allows you to replace the icon in the top left corner of the portal

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FuIrGYCTbN0TKcVgavi7m%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D778bc67b-bd4c-4f36-9d59-73ecd79e744a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6aace8d3&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc183)

2 Operation and Maintenance Management Portal


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc7757)

2.1 Overview

Wizarpos operation and maintenance management portal is a backend system used by operation and maintenance personnel. It is mainly used to open service providers and then view all merchants under the service providers, as well as generated transaction data, order data, and member recharge and consumption data

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc182)

2.2 Login

Enter your username and password on the login page, select the language, and log in to the system

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQeLmlE2UBvfDVFPipWpm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58209906-48d8-4c90-8128-3802284c831c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f34da6f6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc23150)

2.3 Data Overview

Login System After logging in, you will first enter the Dashboard page. Here, the data overview is displayed, showing the current number of merchants, number of members, daily transaction amount, and transaction amount chart data

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FDsX4t4p8m9rwnA6vsxjq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b6d9c42-661c-4b2f-b0a5-369a565ac543&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=87b425a8&sv=2)

You can view transaction data for merchants in the food and retail industry

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FVqbZCB5pgkcPDYwOU8Cd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dadcb9881-64ce-4330-ae9f-4b927470aa24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a51ff210&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc29471)

2.4 Service Provider Management

Click on Service Provider to enter the service provider list, where you can add, search, and modify service providers

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F1bgYn2EMbT744kRK6DFp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5c5e8126-8889-46cf-8c54-c15bcd275bdc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3ed045e1&sv=2)

Clicking on "Add" allows you to create a new service provider. After filling in the information, the service provider will be created. The email sent to the merchant when creating an account will be sent using the email provided by the service provider

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F5lKfBAAw8EZ4IQ0kP6lD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6069edfa-113a-4ced-b5ab-175553fea1bc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b1a001cb&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FFo1ARvZLSPZfzsCULFgq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf19b77e-fc22-418f-966a-f2e643c35ac1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2375d738&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc32113)

2.5 Role Management

Click on Role Manage to enter role management, which displays the current list of all roles. You can create and edit service providers, and authorize menus for service providers

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FllACselcZkBEKvlI9HWj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e885c94-d714-47e6-9efd-89d972ea7ed9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f6d9102d&sv=2)

Clicking on Add allows you to create roles. There are three types of roles here, corresponding to different menu permissions.

PTL-ADMIN is the merchant type, corresponding to the menu permissions of the retail and catering portals. Operations are used to set up retail and catering merchants, and determine which menus they can see

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FZua8HSpPWs9Hxd3wQQh2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63eb0b71-b582-4bd1-874b-09f94f036b06&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=35a2aadd&sv=2)

OPS-ADMIN is a service provider type, used for setting up which menus the service provider can see

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FpZ7i64HOr2luTZaPdFeT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf99734c-49e4-4b75-bcdc-add9ad9ecbc7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=857d1600&sv=2)

SAAS-ADMIN is an operations and maintenance type used to set up which menus the operations and maintenance backend login account can see

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F9NgF9lNq3bfe4youKfuU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9efcd11-37c2-4059-88de-09eeb2f44ca3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1a9539&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc20347)

2.6 Transaction Records

Click on Trans List, operations and maintenance administrators can view the transaction records of all merchants

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FRPx3GZXuQMDgYGJIt8ur%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3cd5548d-4b54-465f-bd8e-41da2a441664&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4348e236&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc31697)

2.7 Order Report

Clicking on "Order Report", the operations and maintenance administrator can view the number and amount of online and offline transactions generated by all merchants each day

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FSXsP6CZigz6rwO5bk00I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61d6e6dd-57c5-4e2d-922f-b5638c4941a8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a55cd31&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#toc28449)

2.8 Membership Report

Clicking on the Membership Report, the operations and maintenance administrator can query all the members under all merchants, as well as the generated records of member recharge and consumption

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F4LOrYbDrkfxrIcsaY4p1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D636fe162-ac50-4bc8-938d-e47caffe0aa2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7953490&sv=2)

Click on Sales Report to view member consumption records

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FAqYvjHvq7nvjinyK5vTX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D601c8e84-8027-443d-8fc2-c58f0a36d482&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b7e6f7fc&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-3-agent-portal)

3 Agent Portal


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-3.1-overview)

3.1 Overview

Wizarpos agent portal, mainly provides functions for agents to manage merchants. It allows agents to add and modify merchants under their agency. The merchant types supported are retail and catering. Agents can view transaction records of each merchant, as well as the terminal information and quantity bound to each merchant

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-3.2-login)

3.2 Login

Enter the account password to log in to the backend. Before logging in, you can choose the language

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FD76HTCyFlUStg5kNIOtq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def8f31f0-d729-4d56-8d52-7a99fe7ebfb7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b6bf10d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-3.3-merchant-management-settlement-records)

3.3 Merchant Management - Settlement Records

Click on Settlement Results to access the settlement records, where you can view all transaction data of merchant members and bank card transactions under this agent

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fq0KfjGkQl8YtCun4m1Xp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3936b159-de77-4a9f-8165-f5763176e981&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8763d900&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-3.4-merchant-management-merchant-information-management)

3.4 Merchant Management - Merchant Information Management

Click on MerchantList to enter the merchant list, click on Add to add a new merchant (retail or catering), search and edit merchant information, resend emails, view bound terminals, enable/disable merchants, etc.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FF4pAxSdEAhIJs6Mf2MWP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03162941-b479-4d89-98de-56667f145d8e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9f6163e0&sv=2)

Click on Add to fill in the merchant information and complete the account opening. The merchant will receive an account opening email and can log in to the merchant portal with the initial account and password to perform operations

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FpC46yhpUDQBzAfiMZHaP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30eeaa4e-2df9-4c66-ad0e-d1ee1e14b82f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cdc3d793&sv=2)

Click on "Resend Email" to resend the email. If the customer forgets their password, clicking on "Resend Email" will send the new password to the email address provided during registration

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FinDq15ZhwGhT8kfx4CHq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b41f8cf-8b33-4ba6-bcbc-9683dca0463d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e09d5467&sv=2)

Clicking on Terminal Manage allows you to view the terminal information bound to the merchant, and you can edit the terminal type and delete the terminal

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FhXMMGsHQBHAJ1BwmYT8o%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ed3a0d3-e590-46ca-a368-45c46132927c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d20ce738&sv=2)

Click Disable to disable the merchant, click Enable to enable the merchant

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F3n1E159HBFqHalBz5wG7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a03ca6b-88b0-4f1c-880e-6434a37525cf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a354620&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-3.5-merchant-management-terminal-management)

3.5 Merchant Management - Terminal Management

Clicking on "Add" allows you to add a new terminal for a specific merchant. The terminal can only be logged in and used after it is bound to the merchant

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FGKhhdZxfvNLZya0U9hws%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0824b8d-85b3-4fe8-b46d-ebc012902e55&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b4b9c733&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-maintenance-management-portal#id-3.6-system-settings-user-management)

3.6 System Settings - User Management

Click on "User Manage" to enter user management. You can view all current account information, add new users, edit existing users, enable/disable accounts, and reset passwords

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FT55vReIQs6d4wEDGPJq1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D093fc982-f9cd-4106-ad8c-52dca8dc90fc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7ad98d23&sv=2)

Click Add to add a new user

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FYSnefpCrCaDEAAlcykbU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db116323c-3ec7-4235-b987-29768d2c091b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57ae9dae&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FBaljjkPhTE13L3CIvpFs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32324ebf-0697-4164-9dfb-9a679f3d30b7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=34d9d07a&sv=2)
