# Manual for Catering Portal | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-1-overview-of-functions)

1\. Overview of Functions


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Wizarpos Catering Portal is a web-based backend management system. Restaurant businesses use this system for various editing and settings related to dishes, membership, and marketing, as well as viewing sales data. The system provides the following main functions:

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-1-dish-management)

1\. Dish Management

Merchants upload various types of dishes in the backend, such as hot dishes, cold dishes, Western cuisine, dim sum, and snacks. Dishes are customized by specifications, taste, preparation method, and additional ingredients to meet different customer ordering needs. Both waitstaff and customers can see the corresponding dishes when using the ordering system.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-2-marketing-activities)

2\. Marketing Activities

Merchants can set up various online and offline marketing activities through the backend, such as discounts, full reductions, special prices, point malls, and consumption vouchers, providing diners with diverse dining experiences.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-3-table-management)

3\. Table Management

Merchants can create various table categories in the backend, such as hall or private room, and then create various tables under these categories.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-4-sales-management)

4\. Sales Management

Merchants can view various business reports, sales documents, consumption statistics, refund statistics, and tip statistics in the backend.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-5-points-mall)

5\. Points Mall

Merchants can configure activities for exchanging goods with points, such as exchanging 100 points for a bottle of cola or 500 points for a dish, increasing user consumption enthusiasm and interest. Waitstaff use handheld devices to scan customer redemption codes to exchange goods for customers.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-6-chain-stores)

6\. Chain Stores

If a merchant has multiple stores, the system supports chain store functionality. Customers can register as members at any store, and the member balance is universally applicable across stores. Coupons obtained from consumption can also be used at any store.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-2-login)

2\. Login


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Open the merchant catering management backend (hereinafter referred to as the backend). For the first login, merchants must use the initial account and password provided by the system to log in. The system supports multi-language login, which can be switched independently.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FqfHdVjnyvxfDtROga9Ti%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7e621fc-a71d-4987-a9c0-6689b741c0ab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=525a17f3&sv=2)

The system is divided into official and trial versions. Users can click Demo Tour to enter the trial version interface without logging in. In the trial version, merchants cannot perform add, delete, or modify operations, only view data. After logging into the trial version, the top right of the interface displays the current status as Demo merchants.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FiDm6bwgEGuth6534I89w%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59f6bb8d-b9a6-46ef-a55d-01da48f56ce9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8f7ccb6f&sv=2)

Note: Unless otherwise stated, this document defaults to the official version interface.

The official version interface is as follows:

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FauqUgbfgpEF6g3rwHb4I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16fcf273-6759-465d-bace-a817c9c66e76&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e72457b&sv=2)

2.1 Homepage

After successfully logging in, users are redirected to the homepage. The homepage displays the store's operating data, such as the number and amount of orders for the current week and month. Below, line or bar charts display data for the week's order count, dish sales, and monthly order count and dish sales.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0YlLYwwOvh69IZF2GwNS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71f340aa-455e-497e-898e-f76e1189a0f9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cac901b3&sv=2)

Password modification and logout: Users can click the account in the top right corner to change the password or log out.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FZSAOZiMXHwFOOsjUw6T8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72ddcb51-a86c-40cf-b99d-450d5d522aca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e861819&sv=2)

The process is as follows: Enter the old password and the new password twice, click confirm, and the account modification is complete.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FbIlpSPhNDyrZ2rtimS6j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff0e0151-ee3c-4046-9a25-c3914b9804b4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90e79ffd&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-3-transaction-records)

3\. Transaction Records


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-3-1-transaction-records)

3.1 Transaction Records

By clicking the Trans List menu, users can view all transaction records of the merchant, searchable by time range, payment type, payment method, etc.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FfaW3sVs2LdOPa9S3lCjg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D10bcc3c8-d898-4d95-ba26-c4c52078a330&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db7d61d7&sv=2)

Transaction records include comprehensive and detailed payment information, including device terminal, table number, payment type, and payment amount.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-3-2-transaction-summary)

3.2 Transaction Summary

By clicking the Trans Report menu, users can view the merchant's transaction data summary, searchable by time range.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Frl4xNtFh4o94YYBOF4tr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5ce2e56-9c5e-4377-afa1-b38ec95b8058&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cd6e3b42&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FwaLnWHNUCNgc1O1xB0mh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1342a3e7-71e0-44c7-8639-f6179b4a6b72&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c60271b6&sv=2)

The transaction summary includes online and offline orders, payment methods, order payment count, and payment amount.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FDBUdIGtX884gApgkdvtE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ba5523a-5528-4db5-86ff-0011cf15d2e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=676d196f&sv=2)

Based on the time range, users can query the transaction amount summary for various payment methods within the period.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-3-3-settlement-records)

3.3 Settlement Records

By clicking the Billing Records menu, users can view the merchant's settlement records.

Merchant settlement refers to the fees the merchant needs to pay to the payment channel providers. The actual settlement amount is displayed based on the connected payment channel and is usually settled to the merchant through a T+1 method.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FHmqghGRNGuOomVlzx7Pp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8722ff9a-79bd-4eab-b5a7-a5ff3e399db5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ecd1c1a9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-4-dish-management)

4\. Dish Management


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-4-1-dish-categories)

4.1 Dish Categories

By clicking Dishes Category, users enter the dish category menu, where merchants can create dish categories, supporting up to two levels.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FUTlL3RBNSNUJKps8Cim2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd28e8190-5aed-42b4-8e45-1d0ab0f326d3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f76e806&sv=2)

By clicking Add, merchants can input category names and codes, supporting enabling and disabling categories for in-store ordering (POS) and H5 ordering (consumer end).

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FxrloZyDF43K72AL7Uaxx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd26977f2-04db-4451-8078-112efb1219e9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c490dbbe&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-4-2-dish-details)

4.2 Dish Details

By clicking Dishes Details, users enter the dish details menu, where all dishes are created.

Dishes support image uploads, visible to both merchants and customers. Additionally, merchants can set dish specifications, tastes, additional ingredients, and preparation methods. All dishes can be exported as an xls document.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FotNcVk7VOFvJX14u6XyP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df977870f-7835-4a88-8d1b-254a138866d0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98e3fa1c&sv=2)

Exported dish tables are as follows:

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Ffu7I69GiNOeHp5lUmmar%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f19ddb4-7586-4357-a7d8-7964e9aebbb1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0525569&sv=2)

Creating a dish: Click Add, input the dish name, select category, unit, and choose dish specifications and other parameters to create a dish.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fnswcq0wh0DlVYHUpeo1e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1638b42e-6e5f-44b1-a437-f2ed367eb306&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2fb63f88&sv=2)

Select specifications, taste, additional ingredients, preparation methods, and other methods to create a complete dish. The specific selected parameters need to be created in the dish properties menu in advance.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fxvs6AM331fV7hFtM0STx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D89866cbb-4f1a-4d9b-a8aa-afc0bc724eee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8582bb7f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-4-3-dish-properties)

4.3 Dish Properties

By clicking Food Properties, users enter the dish properties menu, where merchants can create basic properties of dishes.

These include settings for dish specifications, tastes, additional ingredients, and preparation methods, which merchants can create independently.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FqdNFPWJvQ2y0Pi4NwjlY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8d242b3-a4b7-4062-90e5-c5938ab706ae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=afb709e8&sv=2)

In the "spec" attribute, merchants can set the portion size, such as large, medium, small, or other specifications. Different specifications correspond to different dish prices.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdQXPxCA6QwZNr6R8M4JQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9301f75c-25b9-4dc8-a65a-a889324f7524&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=19938ec3&sv=2)

By clicking the Taste attribute, merchants can set the dish taste.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FcqZf3qXg001xCpn88DiL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8609a1eb-aa65-48c5-bcbc-1562d79653f8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cb54d4d6&sv=2)

By clicking Add, enter the taste name, and merchants will cater according to the selected taste, which does not involve dish pricing.

Add-on allows users to view and add additional ingredients or side dishes, which can be priced separately. For example, if a customer orders a steak and chooses side dishes like eggs and ham, these are the side dishes, which support multiple selections.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fu1Dws6SZ9Wy49zREE4xp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f421923-0e74-42f0-be34-ee23084b92a1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba70e2be&sv=2)

By clicking Add, create side dish names and prices.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FYEmHnoO6BVuPRvxiZcdp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D23717ade-c98e-4634-9bf3-aa37d1cd21d4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5d3a500&sv=2)

By clicking Cooking Method, merchants can create preparation methods for dishes, such as steaming, frying, boiling, etc., which do not affect dish prices.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F9Sc1N0m563n5RQ22RzXl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2df12cd6-d103-4be7-b435-063aa12f97ea&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89ca71f2&sv=2)

By clicking Add Method, create a method name for dishes.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-4-4-combo-meals)

4.4 Combo Meals

By clicking Combo Meal, users enter the combo meal page. Combo meals are a sales method for combining dishes.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FLyPc89QgnKnleUSlpnz7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def26ce44-d5ae-4a6c-badf-a8b0f7802b3b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e6a65571&sv=2)

By clicking Add, create a combo meal by entering the dish name, selecting category and description.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQZIyZZ67axx9SnXQjOzx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad07089e-c6c3-40cc-8cf8-1dcec92983dc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d3442d8&sv=2)

Choose different dishes, enter quantity, price, packaging fee, support image upload, click confirm button, and the combo is created.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FXjU1veNLAUTaxoXWuXMy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D851cc3e6-73ab-4afe-bb22-4fdd03e59c16&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8236c193&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-5-sales-management)

5\. Sales Management


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-5-1-business-reports)

5.1 Business Reports

By clicking Total Report, users can query transaction data summaries for the merchant within a specific time period, querying total member recharge, total discounts, and full refunds.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FaX0pHqJyDbDaiJjlNpoK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D922ec91c-894e-4038-a2f9-8b9158bd9e4b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f2c66b7c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-5-2-sales-documents)

5.2 Sales Documents

By clicking Sales Report, users can view the merchant's sales documents. Merchants can query based on sales orders, types, and time ranges, supporting report export operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FUaHxmMEe7v01f3RLPlee%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D476636c6-945b-4469-9330-53a513878488&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1d1e8e8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-5-3-order-source)

5.3 Order Source

By clicking Order Report, users can view the source statistics of the merchant's sales documents. Sources are divided into dine-in and online ordering, showing transaction amounts, quantities, and transaction methods.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FuArJiCuPLyfiYIWCO51y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc275a3b5-1da5-4118-bd2e-2fa6a14d30a3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=472a60fc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-5-4-sales-statistics)

5.4 Sales Statistics

By clicking Dish Report, users enter the sales statistics menu, displaying the sales quantity and sales amount summary of dishes.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQm8Mjgt3uPic6OdyWmLi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ea2e86d-e556-44e3-bd18-c00442e9e0ea&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c82f0927&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-5-5-refund-statistics)

5.5 Refund Statistics

By clicking Refund Report, users enter the refund statistics menu. Merchants can statistically analyze by time range, refund name, quantity, and amount.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FTSvnGxD3VdAnXf1zDpZR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9eed5790-045e-407d-ab59-91dc5106f89e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=27ebe47b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-5-6-tip-statistics)

5.6 Tip Statistics

By clicking Tip Report, users enter the tip statistics menu. Merchants can query the total amount of tips and details for waitstaff based on the time range.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F5FOhGDpKeSv1KnCO3LfK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da524e7f4-5a35-411e-900b-ff1908766609&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1409accd&sv=2)

By clicking Details, query tip amount details and associated sales order numbers.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Ff2jKnQmCCbNchEiy7HFT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38da0c5d-bd1a-46bd-a213-560ff2ca3be8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0cb77d1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-6-table-management)

6\. Table Management


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By clicking Table Manager, users enter the table management menu, allowing merchants to create all tables in the store. If tables are categorized, such as hall or private room, categories can also be created.

Tables can be bound to a waiter, and table QR codes can be exported. Users scan the table QR code to order when they arrive.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FSSJ8pjhiY4wxvjCIRtom%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7b31110-15c4-401a-9d0f-919b33351f24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1cb0945b&sv=2)

By clicking Table QR Code, download the table QR code, supporting bulk export of all table QR codes.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FxALnhBsFqmkXdUTSfyQW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5ff0fdc-aa82-439f-a193-b170a1cf7a34&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=55f657e9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-7-membership-management)

7\. Membership Management


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-7-1-member-information)

7.1 Member Information

By clicking Membership, users can query all registered member information under the merchant (member registration requires users to scan the merchant or table QR code). Members' email, balance, details, etc., can be viewed, and merchants can freeze or unfreeze members.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FsqK7kyFE9GU7FwE8PL62%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ccf8284-c36a-40db-8606-c611c56f7df6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2269cb49&sv=2)

By clicking Detail, view detailed member information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FNnBSAtkuFkPFageAgUiI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a2c07c8-7bea-4889-9cca-50a784322108&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=53d87af1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-7-2-member-transaction-records)

7.2 Member Transaction Records

By clicking Member Trans, merchants can view members' recharge records, consumption records, and points records.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F5zKru0Ws3gNuXZ0VEyZb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13ae87c3-98d5-45aa-a307-a4d5d4b10cd7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c254913f&sv=2)

By clicking Sales Report, view member consumption records.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F9jv7jYtsKp8ye56KCjWe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33865056-abf2-471c-b9b2-ad487125bfdf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8d59c12&sv=2)

By clicking Points Report, view member points records.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FM6vEi3fEh8cLgGb0YtyW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69d1f93e-b5e7-489d-993c-d1fa33cdca37&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b2626fa&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-8-marketing-center)

8\. Marketing Center


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-8-1-marketing-activities)

8.1 Marketing Activities

By clicking Promotion, merchants can create different marketing activities. The same marketing activity cannot be created twice simultaneously.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FZ44G7d92FCMp6YtJpIXx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5720671-cda2-41dc-b39a-f8f5f618a15d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3aada1ee&sv=2)

By clicking Details, view the details of marketing activities.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FCERZgwvCcsqnewHEopCB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9405b691-fc40-416d-95b6-9c0e016f7021&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1df9eaee&sv=2)

By clicking Create Marketing Activity, create activities such as full reductions, special offers, discounts, points mall, consumption coupons, combo meals, earn points for consumption, member recharge, and member registration activities.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fdu3fXlCIVODk6HnxSxnI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c628801-2459-46bf-b975-11bf53a4c134&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ca74fd2&sv=2)

By clicking Full Discount, create full reduction activities.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FgxjyW9aqMVgNZtdvBUdo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3dac02cc-e2d8-4314-b6e9-d8c9c79f5436&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20a764ca&sv=2)

By clicking Special Offer, create special price activities, selecting one or more products for settings.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FH09zq5Si0AVRKJ2lueYq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D391e0bb7-75a6-47e8-9999-25708cfd5bf3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9bcef679&sv=2)

After selecting the products for special pricing, enter the special price amount to complete the setup.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FZBsBI0owDf34OkErLKMt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc874072-4963-488b-acd2-f5dbb84964b4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=24f5d16e&sv=2)

By clicking Discount, create discount activities, applying discounts according to the set amount. For example, if spending 100 earns a 10% discount, then it's a 90% price.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0XgQLpnMpvQaxl6dUEoR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D383d7291-02d5-4ae2-b78d-0a486ced0f10&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=994af516&sv=2)

By clicking Points Mall, create points mall activities, allowing points to be exchanged for goods.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F43GRF1VsQ8fnCnShfeZO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6742f2c8-3eee-46ce-8a48-b7bcb44eace3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d22c3316&sv=2)

Select products available for exchange, enter the points required for exchange, the total number of products available, and the limit per user.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FikjZwUQ6AoQOdjqlfcWS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e99e3b9-546e-44b0-8268-fc48df763aee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8f10eea4&sv=2)

By clicking Member Consumption Coupon, create consumption coupon activities.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fdieb4KPIumbDFYyGTrEU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e42afc5-ff65-430d-8b49-3b5161d3f59d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=675e39d3&sv=2)

Enter the specific amount, select the coupon specification template to be given, and click confirm to complete the setup.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FafDaTJ2DHqUhxMnljvSR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe56976f-a2c0-4113-946f-2785cc37dcc0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e1f218cb&sv=2)

By clicking Earn points for members spending, create activities where members earn points for consumption. Enter a name, description, select time, and set the specified amount to earn specified points. Customers can exchange products in the points mall.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F8dYWMSME5ffHNEAefdCb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27ae08f3-c4c2-448f-853a-291bc73ceffc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dac8b3b9&sv=2)

Member recharge activities can be created by date, offering coupons, balance, and points.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FKcy6CCRU4HOob5tQRcRk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D468b92fb-c5c9-4a38-92d3-5316220faf33&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba5d0a46&sv=2)

Member registration activities allow first-time registered members to receive points and membership coupons.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjRfDacD4XoneEalCcm4e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02a97ed7-c45b-4525-8697-c138fc9daf47&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8297fa39&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-8-2-full-reduction-and-discount-statistics)

8.2 Full Reduction and Discount Statistics

By clicking Promotion Report, view marketing activity statistics. Merchants can view full reduction and discount statistics.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FSX8A8noBIZEFSJUx6QtO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a555628-66f6-4c7a-9bed-90dba0f640d9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8845d68b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-8-3-create-coupon-templates)

8.3 Create Coupon Templates

By clicking Tickets, merchants can create coupon templates. The coupons given in member consumption coupon activities are created here.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fu21bsVknAqS15TUV5TE8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd63f03ca-c55c-4e0a-b104-6783dfff690d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=193353d1&sv=2)

By clicking Add, create a new coupon template. After completing the required information, click confirm to complete the new template.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FKjqtIcBv1zVW3ve8uppp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c8665d3-4308-4be3-8fef-fd4fb2f61d43&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b6390d3&sv=2)

By clicking Detail, view the coupon template details, and click Delete to remove.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FmNV2gQpVcljHuy6mQA2f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4dffeb0e-5eea-4475-b4f1-ded7755509a7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dc7bd270&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-9-system-settings)

9\. System Settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-9-1-store-information)

9.1 Store Information

By clicking Merchant Info, view detailed information about the merchant.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FODqEjcIIuaCzPSxmwBHv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba4940b1-4d28-4ed9-b335-f707dbbad471&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5bc5135a&sv=2)

By clicking Edit, support editing merchant information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FBzxhjrq4TrTK54tkwF5S%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d813eff-a27f-46da-a778-b92ac64655ed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9aa078b1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-9-2-account-management)

9.2 Account Management

By clicking Account Manage, view and create operators and managers for the merchant. The manager is mainly for backend management, while operators mainly operate handheld POS terminals but can also log into the backend to view data. Permissions can be authorized by the administrator.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FAbZfe5q853Sfn939llUy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0357a9e-22d3-4b53-bedd-1458b5fa3d2a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=989ee2da&sv=2)

By clicking Edit, view and modify account information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F9Rc6v9iZxNmkZlkd5QuC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e501fa0-9ee0-4395-b679-ef70a5c40eed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea979aea&sv=2)

Administrators can also click Terminal Setting in the top right corner of the page to set a security password, which is used for secure verification during refund transactions at store terminals.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fblz9PZs1qm47rejnPFA8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcdd85438-8623-401e-989b-ee967a0e40f1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=559c67dc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-9-3-authorization-management)

9.3 Authorization Management

By clicking Role Manage, enter authorization management. Administrators can set role authorizations for managers and operators.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FTi10QJwdnQE6BWGwczgs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a7dfb3c-f637-4e90-84ec-42b38812a8c9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e900e2e&sv=2)

Based on the selected menus, set menus as visible or not.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FxGW2YfQ4kd569AHj1Rev%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc30d9a8f-ba36-4e49-add1-7e3118e88814&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=edf444f6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-9-4-parameter-configuration)

9.4 Parameter Configuration

By clicking Parameter Setting, configure the H5 ordering program's page settings, advertisement carousel, merchant icon and homepage image, recommended dishes, large screen carousel, and custom order status.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FCOebZZWBkxCfQIvm8Kjs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D216f7b89-f730-475f-a0fe-3e75cfc9742c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea9f543c&sv=2)

By clicking Network print settings, configure the kitchen slip printer used in the restaurant. When a waiter or user places an order, the dish slip will be notified to the kitchen printer via the network, and the printer will print the kitchen slip, allowing chefs to prepare dishes according to it.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjCcUr3uYOMyo5XyCSAJm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D51ff3d38-5a4d-4e4e-9cee-db455cf33975&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=baa33cab&sv=2)

By clicking Other pay setting, create other payment methods used during POS checkout.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FzlLjR48C6ThvtCCktoR9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd7042b3-cdf7-448a-ad7d-f8802a78cd96&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f11bd0ea&sv=2)

By clicking Large screen rotating image settings, create carousel images for the large screen machine. The large screen is a device used in stores for user ordering, allowing users to place orders on the large screen.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrFpdKnvsnbU1t1yU4X3N%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D243af957-47f6-46a0-ae52-35c616c2dc58&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cecf6f26&sv=2)

Large screen carousel, set the D22 large screen terminal, carousel images.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F4uKSWJqU7CsegFFk88G6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99a4ebb1-ff8d-4877-899c-4b58b3b47d42&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86c372c9&sv=2)

Custom order status allows custom takeaway order statuses.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FKaH0nZucI6vfWFM0WfU1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7596c019-19e8-4e1d-ab4d-68802951136c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=70b58bfb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/management/manual-for-catering-portal#id-9-5-delivery-settings)

9.5 Delivery Settings

By clicking Pickup Setting, set the merchant's takeaway pickup point. Users can order through the H5 merchant store and choose in-store pickup.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FcIPhnnMxPYX1VbkbEE61%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a374b54-43c4-4bd6-8a77-d18672995326&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=82706599&sv=2)

Merchants can create pickup point information, filling in the pickup point name and address information, etc.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F5gBYF9FbLOvzPxxziLAz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D515cc662-fb02-4b84-b316-d5ddacfd59c0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3c263b91&sv=2)

# MDB Communication Protocal | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#introduction)

Introduction

This manual describes the serial communication protocol between Q3 Pos and MDB Interface Board, which will be short as “MIB” in follow content.

The basic baud rate of serial port is set as 115200

As the Q3 POS could be receive command from MIB as a slave, and also could send command to MIB as a master (e.g., send “begin session” command to inform the MDB VMC it’s ready for pay), a mode byte was added in serial frame to show if a command is slave response or a master request.

The request command always anticipates a response command except the checksum is wrong, or the incorrect serial format, in another word, the slave will use silence as a NAK. **Please refer to the** [**documentation** arrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/advanceSDK/MDB_interface_board_serial_protocol_20241226.pdf)
**for specific commands and details.**

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#serial-protocol-packet-definition)

Serial Protocol Packet Definition

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#serial-port-parameters)

Serial Port Parameters

*   Baud rate: 115200
    
*   Data format: 8 bits, 1 stop bit, no parity
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#packet-format)

Packet Format

*   Start code: size 1 byte, always be 0x09
    
*   Length: size 1 byte, the number bytes of mode, data, and checksum.
    
*   Mode: size 1 byte, 0x00 means a request packet, 0x01 means a response packet, other value is prohibited.
    
*   Data: size n bytes, The data could be raw MDB commands, such as SETUP, VEND. Or the MIB control commands, such as GET VERSION, SET PARAMETER.
    
*   Checksum: size 1 byte, using LRC algorithm, input data were "mode, data"
    
*   End code: size 1 byte, always be 0x0D.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#specifics)

Specifics

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#mdb-forwarding-mechanism)

MDB Forwarding Mechanism

When the MIB receive the VMC request, it removes the MDB mode bit, fill into serial packet data area, and transmit to serial port. In the opposite direction, the MIB receive the response, it unwraps the packet, and adding mode bit to the tail bytes, sending to the VMC, wait for the acknowledge.MIB will forward all the MDB cashless device commands (MDB spec section 7), except VMC request Poll.

Example: RESET

1.  _VMC -> MIB:_ 0x110 0x10
    
2.  _MIB -> Q3V:_ 0x09 0x04 0x00 0x10 0x10 0xE0 0x0D
    
3.  Q3V _-> MIB:_ 0x09 0x04 0x01 0x00 0x00 0xFF 0x0D
    
4.  _MIB -> VMC:_ 0x00 0x100
    
5.  _VMC -> MIB : 0x00_
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#application-notes)

Application Notes

*   Focus on steps 2 and 3 in the MDB Forwarding Mechanism.
    
*   The application handles all cashless commands except POLL.
    
*   The cashless reader initiates a begin session command to notify the VMC when ready for a transaction.
    
*   MDB raw data includes its checksum byte, distinct from the serial frame checksum.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#a-typical-mdb-transaction-flow)

A Typical MDB Transaction Flow

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%2Fblobs%2F1fZFmaKVoimHuCqczG14%2FMdb_flow_chart.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=451a1480&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#protocol-command-definition)

Protocol Command Definition

circle-info

Please refer to the [documentation arrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/advanceSDK/MDB_interface_board_serial_protocol_20241226.pdf)
for specific commands and details.

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#common-mdb-forwarding-command)

Common MDB Forwarding Command

This command forwards raw MDB commands (including MDB CHK), with the MDB mode bit removed.

Request Packet:

Mode

Data

Request 00H

VMC Request Command

(Reset,Setup,Reader,Expansion,Vend)

Response Packet:

Mode

Data

Response 01H

Peripheral Response

Example: MIB -> Q3V 09 04 00 10 10 E0 0D

Q3V -> MIB 09 04 01 00 00 FF 0D.

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#begin-session-command)

Begin Session Command

When the application is ready for a transaction, it issues a begin session command to inform the VMC master. This marks the beginning of a transaction. Balance amount is 2 bytes; if balance does not exist, fill with 0xFF. This command follows MDB spec definition but is initiated by the app.

Request Packet:

Mode

Data

Request 00H

Begin Session (03H) + Funds Available + MDB Checksum

Response Packet:

Mode

Data

Response 01H

ACK 00H

Example: Q3V -> MIB 09 06 00 03 00 64 67 32 0d

MIB -> Q3V 09 03 01 00 ff 0d

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/mdb-communication-protocal#session-cancel-request-0x04)

Session Cancel Request(0x04)

The application can end a payment session by issuing a session cancel request command. The POS acts as the master during this command.

Request Packet:

Mode

Data

Request 00H

Cancel Session Req(04H) + Funds Available + Checksum

Response Packet:

Mode

Data

Response 01H

ACK 00H

Testing

# CloudPOS SDK AAR | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/cloudpos-sdk-aar#overview)

Overview

Welcome to the CloudPOS SDK AAR documentation! This guide provides information on the CloudPOS SDK AAR (Android Archive) for developers for the SmartPOS. The SDK enables seamless integration of CloudPOS functionalities into your Android application.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/cloudpos-sdk-aar#getting-started)

Getting Started

To ensure optimal performance and compatibility, it is essential to use the latest CloudPOS SDK AAR version. The table below lists recent releases, including download links and release dates:

Version

Download

Release Time

1.7.7.18

[CloudPOS SDK AARarrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/device/java/cloudpossdkV1.7.7.18_Standard.aar)

1.7.7.13

[CloudPOS SDK AARarrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/device/java/cloudpossdkV1.7.7.13_Standard.aar)

2025-12-23

1.7.7.7

[CloudPOS SDK AARarrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/device/java/cloudpossdkV1.7.7.7_Standard.aar)

2025-11-19

1.7.6.9

[CloudPOS SDK AARarrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/device/java/cloudpossdkV1.7.6.9_Standard.aar)

2025-10-21

1.7.6.6

[CloudPOS SDK AAR arrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/device/java/cloudpossdkV1.7.6.6_Standard.aar)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/cloudpos-sdk-aar#versioning)

Versioning

The CloudPOS SDK AAR version number follows the format: Major.Minor.Stage.Build. The main version is updated for architectural changes, the minor version annually, the stage version monthly, and the build version for feature additions or bug fixes.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/cloudpos-sdk/cloudpos-sdk-aar#change-history)

Change History

**1.7.7.18**

*   **Add API for switching between external and internal SIM antennas.**
    
*   **Update EMV-related so files.**
    
*   **Add interfaces for MSR swipe, SmartCard attach, RFCard attach, and the last usage time of Printer write.**
    

**1.7.7.13**

*   **Removed the libraries related to sdk\_secondarydisplaylib .**
    
*   **Modified the CustomerDisplayDevice and the corresponding JavaDoc description. The original interface would scale the image to 320\*240 size, but now the size restriction has been removed and images of any size can be passed.**
    
*   **Changed the AbstracAdvancetDevice method to protected.**
    
*   **Fix the error that does not allow the AES algorithm.**
    
*   **Add an API to stop the application.**
    
*   **Adapt HSM to RSA4096 keys.**
    
*   **Provide an interface for the customer display device to obtain the size.**
    
*   **Add an application interface to obtain the last access time of the terminal card - getDeviceLastAccessTime. The terminal's TMSAgent version should be greater than or equal to 5.4.41.**
    
*   **Add paper status detection to the print HTML interface. If an out of paper is detected during printing, return PRINT\_ERROR.**
    

**1.7.7.7**

*   **Fix the bug of isDeviceExist-customerdisplay .**
    
*   **Delete the unimplemented setAccessibilityService and getAccessibilityService methods in the ISystemDevice interface.**
    
*   **Add the method for setting a static IP for Wi-Fi.**
    
*   **Add skipRATS(), calling it before card search can avoid entering 14443-4.**
    
*   **Fix bug of waitForCardAbsent.**
    
*   **Add support for PSAM card slots 5 and 6.**
    
*   **Add Admin/user login/logout interfaces.**
    
*   **Optimize the judgment of whether MSR exists.**
    

**1.7.6.9**

*   **Added LEDGroupDevice to turn on LEDs simultaneously.**
    
*   **JavaSDK minimum Android SDK version upgraded to 23.**
    
*   **Pinpad added the updateUserKeyByX9\_143 interface.**
    
*   **Optimized contactless card type detection.**
    
*   **Fixed the issue of SDK failing to open the RJ45-to-USB serial interface.**
    
*   **Added methods to read/write raw MDB data in ExtBoardDevice.**
    

**1.7.6.6**

*   **When testing the serial port using the new SDK, open failures may occur.**
    
*   **Added functionality for setting Wi-Fi certificates.**
    
*   **Fixed a bug when calling the decreaseValue method.**
    
*   **Added ExtBoard library functionality for manipulating the DigitIO port.**
    
*   **Added a keepImageOnSleep(boolean) method to CustomerDisplayDevice.**
    
*   **Added independent control for enabling/disabling the three navigation bar buttons.**
    
*   **Set the terminal's reverse display state in the accessibility service.**
    
*   **Added interfaces for obtaining Wi-Fi MAC, Ethernet MAC, imei, and simCardSn.**
    
*   **Added an interface for setting setBatteryPercentEnabled.**
    
*   **Supported checking for the presence of a customer display.**
    
*   **Changed the serial port name from SERIAL\_VENDOR to SERIAL\_EXT2. Added a corresponding ID for external calls: ID\_SERIAL\_EXT2.**
    
*   **Add screenshot interfaces.**
    

**1.7.5.1**

*   **Add the "enableStaticIp" method to implement it.**
    
*   **Modify the implementation of the APN addByAllArgs interface.**
    
*   **Modify the implementation of the getLevel method.**
    
*   **Fix the issue where the printBitmap method in Android 14 has a slow printing speed of images.**
    
*   **Fix the issue with the SDK scanning API.**
    
*   **Add the screen-off interface "lockNow", enabling continuous work even when the screen is off.**
    

**1.7.4.16**

*   **Disabled obfuscation for the** `**sdk_pdfboxlib**` **library.**
    
*   **Added cash drawer open method for D3 devices.**
    
*   **Enabled buffer overflow protection in GCC/CLang for the SO files.**
    
*   **Integrated Java SDK for Q1K secondary display.**
    
*   **Removed SDK logs containing the 'q2p' character sequence.**
    
*   **Fix the issue where the RF card ID retrieval method sometimes returns all zeros.**
    
*   **Add API to set the text when locking the screen.**
    
*   **Add an API to set the privacy options in the lock screen settings, including whether to show or not show notifications.**
    

**1.7.4.7**

*   **New Feature:** Add screen rotation system method for Q3AU: setSystemOrientation
    
*   **New Feature:** Support Dex serial port, Port ID: SerialPortDevice.ID\_SERIAL\_VENDOR
    
*   **New Feature:** Add method to initiates the WiFi Access Point (AP)
    
*   **New Feature:** Add CashDrawer implement for D3
    
*   **Fix bug:** Print crash in D3
    
*   **Fix bug:** If the width of the picture printed by the automatic grayscale method is not a multiple of 8, a black vertical line will appear on the far right.
    

1.7.4.2

*   **Fix bug:** Added adaptation for the `isDeviceExist` method on Q2 and Q3 series devices.
    

1.7.3.9

*   **Fix bug:** `printBitmapAutoGrayscale()` is now compatible with Android 12 and later.
    
*   **Fix bug**: Optimized the code for the D3 USB printer.
    
*   **New Feature**: Added three interfaces in the SDK's PINPad module to update the transfer key and master key using the TR31 format.
    
*   **Fix bug**: Updated the EMV implementation to support Android NFC.
    

1.7.2.2

*   Add charset to ensure proper text encoding in print output.
    

1.7.1.5

*   Optimization of EMV implementation.
    
*   Fixed the default printing image effect.
    
*   Fixed issues with getModel, getManufacturer, and getModuleVersion.
    
*   Added an advanced SDK: ISystemDevice，IScannerDevice，IPINPadDevice.
    

1.6.5.0

*   Optimization of EMV implementation.
    
*   Add isPrintingDone method, now only Q2Premium supports it.
    

1.6.4.4

*   Relolved an issue, when the back button is disabled, go to print html. At the moment start converting html, click the back button, occasionally print a blank page.
    
*   Add new setLogLevel(int level) method.
    

1.6.4.2

*   Add new setGlobalGUIConfiguration() method.
    
*   Resolved an issue with the `checkIntRange()` function when invoking `selectPinblockFormat()`.
    

1.6.3.9

*   Optimization of EMV implementation.
    

1.6.3.7

*   When using the `printhtml` method, there is an occasional issue where the `onFinish` callback is triggered twice.
    
*   Optimization of EMV implementation.
    

1.6.3.6

*   Fixed heigh=0 issue in printHTML method.
    
*   Optimization of EMV implementation.
    

1.6.3.4

*   Add new calculateMac method, which support CMAC MAC algorithm(Supported model: Q3A7).
    
*   Support DUKPT AES algorithm(Suppported model: Q3 Android 7/Q2Premium).
    
*   When SDK open the printer, check the power level, and stop working when the power level is 0% .
    
*   Reduce the printing of SDK serial ports and PINPAD logs
    
*   Optimization of EMV implementation.
    
*   Fixed bug in HSM isKeyExist API.
    

1.6.3.1

*   Upgrade the Cipher algorithm used for PDF printing.
    

1.6.2.9

*   Adapt to print with the new Chengdong HD15p and HD25p models.
    
*   Fixed the issue of the entire MSR failing after a specific track failure.
    
*   Modify the comments for `SelectPinblockFormat()` and restrict the input parameters.
    

1.6.2.8

*   Fixed bug in SmartCard API: IC Card implement has not detect card when inserted PSAM Card.
    

1.6.2.7

*   Fixed bug in RFCard API: Modify the timeout from 200ms to 300ms when detecting whether a RFCard is removed
    
*   Fixed bug in SerialPort API: Return LEVEL\_3\_HALTED when cable disconnect.
    
*   Add Extended Serial Port power on/off API.
    
*   Optimization of EMV implementation.
    
*   Fixed bug in Smartcard API: Reset the isConnected status in the card removal callback.
    
*   Supports SAM 1 for Q2Premium
    

1.6.2.1

*   Optimization of EMV implementation.
    
*   Supports decryption with DUKPT 2009 Data Key.
    

1.6.1.5

*   Completely remove printStackTrace statements from the SDK.
    
*   Optimization of EMV implementation.
    
*   Added logging in the HSM JNI getrandom method to print the length of the input buffer parameter.
    
*   Enhanced RF reader Capabilities: Added methods to enables/disables low power card detection mode.
    
*   EMV Implementation Updates: The PINPad keyboard is closed when the emv\_stop\_process function is executed.
    
*   Polish javadoc.
    

1.5.4.93

*   New USB Printer Support: Introduced a new USB type specifically for USB printers, enhancing connectivity and compatibility.
    
*   Enhanced Printing Capabilities: Added a method to print PDFs or bitmaps with varying brightness levels, allowing for more flexible printing options.
    
*   Bug Fix in convertHTML2image: Resolved a bug in the convertHTML2image function. Implemented a default timeout of 30 seconds to prevent blocking within the method, enhancing reliability and performance.
    
*   EMV Implementation Updates: The EMV (Europay, MasterCard, and Visa) implementation has been updated for improved functionality and security.
    
    *   Rupay Service Parameter API: Added an API specifically for Rupay Service Parameter
        
    
*   Reboot Time Setting Method: Introduced a method to set the reboot time. This is available in the com.wizarpos.wizarviewagentassistant.aidl ISystemManagerService, which is included in the SDK and does not require separate addition.
    
*   New PINPAD Layout Support: Added support for a new PINPAD layout, which includes function buttons at the bottom of the keyboard, enhancing usability and user experience.
    

1.5.4.84

*   Fixed a bug in PrinterDevice.convertHTML2image(\*).
    
*   Fixed a bug in SmartCardReaderDevice.open(int logicalID, int cardEmvMode).
    
*   Updated EMV implementation.
    

1.5.4.80

*   Updated EMV implementation, added emv\_set\_log\_level (default is 0: no log output).
    

1.5.4.76

*   Added support for ESP mode to calculate pin block.
    
*   Added support for getting the current PIN length when using default PINPAD UI.
    

1.5.4.74

*   Added support for calculating MAC response for DUKPT.
    

1.5.4.73

*   Fixed bug for enableEmvAuthOption.
    

1.5.4.72

*   Updated EMV implementation.
    
*   Added support for PSAM card slots 0 and 2 in Q2 Android 12.
    
*   Added serial ID: ID\_USB\_GPRINTER.
    

1.5.4.66

*   Updated EMV implementation.
    
*   Added API for updating master by old master key.
    

1.5.4.60

# PINPAD | CloudPOS SDK

*   **Input PIN specification**
    

If no input is entered, it will timeout after 1 minute, and the interval for each PIN input is 10s after the input begins

*   **\-97536(0x17d00) means operation is canceled**
    

Logs are like:

`######Hooker::HOOKER_CTRL_EVENT_Cancel`

`HAL_Pinpad : Operation canceled`

*   **Encrypt specification**
    

Plain date should be multiple of 8.

*   \-76800 means break rules about data sensitivity
    

For master key/transport key, can not inject same key with the current existed key in the slot.

For user key(session key), under the protection of a master key, the injected userkey cannot be the same as the existed userkeys.

Please notice, for every bytes of the key, if only the last bit of the byte is different, that is same too.

[PreviousPrinterchevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/sdk-error-collection/printer)
[NextContactless Cardchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/sdk-error-collection/contactless-card)

Last updated 4 months ago

# Choose Your Best Practice | Paywizard Integration

**We offer three integration methods:**

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/choose-your-best-practice#id-1.-cloud-api)

**1\. Cloud API:**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FJIYYQ6HJzDNjFviWOSNR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7740ca2e-7d48-4781-836d-388c1434aefa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cf48597a&sv=2)

[playQuick Start - Cloud APIchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/quick-start-cloud-api)

The Point of Sale (POS) system and the payment terminal are connected indirectly via a cloud API, with no direct physical link or requirement for the same network segment. This enables flexible integration and secure data transmission.

**Advantages:**

1.  **Flexibility and Scalability:** Easily add or remove terminals and POS systems to accommodate business growth. Cloud-based solutions scale seamlessly, minimizing hardware upgrade needs.
    
2.  **Centralized Data Management:** Transaction data is stored centrally, simplifying report generation, sales trend analysis, and inventory management for efficient decision-making.
    
3.  **Location Independence:** Supports multi-location deployments, making it ideal for businesses with multiple branches, while maintaining a unified system without local configurations.
    
4.  **Reduced Physical Dependency:** Eliminates reliance on cables and local wiring, lowering maintenance costs and enhancing system reliability.
    

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/choose-your-best-practice#id-2.-local-integration)

**2\. Local Integration:**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FYYy4AbCIB8gQPt4u3Nkv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da90dd403-2e3f-4da8-9cbb-a8138b615cb7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e3f996aa&sv=2)

[Payment App Integration Protocolchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol)

The Point of Sale (POS) system and the payment terminal are connected directly via USB, WIFI, Bluetooth, or a wired network to initiate transactions quickly and reliably.

**Advantages:**

1.  **Faster Transaction Speeds:** Direct local connections enable quicker processing, outperforming cloud-based options in areas with unstable internet.
    
2.  **Enhanced Security:** Data is transmitted locally, reducing exposure to online threats, but requires strong security measures (e.g., encryption) to address potential local vulnerabilities.
    

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/choose-your-best-practice#id-3.-internal-integration)

**3\. Internal Integration:**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FmJUjpwQ1IYrlT0A6xbdG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a1ba764-388e-4b6a-979c-62a41fb4616f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8db113ca&sv=2)

[Payment App AIDL Integration Protocolchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/payment-app-aidl-integration-protocol)

In the payment terminal, the business application directly invokes the AIDL interface provided by the OPC to process transactions internally on the same device, eliminating the need for external connections.

**Advantages:**

1.  **Ultra-Fast Processing:** Internal calls reduce latency, enabling near-instant transaction handling without network delays.
    
2.  **Efficient Resource Use:** Leverages local device resources, minimizing overhead and optimizing battery life and performance.
    
3.  **Heightened Security:** Limits data exposure by keeping operations within the device, reducing risks associated with external data transmission.
    
4.  **Simplified Development:** Streamlines integration for developers, as AIDL facilitates easy inter-app communication without complex setups.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/choose-your-best-practice#in-summary)

**In summary:**

1.  **Local Network Connection**
    
    *   **Pros:**
        
        *   Faster transaction speeds due to direct communication, ideal for environments with unstable internet.
            
        *   Enhanced security by keeping data local, reducing exposure to external threats.
            
        
    *   **Cons:**
        
        *   Relies on stable local hardware (e.g., WIFI or Bluetooth signals), which can fail in interference-prone areas.
            
        *   Potential security vulnerabilities if local connections aren't properly encrypted or managed.
            
        
    
2.  **Internal Invocation (via AIDL)**
    
    *   **Pros:**
        
        *   Ultra-fast processing with minimal latency, as everything happens on-device.
            
        *   Efficient resource use, improving battery life and performance while maintaining high security through localized operations.
            
        *   Simplified development and integration for teams.
            
        
    *   **Cons:**
        
        *   Limited to a single device, making it inflexible for multi-device or scalable setups.
            
        *   Requires advanced technical expertise to implement and troubleshoot.
            
        
    
3.  **Cloud-Based API**
    
    *   **Pros:**
        
        *   Highly scalable and accessible, allowing remote management, real-time updates, and integration across multiple locations.
            
        *   Easier to maintain and update software centrally.
            
        
    *   **Cons:**
        
        *   Slower processing times in areas with poor internet, potentially disrupting transactions.
            
        *   Higher security risks due to data transmission over the internet, increasing exposure to breaches.
            
        
    

circle-info

**Notice:**

If you use WizarPOS ECR or self-service machine, we provide an more easy way to integrate

**Embedded Integration (WizarPOS D22/D3)** is ideal for businesses seeking a compact, all-in-one solution with a streamlined user experience.

[Accessory Agent Service D22/Q3chevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/usb-serial-port/accessory-agent-service-d22-q3)

[PreviousOverviewchevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api)
[NextIntegration & Go-Live Guidechevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [1\. Cloud API:](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/choose-your-best-practice#id-1.-cloud-api)
    
*   [2\. Local Integration:](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/choose-your-best-practice#id-2.-local-integration)
