# Integration & Go-Live Guide | Paywizard Integration

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FG27dCwgVkw4aFGjHMXId%252FIntegration%2520Roadmap.drawio.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98171b28-62e9-4e10-9b53-7cc549a86405&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8316206f&sv=2)

* * *

1

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#milestone-0-project-kick-off)

MILESTONE 0: PROJECT KICK OFF


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before writing any code, we must ensure all administrative and logistical prerequisites are met to ensure a smooth integration journey.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-1.-administrative-and-logistics)

**1\. Administrative & Logistics**

*   **In-take Form:** Complete and sign the project In-take form to register your project scope.
    
*   **Device Shipping:** We will ship the test terminals to your designated office.
    
*   **Resource Allocation:** A dedicated **Test Analyst** will be assigned to your account to guide you through the testing phases.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-2.-obtain-credentials-and-setup)

**2\. Obtain Credentials & Setup**

The preparation depends on your integration method:

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-2.1-for-cloud-api-integrators)

**2.1 For Cloud API Integrators:**

*   System will send you **3 separate emails**. Please check your inbox (including the spam folder) for the following:
    
    1.  **Developer Account**: Contains your unique **Developer ID** and **Secret**.
        
    2.  **Test Merchant Token**: The authentication token required for API calls.
        
    3.  **Portal Credentials**: Login details for the Test Merchant Portal to view sandbox transaction details.
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-2.2-for-semi-integration-integrators)

**2.2 For Semi-Integration Integrators:**

*   Once you have set up your physical test environment, you can begin testing immediately.
    
*   \* **Optional Portal Access:** If you wish to view real-time data for your test transactions, we can provision a **Test Merchant Account** for you upon request. This will allow you to log in to the dashboard and analyze your testing results.
    

> 🔗 **Refernce:** [**https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/integration-best-practices**arrow-up-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/integration-best-practices)

> ✅ **Milestone Goal:** You have the hardware, the accounts, and the contact person ready to start.

2

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#milestone-1-sandbox-integration)

MILESTONE 1: SANDBOX INTEGRATION


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With the environment ready, you enter the development phase. Your goal is to connect your system to ours and pass the standard functional tests in a risk-free environment.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-1.-setup-and-development)

**1\. Setup & Development**

*   **Connect Device:** Power on your test terminal and ensure it is connected to the internet.
    
*   **Testing APP:**
    
    *   **Paywizard Middleware:** Ensure the middleware service is running on the device.
        
    *   **Paywizard Test Payment App:** Open the simulator payment app which processes transactions **without charging real money**.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-2.-integration-and-verification)

**2\. Integration & Verification**

Perform the coding or configuration required for your integration method (Cloud API or Semi-integration).Before moving to the next phase, you must validate your integration against a complete set of test cases to ensure the **robustness** of your system:

*   **Standard Transactions:** Develop and verify all required transaction types (Sale, Void, Refund, Pre-auth).
    
*   **Exception Handling:** Simulate edge cases (e.g., Network Timeout, Card Decline) using the Test Payment App's simulation features.
    
*   **Test Case Submission:** Run the full suite of **Standard Test Cases** provided by your Test Analyst and submit the results for review.
    

circle-info

**Note:** All transactions in this phase are simulated. You can safely test edge cases (e.g., network errors) without using a real credit card.

circle-info

**Ready for Next Step?** Once your test cases are reviewed and approved by your Test Analyst, you will be cleared to move to **Milestone 2: Pre-Production Pilot**.

3

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#milestone-2-pre-production-pilot)

MILESTONE 2: PRE-PRODUCTION PILOT


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Upon completing Sandbox verification, you will migrate to the Production Environment. In this phase, you will use **real Production Parameters** and the **actual Processor Payment App** to verify the system before deploying to live merchants.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-1.-obtain-production-parameters)

**1\. Obtain Production Parameters**

Paywizard will provision a new set of credentials specifically for the live environment. Please ensure you update your system with the following:

*   **Production Developer Credentials:** A new **Developer ID** and **Secret** specific to the production environment.
    
*   **Production Portal Access:** Access to the Production Merchant Portal for viewing live transaction data.
    
*   **Production Merchant Parameters:** Configuration data linked to the **real Processor/Acquirer MID** that you provided.
    

> ⚠️ **Action Required:** Update your Machine/Terminal Application or Server-side Application to use these new production endpoints and credentials.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-2.-device-and-application-reconfiguration)

**2\. Device & Application Reconfiguration**

You must transition the physical WizarPOS terminal from "Debug Mode" to "Live Mode" by following these steps:

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-2.1-reconfigure-middleware)

**2.1 Reconfigure Middleware:**

Update the **Paywizard Middleware** settings on the device to point to the Production Environment parameters.

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-2.2-swap-payment-applications)

**2.2 Swap Payment Applications:**

*   🛑 **Uninstall:** Remove the _Paywizard Test Payment App_ (it is no longer used).
    
*   ✅ **Install:** Install the specific **Processor/Acquirer Payment App** required for your region/bank.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-2.3-apply-varsheet-configuration)

**2.3 Apply Varsheet Configuration:**

Configure the newly installed Processor Payment App using the **Production Varsheet** provided by the acquirer/processor.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-3.-production-verification-round)

**3\. Production Verification Round**

Before deploying to any real merchant store, you must perform a final "Pilot Test" using the production setup:

*   **Full Regression Test:** Repeat the full suite of test cases (all transaction types: Sale, Refund, Void, etc.) that you performed in the Sandbox.
    
*   **Exception Handling:** Re-verify common exception scenarios (e.g., user cancellation, card decline) to ensure the production app behaves as expected.
    

triangle-exclamation

**Critical:** You may only proceed to **Step 3 (Go Live)** and deploy to real merchants after **successfully passing** this full round of production testing.

4

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#milestone-3-go-live)

MILESTONE 3: GO LIVE!


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Congratulations! Having successfully passed the production pilot test, you are now ready to deploy the fully configured solution to actual merchant locations.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-1.-merchant-deployment)

**1\. Merchant Deployment**

Deploy the system to your real merchants using the **validated production configuration** from Step 2.

*   Ensure the WizarPOS terminal and your application are retaining the correct **Production MID** and **Varsheet parameters**.
    
*   No further configuration changes should be made at this stage without prior testing.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/integration-and-go-live-guide#id-2.-live-processing)

**2\. Live Processing**

You may now begin processing real transactions with actual customers.

*   **Monitoring:** We recommend closely monitoring the first batch of live transactions via the Production Portal to ensure stability.
    
*   **Support:** If any issues arise during the initial launch, please contact our support team immediately.
    

circle-check

**Launch Successful!**

Your integration is now complete. We appreciate your partnership and cooperation throughout this process.

**We wish you a prosperous business and great success!**

# PayWizard Open Platform API Signature Guide V3 | Paywizard Integration

This document details the process for generating and verifying signatures for PayWizard Open Platform API requests using version 3 of our signature scheme. This process ensures the integrity and authenticity of API requests.

API request messages are signed using a **SHA256-HMAC** algorithm with your unique **developer secret key**.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#signature-generation-steps)

Signature Generation Steps:

The general procedure for generating the `signValue` is as follows:

1

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#obtain-request-body-stringa)

**Obtain Request Body (**`**stringA**`**)**:

The raw JSON string from the request body constitutes `stringA`. Ensure no whitespace or reordering of keys is introduced if the original JSON string is obtained directly from the request.

Copy

    {
        "clientId": "client12345",
        "merchantId": "10800000003",
        "posId": "D31231234567890",
        "terminalId": "12345678",
        "terminalSn": "WP123987987897"
    }

2

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#construct-signature-string-stringsigntemp)

**Construct Signature String (**`**stringSignTemp**`**)**:

Concatenate the following string `&clientId={clientId}&clientSecret={clientSecret}` to the end of `stringA`. The resulting string is `stringSignTemp`.

Copy

    {"clientId":"client12345","merchantId":"10800000003","posId":"D31231234567890","terminalId":"12345678","terminalSn":"WP123987987897"}&clientId=client12345&clientSecret=9fb645400aabaa33ee0e423405d8c676

3

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#apply-hmac-sha256-hashing)

**Apply HMAC-SHA256 Hashing**

Perform an **HMAC-SHA256 hash calculation** on `stringSignTemp` using your designated **developer secret key**. The hexadecimal representation of the resulting hash value is the `signValue`.

circle-info

The `clientId` and `clientSecret` used in `stringSignTemp` are your unique API credentials provided by PayWizard for signature generation.

4

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#include-signature-in-request-header)

**Include Signature in Request Header**

The calculated `signValue` must be included in the request header under the parameter name `sign`.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#example-request)

Example Request:

Below is an illustrative `curl` command demonstrating a signed API request:

Copy

    curl --location --request POST 'https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openVarSheet/queryStatus' \
    --header 'jwt-token: BIKE195JVXTN7WA5DXZISQ11GPEUYI7A' \
    --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
    --header 'sign: 57ba54072ed2aaa4b2905c41e7c91fd1395ef8f6f76e6e7cdbefe7a88437de6c' \
    --data-raw '{
        "clientId": "825420368247390208",
        "pushId":"942783670425616384"
    }'

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#sample-code-for-encrypt)

Sample Code for Encrypt:

[PreviousIntegration Best Practiceschevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/integration-best-practices)
[NextPOS & Payment Terminal Binding Processchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process)

Last updated 4 months ago

*   [Signature Generation Steps:](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#signature-generation-steps)
    
*   [Obtain Request Body (stringA):](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#obtain-request-body-stringa)
    
*   [Construct Signature String (stringSignTemp):](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#construct-signature-string-stringsigntemp)
    
*   [Apply HMAC-SHA256 Hashing](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#apply-hmac-sha256-hashing)
    
*   [Include Signature in Request Header](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#include-signature-in-request-header)
    
*   [Example Request:](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#example-request)
    
*   [Sample Code for Encrypt:](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3#sample-code-for-encrypt)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    /**
    * Encrypts data using HmacSHA256.
    * @param data The string to be encrypted.
    * @param key The secret key.
    * @return java.lang.String The encrypted string in hexadecimal format.
    **/
    public static String sha256Hmac(String data, String key) {
        String cipher = "";
        try {
            byte[] byteList = key.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
            // Construct a secret key from the given byte array for a specified algorithm name,
            // in this case, generating a key specific to HmacSHA256.
            SecretKey secretKey = new SecretKeySpec(byteList, "HmacSHA256");
    
            // Get a Mac object for a specified MAC algorithm.
            Mac mac = Mac.getInstance("HmacSHA256");
            // Initialize the Mac object with the given secret key.
            mac.init(secretKey);
            byte[] text = data.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
            byte[] encryptByte = mac.doFinal(text);
            cipher = bytesToHexStr(encryptByte);
        } catch (NoSuchAlgorithmException | InvalidKeyException e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
        return cipher;
    }
    
    /**
    * Converts a byte array to a hexadecimal string.
    * @param bytes The byte array to convert.
    * @return java.lang.String The resulting hexadecimal string.
    **/
    public static String bytesToHexStr(byte[] bytes) {
        StringBuilder hexStr = new StringBuilder();
        for (byte b : bytes) {
            String hex = Integer.toHexString(b & 0xFF);
            if (hex.length() == 1) {
                hex = '0' + hex;
            }
            hexStr.append(hex);
        }
        return hexStr.toString();
    }
    
    /**
    * Generates a signature.
    * @param paramsStr The data to be sent.
    * @param clientId The developer ID.
    * @param clientSecret The developer secret key.
    * @return java.lang.String The generated signature.
    **/
    public static String generateSign(String paramsStr, String clientId, String clientSecret) {
        String str = StrUtil.format("{}&clientId={}&clientSecret={}", paramsStr, clientId, clientSecret);
        log.info("paramsStr:{}", str);
        return sha256Hmac(str, clientSecret);
    }
    
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        JSONObject params = new JSONObject();
        params.put("clientId", "825429536610058240");
        params.put("merchantId", "10800000003");
        params.put("posId", "D31231234567890");
        String str = JSON.toJSONString(params);
        System.out.println(generateSign(str, "825429536610058240", "K8VZMX99LTVHZW9IJZXE3BIIWU3QJZD2"));
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Integration Best Practices | Paywizard Integration

Welcome to the Wizarpos PayWizard Cloud API! To ensure a smooth and secure integration process, please follow these best practices when connecting your services to our platform.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/integration-best-practices#id-1.-getting-started-developer-account-application)

1\. Getting Started: Developer Account Application


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you begin the integration process, the first step is to apply for a developer account. Please contact our support team to submit your application.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/integration-best-practices#id-2.-sandbox-environment-for-development-and-testing)

2\. Sandbox Environment for Development and Testing


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once your developer account application is approved, we will provide you with credentials for our sandbox environment. This includes:

*   **An Email with Sandbox Developer Account**: This account gives you access to the testing environment.
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252F4lufiCTRueHpCvUOIGzi%252Fdev%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c835b3c-205b-41fd-9795-cc77a9d81f8c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b90805f3&sv=2)

*   **An Email with Test Merchant Parameters**: Credentials for a test merchant portal login.
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252F4q9Ko8YvLvPIQkhCrvcK%252Fmerchant%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47f114fd-535e-4a68-a74b-a79e72ca2f56&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c45ce13f&sv=2)

*   **An Email with Test Merchant API Token**: A unique token specifically for your dev id and test merchant.
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FebNflvGachHjaXUIIdwG%252Ftoken%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37da363b-c86f-4515-a46a-acab27bdc7fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c1e2e089&sv=2)

Use these credentials to develop and test your integration thoroughly. The sandbox environment is designed to mimic the functionality of the production environment without affecting live data.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/integration-best-practices#id-3.-integrating-with-the-api)

3\. Integrating with the API


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

During the integration phase, please use the provided sandbox developer account and test merchant parameters. This will allow you to test all API endpoints and webhooks to ensure your application is working correctly before going live.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/integration-best-practices#id-4.-transitioning-to-the-production-environment)

4\. Transitioning to the Production Environment


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After you have successfully completed your integration and testing in the sandbox, you will be ready to move to the production environment. For this step, you will need to:

*   Request Production Credentials: Contact us to receive your production developer account and production merchant parameters.
    
*   Replace Sandbox Credentials: It is crucial to replace all sandbox credentials in your application with the new production credentials. This includes the developer account details, merchant parameters, and the API token.
    

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/integration-best-practices#important-note-on-api-tokens)

Important Note on API Tokens:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please be aware that each merchant has its own unique API token. The token you use in the sandbox environment is for testing purposes only and will not work in the production environment. Similarly, each of your live merchants in the production environment will have a distinct token that must be used for all API requests associated with that merchant.

By following these best practices, you can ensure a successful and secure integration with our Cloud API. If you have any questions, please refer to our API documentation or contact our developer support team.

[PreviousQuick Start - Cloud APIchevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/quick-start-cloud-api)
[NextPayWizard Open Platform API Signature Guide V3chevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)

Last updated 1 month ago

The Point of Sale (POS) system and the payment terminal are connected directly via USB, WIFI, Bluetooth, or a wired network to initiate transactions quickly and reliably.

**E-Receipt**

# Close Order | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/close-order#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to close an order that has been created but has not yet been paid. This action prevents the customer from completing the payment for the specified transaction.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/close-order#environments)

Environments


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/closeOrder`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/closeOrder`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/close-order#headers)

**Headers**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guidearrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776446)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/close-order#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`checkoutId`

String

No

The unique transaction ID generated by the payment platform.

`transIndexCode`

String

No

The unique order ID that was generated by your system.

circle-exclamation

_Note: At least one of_ `_checkoutId_` _or_ `_transIndexCode_` _must be provided. If both are sent,_ `_checkoutId_` _will take precedence._

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/close-order#request-example)

**Request Example**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/close-order#response-body)

**Response Body**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response acknowledges that the request to close the transaction has been received and processed.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request. Any other value indicates an error.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message describing the result. "success" on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/close-order#success-response-example)

**Success Response Example**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Quick Start: QR Payment API Integration | Paywizard Integration

This guide provides a quick overview of integrating the QR payment APIs to enable both Merchant-Presented Mode (MPM) and Customer-Presented Mode (CPM) transactions, along with essential post-payment operations like querying, refunding, and voiding transactions.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#i.-introduction-to-qr-payments)

I. Introduction to QR Payments


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

QR code payments offer a convenient way for merchants to accept payments, primarily through two modes:

*   **Merchant-Presented Mode (MPM)**: The merchant generates and displays a QR code, which the customer scans using their mobile wallet to complete the payment.
    
*   **Customer-Presented Mode (CPM) / Quick Pay**: The customer generates a QR code on their mobile wallet app and presents it to the merchant for scanning to initiate the payment.
    

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#ii.-prerequisites)

II. Prerequisites


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you begin, ensure you have:

*   **API Client/SDK**: Install a suitable API library for your programming language (e.g., Java SDK).
    
*   **Authentication Credentials**: Obtain your `CLIENT_ID` to initialize the API client.
    

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#iii.-payment-initiation-flows)

III. Payment Initiation Flows


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#a.-merchant-presented-mode-mpm-generate-qr-code-customer-scan)

**A. Merchant Presented Mode (MPM): Generate QR Code (Customer Scan)**

This flow is suitable when the merchant displays a QR code for the customer to scan (`generate-qr-code-customer-scan`).

**Steps:**

1

**Initiate Payment Request (Server-side)**:

*   Your merchant system submits an order payment request including details like `paymentRequestId` (unique ID from merchant), `paymentAmount` (currency and value), `order` information, `productCode` (e.g., `CASHIER_PAYMENT`), `paymentNotifyUrl`, and `paymentRedirectUrl`.
    
*   Call the `generate-qr-code-customer-scan` API (or `pay` API) with these parameters.
    

2

**Receive Payment Response (Server-side)**:

The API returns a response containing the QR code data, often as a `normalUrl` or `codeValue`. This URL typically leads to a checkout page or an image of the QR code.

3

**Display QR Code (Client-side)**:

Pass the `normalUrl` or `codeValue` to your client-side application. The merchant system displays the generated QR code to the customer.

4

**Customer Scans and Pays**:

The customer uses their mobile wallet app to scan the displayed QR code and authorize the payment.

5

**Receive Payment Result Notification (Server-side)**:

Antom (or the payment service) sends an asynchronous notification (`notifyPayment`) to your specified `paymentNotifyUrl` once the payment is completed or fails. This notification contains the `paymentRequestId`, `paymentId`, `paymentAmount`, and `result` status (e.g., `SUCCESS`, `FAIL`, `PROCESSING`). You should verify the notification's signature.

6

**Display Payment Results (Client-side)**:

After the payment, the customer might be redirected to your `paymentRedirectUrl` to show transaction results. Note that client redirection alone should not be the sole basis for determining payment success.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#b.-customer-presented-mode-cpm-quick-pay-merchant-scan)

**B. Customer Presented Mode (CPM): Quick Pay (Merchant Scan)**

This flow is used when the customer presents a QR code for the merchant to scan (`quick-pay-merchant-scan`).

**Steps:**

1

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#customer-presents-qr-code)

**Customer Presents QR Code**:

The customer generates and presents a QR code (often referred to as a "payment code" or "barcode") via their mobile wallet app.

2

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#merchant-scans-qr-code)

**Merchant Scans QR Code**:

The merchant's POS system or reader scans the customer's presented QR code. This scan typically obtains a customer payment token (e.g., `authCode`).

3

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#submit-payment-request-server-side)

**Submit Payment Request (Server-side)**:

*   Your merchant system submits a payment request to the API, including the `paymentRequestId`, `paymentAmount`, `order` information, and the `authCode` obtained from scanning the customer's QR code.
    
*   Call the `quick-pay-merchant-scan` API with these details.
    

4

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#receive-payment-result-notification-server-side)

**Receive Payment Result Notification (Server-side)**:

The payment service processes the request and sends an asynchronous notification (`notifyPayment`) to your specified `paymentNotifyUrl` with the `paymentId` and ultimate transaction `result`.

5

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#confirm-payment-merchant-side)

**Confirm Payment (Merchant-side)**:

Update the order status in your system based on the notification. Confirm the payment to the customer.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#iv.-post-payment-operations)

IV. Post-Payment Operations


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#a.-query-transaction-status-query-transaction-status)

**A. Query Transaction Status (**`**query-transaction-status**`**)**

To check the status of a specific transaction:

1.  **Create Query Request (Server-side)**:
    
    *   Initiate a query request using the merchant's `paymentRequestId` or the `paymentId` received from the payment system.
        
    
2.  **Retrieve Response**:
    
    *   The response will contain the `paymentStatus` (e.g., `SUCCESS`, `FAIL`, `PROCESSING`) and other transaction details.
        
    
3.  **Best Practice**: It is recommended to perform a round-robin query at intervals (e.g., every 2 seconds) until a final status (SUCCESS/FAIL) or an asynchronous notification is received.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#b.-refund-refund)

**B. Refund (**`**refund**`**)**

To issue a refund for a successful transaction:

1.  **Initiate Refund Request**:
    
    *   Send a refund request including the `paymentId` of the original transaction, the `refundAmount`, and a `refundRequestId`.
        
    *   Call the `refund` API.
        
    
2.  **Process Refund Response**:
    
    *   Handle the response, which will indicate whether the refund was initiated successfully.
        
    *   (Optional) You can query refund progress using a refund inquiry API if the refund is not immediate.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#c.-void-void)

**C. Void (**`**void**`**)**

To cancel a pending payment or pre-authorized transaction before settlement:

1.  **Initiate Void Request**:
    
    *   Send a void request, typically using the `paymentRequestId` or `paymentId` of the transaction you wish to cancel.
        
    *   Call the `void` API.
        
    
2.  **Process Void Response**:
    
    *   The response confirms if the void operation was successful.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration#d.-close-order-close-order)

**D. Close Order (**`**close-order**`**)**

To explicitly close an order, often when a payment has timed out or is no longer expected to be completed:

1.  **Initiate Close Order Request**:
    
    *   Send a request to close the order, using the `paymentRequestId` or a similar order identifier.
        
    *   Call the `close-order` API.
        
    
2.  **Process Close Order Response**:
    
    *   The response confirms the order has been marked as closed on the payment system's side.
        
    

[PreviousClient SDK APIchevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api)

# Quick Start - Payment Parameter Push | Paywizard Integration

This API series establishes a robust and automated channel for the secure and efficient transmission of critical terminal parameters, ensuring that payment terminals are correctly configured based on data retrieved from the processor by the customer's system.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252F8tkQxM0T90opYLTM1W18%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25173cdf-47e0-4827-ab94-7de943afbd41&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e8badf2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/quick-start-payment-parameter-push#id-1.-your-system-initiates-parameter-retrieval)

1\. Your System Initiates Parameter Retrieval:

**Get Varsheet from Processor:** Your system first obtains the "varsheet" from a payment processor. **Log the parameters into the system:** Once received, these parameters are then logged and stored within your system.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/quick-start-payment-parameter-push#id-2.-paywizard-processes-and-routes-parameters)

2\. PAYwizard Processes and Routes Parameters:

**Payment Para API:** Your system utilizes a "Payment Para API" to transmit the logged parameters to the PAYwizard platform. This API acts as a dedicated channel for this purpose. **Get varsheet para and create xml:** Upon receiving the parameters via the API, PAYwizard processes them and generates an XML file containing the necessary "varsheet" information. **Push to TMS:** PAYwizard then pushes this processed XML data to the TMS (Terminal Management System).

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/quick-start-payment-parameter-push#id-3.-tms-wizarview-delivers-to-terminal)

3\. TMS (Wizarview) Delivers to Terminal:

**Push to Terminal:** The TMS (Wizarview) is responsible for pushing the parameters it received from PAYwizard directly to the target payment terminal.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/quick-start-payment-parameter-push#id-4.-payment-terminal-applies-parameters)

4\. Payment Terminal Applies Parameters:

**Get Para and Apply:** Finally, the payment terminal receives these parameters and applies them.

[PreviousAIDL Integration Best Practicechevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/aidl-integration-best-practice)
[NextTSYS Transit Parameter Pushchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/tsys-transit-parameter-push)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [1\. Your System Initiates Parameter Retrieval:](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/quick-start-payment-parameter-push#id-1.-your-system-initiates-parameter-retrieval)
    
*   [2\. PAYwizard Processes and Routes Parameters:](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/quick-start-payment-parameter-push#id-2.-paywizard-processes-and-routes-parameters)
    
*   [3\. TMS (Wizarview) Delivers to Terminal:](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/quick-start-payment-parameter-push#id-3.-tms-wizarview-delivers-to-terminal)
    
*   [4\. Payment Terminal Applies Parameters:](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/quick-start-payment-parameter-push#id-4.-payment-terminal-applies-parameters)

# Get Transaction Result | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result#overview)

Overview

1.  Third-party SAAS initiates a payment request by interacting with the Paywizard system via API.
    
2.  The Paywizard system forwards the payment transaction to the POS Terminal where it is processed.
    
3.  Once completed, the POS Terminal sends the transaction result back to Paywizard.
    
4.  Paywizard pushes the transaction result notification to the Customer's SAAS via API.
    

[webhookWebhook: Push Transaction Resultchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result)

The Customer's SAAS can query order transaction status via the API interface if didn\`t get result push.

[brackets-curlyAPI: Get Transaction Resultchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/api-get-transaction-result)

[PreviousTerminal API: Subscribe Transaction Resultschevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/terminal-api-subscribe-transaction-results)
[NextWebhook: Push Transaction Resultchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result)

Last updated 9 months ago

# E-Receipt Intro | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/e-receipt-intro#the-paywizard-system-supports-an-e-receipt-system.-after-your-payment-application-completes-a-paymen)

The Paywizard system supports an e-receipt system. After your payment application completes a payment, you can choose to upload the desensitized transaction information to the backend. The system can then automatically send receipt information to consumers via SMS or email, especially useful for terminals without receipt printers.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FZcTwFMFL0hPiFkGbnnbZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9458cbc4-64fa-486e-8688-209d4a5cceae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f1eadf40&sv=2)

# Fiserv Parameter Push | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/fiserv-parameter-push#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to upload and push Fiserv WizarPOS payment configuration parameters to a specific terminal.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/fiserv-parameter-push#environments)

Environments


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openVarSheet/fiserv/configuration/push`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openVarSheet/fiserv/configuration/push`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/fiserv-parameter-push#authentication)

Authentication


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Authentication is handled through a JSON Web Token (JWT) included in the request header. A signature must also be provided in the headers for request verification.

For detailed instructions on generating the required signature, please refer to our [Signature Generation Guidearrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776446)
.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/fiserv-parameter-push#endpoint-push-fiserv-configuration)

Endpoint: Push Fiserv Configuration

`POST /ovstrade/openVarSheet/fiserv/configuration/push`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/fiserv-parameter-push#headers)

**Headers**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

String

Yes

Yes

.

String

Configuration for modifying reversal amount.

`partialAuthCap`

String

No

Flag for partial authorization capability.

`networkAccessIndicator`

String

No

The network access indicator.

`pinlessPosDebit`

String

No

Flag for PIN-less POS debit.

`facilitator`

String

No

Flag for facilitator setting.

`alternateMerchant`

String

No

Flag for alternate merchant setting.

`refundType`

String

No

The type of refund processing.

`cashBack`

String

No

Flag to enable/disable cash back.

`cashDiscount`

String

No

Flag to enable/disable cash discounting.

`floorLimit`

String

No

The transaction floor limit.

`contactlessTranLimit`

String

No

The limit for contactless transactions.

`contactlessFloorLimit`

String

No

The floor limit for contactless transactions.

`cmvRequiredLimit`

String

No

The Cardholder Verification Method (CVM) required limit.

`forceSettle`

String

No

Flag to force settlement.

`closeOfBusinessTime`

String

No

The time for automatic end-of-day settlement.

`batchNumber`

String

No

The current batch number.

`transExpiredDays`

String

No

The number of days after which a transaction expires.

`traceNo`

String

No

The current trace number.

`receipt`

String

No

Receipt printing configuration.

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/fiserv-parameter-push#request-example)

**Request Example**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/fiserv-parameter-push#response-body)

**Response Body**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response acknowledges the request and provides the status of the configuration push.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message. `success` on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.pushId`

String

A unique ID for this configuration push operation.

`data.status`

Integer

An integer code representing the status of the push. See [Push Status Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23push-status-codes)
 below.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/fiserv-parameter-push#push-status-codes)

**Push Status Codes**

Status Code

Description

`0`

In Progress (Parameters are being pushed)

`1`

Success (Parameters were pushed successfully)

`2`

Failure (Parameter push failed)

# Quick Start - Semi Integration | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/quick-start-semi-integration#id-1.-local-integration)

1**. Local Integration:**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FYYy4AbCIB8gQPt4u3Nkv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da90dd403-2e3f-4da8-9cbb-a8138b615cb7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e3f996aa&sv=2)

[Payment App Integration Protocolchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol)

The Point of Sale (POS) system and the payment terminal are connected directly via USB, WIFI, Bluetooth, or a wired network to initiate transactions quickly and reliably.

**Advantages:**

1.  **Faster Transaction Speeds:** Direct local connections enable quicker processing, outperforming cloud-based options in areas with unstable internet.
    
2.  **Enhanced Security:** Data is transmitted locally, reducing exposure to online threats, but requires strong security measures (e.g., encryption) to address potential local vulnerabilities.
    

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/quick-start-semi-integration#id-2.-internal-integration)

**2\. Internal Integration:**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FmJUjpwQ1IYrlT0A6xbdG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a1ba764-388e-4b6a-979c-62a41fb4616f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8db113ca&sv=2)

[Payment App AIDL Integration Protocolchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/payment-app-aidl-integration-protocol)

In the payment terminal, the business application directly invokes the AIDL interface provided by the OPC to process transactions internally on the same device, eliminating the need for external connections.

**Advantages:**

1.  **Ultra-Fast Processing:** Internal calls reduce latency, enabling near-instant transaction handling without network delays.
    
2.  **Efficient Resource Use:** Leverages local device resources, minimizing overhead and optimizing battery life and performance.
    
3.  **Heightened Security:** Limits data exposure by keeping operations within the device, reducing risks associated with external data transmission.
    
4.  **Simplified Development:** Streamlines integration for developers, as AIDL facilitates easy inter-app communication without complex setups.
    

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/quick-start-semi-integration#firstheading)

Payment App Integration Details:


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sdkwiki.wizarpos.com/index.php?title=Payment\_Apparrow-up-right](https://sdkwiki.wizarpos.com/index.php?title=Payment_App)

[PreviousTerminal API : Upload Settlement Infochevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/e-receipt-intro/terminal-api-upload-settlement-info)
[NextLocal Integrationchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration)

Last updated 7 months ago

# Web Element Integration | Paywizard Integration

The PayWizard Web Element SDK provides a powerful and secure set of payment processing tools, helping developers easily integrate payment functionalities into web applications and **keep their system out of the PCI DSS scope.**

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PayWizard Web Element SDK is a secure and flexible payment integration solution that provides a seamless payment experience within your website using iframe technology. The SDK is designed to simplify the payment process while ensuring the highest level of security and compatibility.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#core-features)

Core Features

*   **Secure Payment Interface** - Isolates sensitive information via iframe
    
*   **Multiple Payment Methods** - Supports various payment options including credit cards, debit cards, etc.
    
*   **Flexible Theme Customization** - Adapts to your website's design style
    
*   **Payment Method Storage** - Simplifies payment process for returning customers
    
*   **Multi-language Support** - Provides localized experience for global users
    
*   **Responsive Design** - Offers a consistent experience across various devices
    

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#payment-flow-overview)

Payment Flow Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FkN7tzaTMGCXECzWisk3n%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba01573e-83cb-412b-9f01-8b15d8ecd42e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a8c7b03&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#installation-and-setup)

Installation and Setup


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#using-script-tag)

Using Script Tag

Add the following script to the `<head>` section of your HTML page:

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#basic-html-structure)

Basic HTML Structure

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#core-integration-steps)

Core Integration Steps


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section details the core steps for integrating the PayWizard SDK, corresponding to the interaction sequence in the Payment Flow Overview.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-1-merchant-system-creation-of-payment-order)

Step 1: Merchant System Creation of Payment Order

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FMPQm1J0t8pRlK2J4bKmc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf1f17f0-9659-4b54-9262-3f62b5e49a3b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a003b732&sv=2)

The first step in the payment process is to call PayWizard's "Create Online Payment Order" API on your server-side. The purpose of this API is to register a new payment transaction with the PayWizard system and obtain a `checkoutId`. This `checkoutId` is a crucial parameter required for subsequent client-side SDK initialization.

circle-exclamation

**Key Actions**

*   Your server sends a request to the PayWizard server, including information such as order amount, transaction type, `redirectUrl` (for synchronous result redirection), and `notifyUrl` (for asynchronous result notification).
    
*   The PayWizard server returns the `checkoutId` and other relevant information (corresponds to Flowchart Step 2).
    

For detailed API request and response format, please refer to the Create Online Payment Order API details section later in this document.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-2-client-checkout-page-sdk-initialization-and-checkout)

Step 2: Client Checkout Page SDK Initialization and Checkout

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FO8OEH8dVBWeAGPUr48pw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2de60b5-0886-4521-886a-99c054162bc8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48058fb6&sv=2)

After obtaining the `checkoutId`, you need to initialize the PayWizard SDK on the client-side (the user's browser) and create a checkout session. PayWizard will validate the access and order validity and return the result to the client.

For detailed parameters of the `PayWizard()` and `initCheckout()` methods, please refer to the Client-side SDK Method Details.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-3-client-checkout-page-session-configuration-optional)

Step 3: Client Checkout Page Session Configuration (Optional)

If your system supports user accounts and you wish to leverage PayWizard's payment method storage feature (i.e., allowing users to select saved cards for payment), you can configure session parameters in this step, such as the customer identifier (`customer`) and saved payment method identifier (`card`).

If you need to retrieve the user's saved payment methods (`cardToken`), your server-side can call the Retrieve Bank Card Information by UserId API. For detailed information, please refer to the description of the `checkout.session(options)` method.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-4-client-checkout-page-rendering-of-payment-interface)

Step 4: Client Checkout Page Rendering of Payment Interface

After configuration, call the `mount` method to render PayWizard's secure payment form (in the form of an iframe) into the specified DOM element on your page.

For detailed information, please refer to the description of the `checkout.mount(selector)` method.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-5-client-checkout-page-processing-payment-and-retrieving-synchronous-result)

Step 5: Client Checkout Page Processing Payment and Retrieving Synchronous Result

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FcQMIC9ad21N5O4Cg1tUD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a4cd7a5-b6ed-4896-97b6-89dee9ed49fc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c0bf13a&sv=2)

When the user fills in the payment information and clicks the payment button on your page, call the `confirm` method to submit the payment (corresponds to Flowchart Step 5). PayWizard processes the payment (internally interacting with the payment channel, i.e., Flowchart Steps 6 and 7), and then returns the synchronous result to the client, or redirects to the `redirectUrl` you specified when creating the order (corresponds to Flowchart Step 8).

For detailed information, please refer to the description of the `checkout.confirm()` method.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-6-merchant-system-processing-asynchronous-notification)

Step 6: Merchant System Processing Asynchronous Notification

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FJ67sBtNdW1oILSfh6qwy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda593b97-16f9-4a5f-a998-31463a81b166&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=87522d79&sv=2)

In addition to the synchronous result obtained by the client through the `confirm()` method (or received via `redirectUrl`), the PayWizard server will also send an asynchronous notification to the `notifyUrl` you provided in the "Create Online Payment Order" API. This ensures that your system reliably receives the final payment result even if the user closes the browser or the network is interrupted.

circle-exclamation

Your server-side needs to:

*   Provide a publicly accessible `notifyUrl` endpoint.
    
*   Receive the POST request sent by PayWizard (usually in JSON format, please refer to PayWizard's notification specifications for details).
    
*   Verify the signature of the received notification (see PayWizard's signature verification documentation) to ensure security.
    
*   Update the order status in your system based on the notification content (e.g., mark as payment successful, failed, etc.).
    
*   Return a successful response (e.g., HTTP 200) to the PayWizard server, indicating that the notification has been successfully received and processed.
    

This step corresponds to Step 9 in the flowchart. The `notifyUrl` is set during the Create Online Payment Order API call.

[PreviousQuick Start - Online Paymentchevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/quick-start-online-payment)
[NextClient SDK APIchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api)

*   [Core Integration Steps](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#core-integration-steps)
    
*   [Step 1: Merchant System Creation of Payment Order](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-1-merchant-system-creation-of-payment-order)
    
*   [Step 2: Client Checkout Page SDK Initialization and Checkout](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-2-client-checkout-page-sdk-initialization-and-checkout)
    
*   [Step 3: Client Checkout Page Session Configuration (Optional)](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-3-client-checkout-page-session-configuration-optional)
    
*   [Step 4: Client Checkout Page Rendering of Payment Interface](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-4-client-checkout-page-rendering-of-payment-interface)
    
*   [Step 5: Client Checkout Page Processing Payment and Retrieving Synchronous Result](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-5-client-checkout-page-processing-payment-and-retrieving-synchronous-result)
    
*   [Step 6: Merchant System Processing Asynchronous Notification](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/web-element-integration#step-6-merchant-system-processing-asynchronous-notification)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    <script src="https://cdn.paywizard.com/sdk/paywizard_0.0.2.umd.js"></script>

Copy

    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <meta charset="utf-8" />
        <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
        <title>PayWizard Integration</title>
        <script src="https://cdn.paywizard.com/sdk/paywizard_0.0.2.umd.js"></script>
      </head>
      <body>
        <!-- The payment interface will be mounted to this container -->
        <div id="checkout-container"></div>
    
        <!-- Payment Button -->
        <button id="pay-button">Complete Payment</button>
      </body>
    </html>

Copy

    // Initialize the SDK with your developer Token
    const payWizard = PayWizard("your-client-token");
    
    // Create a checkout session using the checkoutId obtained from the server
    async function initializeCheckout(checkoutIdFromServer) {
      const checkout = await payWizard.initCheckout({
        clientId: "your-client-id",
        merchantId: "your-merchant-id",
        checkoutId: checkoutIdFromServer, // **IMPORTANT**: Use the checkoutId returned from the server in the previous step
        elementsOptions: {
          appearance: {
            width: "100%", // Control iframe width
            theme: "light", // Optional: "light" or "night"
          },
        },
        savePaymentMethods: true, // Enable payment method storage feature
      });
      // Paywizard-->>Checkout Page: 4. Validate access and order validity result (This is handled internally by initCheckout)
      return checkout;
    }
    // Example call:
    const checkout = await initializeCheckout("checkout-id-from-your-server");

Copy

    // The checkout object is the instance returned from the initCheckout in the previous step
    checkout.session({
      customer: "customer-id-from-your-server", // Optional, your system's user ID
      card: "saved-card-token-from-your-server", // Optional, Token of the saved payment method
    });

Copy

    <!-- Ensure this container exists on the page -->
    <div id="checkout-container"></div>

Copy

    // The checkout object is the instance returned from the initCheckout in the previous step
    await checkout.mount("#checkout-container");

Copy

    <!-- Payment Button -->
    <button id="pay-button">Complete Payment</button>

Copy

    // The checkout object is the instance returned from the initCheckout in the previous step
    document.getElementById("pay-button").addEventListener("click", async () => {
      try {
        const result = await checkout.confirm(); // Corresponds to Flowchart Step 5
        console.log("Payment successful (synchronous result):", result); // Part of Flowchart Step 8
        // The result object contains the transaction result.
        // Handle successful payment logic based on the result, such as redirecting to a success page or displaying a success message.
    
        // Note: If redirectUrl was specified during server-side "Create Online Payment Order",
        // calling confirm may automatically redirect the page to that redirectUrl (corresponds to Flowchart Step 8).
        // In this case, the redirectUrl will include query parameters: checkoutId, result, customerId (optional), cardToken (optional).
        // You need to handle these parameters on the page pointed to by redirectUrl.
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Payment failed (synchronous result):", error);
        // Handle payment failure logic
      }
    });

# Query Transaction Status | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint allows you to query the status and details of a specific transaction using either the platform's `checkoutId` or your original `transIndexCode`.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#environments)

Environments


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/queryOrder`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/queryOrder`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#headers)

**Headers**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guide](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`checkoutId`

String

No

The unique transaction ID generated by the payment platform.

`transIndexCode`

String

No

The unique order ID that was generated by your system.

circle-exclamation

_Note: At least one of_ `_checkoutId_` _or_ `_transIndexCode_` _must be provided. If both are sent,_ `_checkoutId_` _will take precedence._

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#request-example)

**Request Example**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#response-body)

**Response Body**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response object contains the current details of the queried transaction.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request. Any other value indicates an error.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message describing the result. "success" on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error or if the order is not found.

`data.mid`

String

The merchant ID.

`data.paywizardId`

String

The unique platform ID for the transaction.

`data.checkoutId`

String

The unique transaction ID generated by the payment platform.

`data.transIndexCode`

String

The original third-party order ID from the request.

`data.state`

Integer

An integer code representing the current status of the transaction. See [Transaction Statesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23transaction-states)
 below.

`data.amount`

String

The transaction amount.

`data.tranTime`

String

The UTC timestamp of when the transaction was successfully completed. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`. Returned only on successful transactions.

**Transaction States**

The `state` field in the response data indicates the current status of the order.

State Code

Description

`1`

Not Paid

`2`

Payment/Operation Complete

`3`

Canceled

`4`

Refunded

`5`

Order Closed

`6`

Partially Refunded

`7`

Pre-authorization Complete

`8`

Pre-authorization Canceled

`9`

Partially Canceled

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#success-response-example)

**Success Response Example**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[NextRefundchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/refund)

Last updated 4 months ago

*   [Headers](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#headers)
    
*   [Request Body Parameters](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#request-body-parameters)
    
*   [Request Example](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#request-example)
    
*   [Response Body](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/query-transaction-status#response-body)

# Quick Pay - Merchant Scan | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-pay-merchant-scan#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint processes a payment using a customer-provided authorization code (often from a QR code or barcode on their device). This is typically used in a "merchant-scan" scenario where the merchant's point-of-sale system scans the customer's payment code.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-pay-merchant-scan#environments)

Environments


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/microPay`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/microPay`

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-pay-merchant-scan#headers)

**Headers**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guide](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-pay-merchant-scan#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`transIndexCode`

String

Yes

The unique order ID generated by your system.

`scanChannel`

String

Yes

The payment channel associated with the auth code. See [Scan Channelsarrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776416)
 for valid values.

`amount`

String

Yes

The total transaction amount. Example: `"10.50"`.

`authCode`

String

Yes

The authorization code scanned from the customer's device.

`tranCurrency`

String

Yes

The 3-letter ISO currency code for the transaction. Example: `"USD"`.

`productDesc`

String

No

A brief description of the product(s) or service(s).

`payerType`

String

Conditionally Required

The type of payer identifier. Valid values: `MSISDN`, `EMAIL`, `PARTY_CODE`. Required when `scanChannel` is `MOMO`.

`notifyUrl`

String

No

The callback URL where you will receive the final transaction result notification.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-pay-merchant-scan#request-example)

**Request Example**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-pay-merchant-scan#response-body)

**Response Body**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response object contains the status of the request and the transaction details.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request. Any other value indicates an error.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message describing the result. "success" on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.mid`

String

The merchant ID.

`data.paywizardId`

String

The unique platform ID for the transaction.

`data.checkoutId`

String

The unique transaction ID generated by the payment platform.

`data.transIndexCode`

String

The original third-party order ID from the request.

`data.result`

Integer

The status of the transaction. <br> `0`: Success <br> `1`: Failure <br> `2`: Pending

`data.amount`

String

The transaction amount.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-pay-merchant-scan#success-response-example)
