# Generate QR Code - Customer Scan | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/generate-qr-code-customer-scan#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint allows you to generate a QR code for a "customer-scan" payment scenario. The customer scans the generated QR code with their device to complete the payment.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/generate-qr-code-customer-scan#environments)

Environments


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/generateQrCode`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/generateQrCode`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/generate-qr-code-customer-scan#headers)

**Headers**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guide](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/generate-qr-code-customer-scan#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`transIndexCode`

String

Yes

The unique order ID generated by your system.

`payChannel`

String

Yes

The payment channel to be used. See [Payment Channelsarrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776416)
 for valid values.

`amount`

String

Yes

The total transaction amount. Example: `"10.50"`.

`currency`

String

Yes

The 3-letter ISO currency code for the transaction amount. For PIX transactions, this must be `BRL`.

`exchangeCurrency`

String

Conditionally Required

The currency code for settlement. Valid values: `BRL`, `USD`, `EUR`. Required for PIX transactions. Currently only `BRL` is supported.

`documentNumber`

String

Conditionally Required

The customer's tax identification number (e.g., CPF or CNPJ). Required for PIX transactions.

`socialName`

String

Conditionally Required

The full name of the customer. Required for PIX transactions.

`dynamicPixExpiresAt`

String

No

The expiration timestamp for a dynamic PIX QR code in ISO 8601 format: `YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm:ssZ`.

`productDesc`

String

No

A brief description of the product(s) or service(s).

`notifyUrl`

String

No

The callback URL where you will receive the transaction result notification.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/generate-qr-code-customer-scan#request-example)

**Request Example**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/generate-qr-code-customer-scan#response-body)

**Response Body**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response object contains the status of the request and, upon success, the data needed to display the payment QR code.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates success. Any other value indicates an error.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message describing the result. "success" on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.mid`

String

The merchant ID.

`data.paywizardId`

String

The unique platform ID for the transaction.

`data.checkoutId`

String

The unique transaction ID generated by the payment platform.

`data.transIndexCode`

String

The original third-party order ID from the request.

`data.qrCode`

String

The raw data string for the payment QR code. This should be used to generate the QR code image.

`data.amount`

String

The transaction amount.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/generate-qr-code-customer-scan#success-response-example)

# TSYS Transit Parameter Push | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/tsys-transit-parameter-push#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to upload and push TSYS Trasit payment configuration parameters to a specific terminal.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/tsys-transit-parameter-push#environments)

Environments


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openVarSheet/tsystrasit/configuration/push`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openVarSheet/tsystrasit/configuration/push`

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/tsys-transit-parameter-push#authentication)

Authentication

Authentication is handled through a JSON Web Token (JWT) included in the request header. A signature must also be provided in the headers for request verification.

For detailed instructions on generating the required signature, please refer to our [Signature Generation Guidearrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776446)
.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/tsys-transit-parameter-push#endpoint-push-tsys-trasit-configuration)

Endpoint: Push TSYS Trasit Configuration

`POST /ovstrade/openVarSheet/tsystrasit/configuration/push`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/tsys-transit-parameter-push#headers)

**Headers**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guidearrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776446)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/tsys-transit-parameter-push#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/tsys-transit-parameter-push#root-parameters)

**Request Example**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_Note: The_ `_paymentAppParams_` _object is extensive. This example shows the complete structure._

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/tsys-transit-parameter-push#response-body)

**Response Body**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response acknowledges the request and provides the status of the configuration push.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message. `success` on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.pushId`

String

A unique ID for this configuration push operation.

`data.status`

Integer

An integer code representing the status of the push. See [Push Status Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23push-status-codes)
 below.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/payment-parameter-varsheet-api/tsys-transit-parameter-push#push-status-codes)

**Push Status Codes**

Status Code

Description

`0`

In Progress (Parameters are being pushed)

`1`

Success (Parameters were pushed successfully)

`2`

Failure (Parameter push failed)

# VOID | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to reverse (or void) a transaction. A reversal is typically used to cancel a transaction on the same day it was made, before the funds have settled.

circle-exclamation

Note: Partial reversals are not supported by all payment channels.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#environments)

Environments


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/reversalOrder`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/reversalOrder`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#headers)

**Headers**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guidearrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776446)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To identify the transaction to be reversed, you must provide either the `oriCheckoutId` or the `oriTransIndexCode`.

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`transIndexCode`

String

Yes

A new, unique order ID for this specific reversal request, generated by your system.

`oriCheckoutId`

String

Conditionally Required

The original `checkoutId` of the transaction you want to reverse.

`oriTransIndexCode`

String

Conditionally Required

The original `transIndexCode` of the transaction you want to reverse.

`amount`

String

Yes

The amount to be reversed. Example: `"1.50"`.

`notifyUrl`

String

No

The callback URL where you will receive the final reversal result notification.

circle-exclamation

_Note: You must provide at least one of the original identifiers (_`_oriCheckoutId_` _or_ `_oriTransIndexCode_`_). If both are sent,_ `_oriCheckoutId_` _will take precedence._

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#request-example)

**Request Example**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#response-body)

**Response Body**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response object contains the immediate status of the reversal request.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request. Any other value indicates an error.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message describing the result. "success" on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.mid`

String

The merchant ID.

`data.paywizardId`

String

The unique platform ID for the transaction.

`data.checkoutId`

String

The new, unique transaction ID for this reversal, generated by the payment platform.

`data.transIndexCode`

String

The unique reversal order ID that you provided in the request.

`data.result`

Integer

An integer code representing the status of the reversal. See [Reversal Status Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23reversal-status-codes)
 below.

`data.amount`

String

The reversed amount.

`data.oriCheckoutId`

String

The `checkoutId` of the original transaction that was reversed.

`data.oriTransIndexCode`

String

The `transIndexCode` of the original transaction that was reversed.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#reversal-status-codes)

**Reversal Status Codes**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `result` field indicates the immediate outcome of the reversal request. The final status may be delivered via the `notifyUrl`.

Result Code

Description

`0`

Success

`1`

Failure

`2`

Pending / In Progress

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#success-response-example)

**Success Response Example**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[PreviousRefundchevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/refund)
[NextClose Orderchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/close-order)

Last updated 4 months ago

*   [Environments](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#environments)
    
*   [Headers](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#headers)
    
*   [Request Body Parameters](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#request-body-parameters)
    
*   [Request Example](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#request-example)
    
*   [Response Body](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#response-body)
    
*   [Reversal Status Codes](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void#reversal-status-codes)

# Redeem Points | Paywizard Integration

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/redeem-points#overview)

Overview

This endpoint is used to redeem (or consume) loyalty points from a customer's prepaid card. This is the counterpart to the "Add Points" operation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/redeem-points#environments)

Environments

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/loyaltyRedemption`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/loyaltyRedemption`

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/redeem-points#authentication)

Authentication

Authentication is handled through a JSON Web Token (JWT) included in the request header. A signature must also be provided in the headers for request verification.

For detailed instructions on generating the required signature, please refer to our [Signature Generation Guidearrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776446)
.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/redeem-points#endpoint-redeem-loyalty-points)

Endpoint: Redeem Loyalty Points

`POST /ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/loyaltyRedemption`

**Headers**

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guidearrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776446)
.

**Request Body Parameters**

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`tranOrderNo`

String

Yes

The unique order ID for this points redemption transaction, generated by your system.

`loyaltyChannel`

String

Yes

The prepaid channel provider. See [Prepaid Channelsarrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776425)
 for valid values.

`accountId`

String

Yes

The unique identifier for the prepaid card.

`entryType`

String

Yes

The method used to input the `accountId`. See [Entry Type Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23entry-type-codes)
 below.

`amount`

String

Yes

The number of loyalty points to redeem from the card.

**Entry Type Codes**

Code

Description

`B`

Barcode

`K`

Keyed (manually entered)

`M`

Magnetic Stripe

`P`

Proximity (NFC/Contactless)

**Request Example**

JSON

* * *

**Response Body**

The response object contains the status of the points redemption transaction.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message. `success` on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.mid`

String

The merchant ID.

`data.paywizardId`

String

The unique platform ID for the transaction.

`data.checkoutId`

String

The unique transaction ID generated by the payment platform.

`data.transIndexCode`

String

A unique transaction reference code.

`data.amount`

String

The number of points that were redeemed.

`data.result`

Integer

An integer code representing the status of the transaction. See [Transaction Status Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23transaction-status-codes)
 below.

**Transaction Status Codes**

The `result` field indicates the immediate outcome of the points redemption request.

Result Code

Description

`0`

Success

`1`

Failure

`2`

Pending / In Progress

**Success Response Example**

JSON

# Add Tip | Paywizard Integration

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/add-tip#overview)

Overview

This endpoint is used to add a tip to a previously completed prepaid card transaction. This is often used in restaurant or service environments where the tip amount is determined after the initial payment is made.

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/add-tip#environments)

Environments

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftTip`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftTip`

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/add-tip#authentication)

Authentication

Authentication is handled through a JSON Web Token (JWT) included in the request header. A signature must also be provided in the headers for request verification.

For detailed instructions on generating the required signature, please refer to our [Signature Generation Guidearrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776446)
.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/add-tip#endpoint-add-tip-to-prepaid-transaction)

Endpoint: Add Tip to Prepaid Transaction

`POST /ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftTip`

**Headers**

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guidearrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776446)
.

**Request Body Parameters**

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`tranOrderNo`

String

Yes

A new, unique order ID for this specific tip transaction, generated by your system.

`oriOrderNo`

String

Yes

The `checkoutId` of the original payment transaction to which the tip is being added.

`tranCurrency`

String

Yes

The 3-letter ISO currency code for the tip amount. Example: `"USD"`.

`amount`

String

Yes

The tip amount to be added.

`accountId`

String

Yes

The unique identifier for the prepaid card used in the original transaction.

`entryType`

String

Yes

The method used to input the `accountId`. See [Entry Type Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23entry-type-codes)
 below.

**Entry Type Codes**

Code

Description

`B`

Barcode

`K`

Keyed (manually entered)

`M`

Magnetic Stripe

`P`

Proximity (NFC/Contactless)

**Request Example**

JSON

* * *

**Response Body**

The response object contains the status of the tip adjustment transaction.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message. `success` on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.mid`

String

The merchant ID.

`data.paywizardId`

String

The unique platform ID for the transaction.

`data.checkoutId`

String

The new, unique transaction ID for this tip adjustment, generated by the payment platform.

`data.transIndexCode`

String

A unique transaction reference code.

`data.amount`

String

The tip amount that was processed.

`data.result`

Integer

An integer code representing the status of the transaction. See [Transaction Status Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23transaction-status-codes)
 below.

**Transaction Status Codes**

The `result` field indicates the immediate outcome of the tip adjustment request.

Result Code

Description

`0`

Success

`1`

Failure

`2`

Pending / In Progress

**Success Response Example**

JSON

# Void | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/void#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to void a prior prepaid card transaction, such as a payment or a reload. A void typically cancels a transaction before it has been settled, effectively reversing the original operation.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/void#environments)

Environments


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftVoid`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftVoid`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/void#headers)

**Headers**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guide](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/void#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`tranOrderNo`

String

Yes

A new, unique order ID for this specific void request, generated by your system.

`oriOrderNo`

String

Yes

The `checkoutId` of the original prepaid transaction you want to void.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/void#request-example)

**Request Example**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

**Response Body**

The response object contains the status of the void transaction request.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message. `success` on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.mid`

String

The merchant ID.

`data.paywizardId`

String

The unique platform ID for the transaction.

`data.checkoutId`

String

The new, unique transaction ID for this void, generated by the payment platform.

`data.transIndexCode`

String

The unique void order ID that you provided in the request.

`data.oriCheckoutId`

String

The `checkoutId` of the original transaction that was voided.

`data.oriTransIndexCode`

String

The `transIndexCode` of the original transaction that was voided.

 below.

**Transaction Status Codes**

`1`

Failure

Pending / In Progress

# Refund | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/refund#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to issue a full or partial refund for a previously completed transaction.

Note: Partial refunds are not supported by all payment channels. Please check the documentation for your specific channel.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/refund#environments)

Environments


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/refundOrder`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openPay/refundOrder`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/refund#headers)

**Headers**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guide](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/refund#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To identify the transaction to be refunded, you must provide either the `oriCheckoutId` or the `oriTransIndexCode`.

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`transIndexCode`

String

Yes

A new, unique order ID for this specific refund request, generated by your system.

`oriCheckoutId`

String

Conditionally Required

The original `checkoutId` of the transaction you want to refund.

`oriTransIndexCode`

String

Conditionally Required

The original `transIndexCode` of the transaction you want to refund.

`amount`

String

Yes

The amount to be refunded. Example: `"1.50"`.

`notifyUrl`

String

No

The callback URL where you will receive the final refund result notification.

circle-exclamation

_Note: You must provide at least one of the original identifiers (_`_oriCheckoutId_` _or_ `_oriTransIndexCode_`_). If both are sent,_ `_oriCheckoutId_` _will take precedence._

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/refund#request-example)

**Request Example**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

**Response Body**

The response object contains the immediate status of the refund request.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request. Any other value indicates an error.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message describing the result. "success" on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.mid`

String

The merchant ID.

`data.paywizardId`

String

The unique platform ID for the transaction.

`data.checkoutId`

String

The new, unique transaction ID for this refund, generated by the payment platform.

`data.transIndexCode`

String

The unique refund order ID that you provided in the request.

`data.result`

Integer

An integer code representing the status of the refund. See [Refund Status Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23refund-status-codes)
 below.

`data.amount`

String

The refunded amount.

`data.oriCheckoutId`

String

The `checkoutId` of the original transaction that was refunded.

`data.oriTransIndexCode`

String

The `transIndexCode` of the original transaction that was refunded.

**Refund Status Codes**

The `result` field indicates the immediate outcome of the refund request. The final status may be delivered via the `notifyUrl`.

Result Code

Description

`0`

Success

`1`

Failure

`2`

Pending / In Progress

**Success Response Example**

JSON

[NextVOIDchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/void)

# Query | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/query#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to query the current balance and associated customer information for a specific prepaid (loyalty/gift) card.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/query#environments)

Environments


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftInquiry`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftInquiry`

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/query#headers)

**Headers**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guide](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/query#request-body-parameters)

Type

Required

Description

String

Yes

Yes

 for valid values.

`accountId`

String

Yes

The unique identifier for the prepaid card.

String

Yes

The method used to input the `accountId`. See [Entry Type Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23entry-type-codes)
 below.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/query#entry-type-codes)

**Entry Type Codes**

Code

Description

`B`

Barcode

`K`

Keyed (manually entered)

`M`

Magnetic Stripe

`P`

Proximity (NFC/Contactless)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/query#request-example)

**Request Example**

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/query#response-body)

**Response Body**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response returns the card's current balance information and any associated customer data.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message. `success` on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.accountId`

String

The unique identifier for the prepaid card.

`data.balances`

Array

An array of [Balances Objectarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23balances-object)
 detailing the card's value.

`data.customerInfo`

Object

The [CustomerInfo Objectarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23customerinfo-object)
 associated with the card.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/query#customerinfo-object)

**CustomerInfo Object**

Parameter

Type

Description

`customerType`

String

`1`: Primary account holder, `2`: Alternate, `3`: Giver of card.

`firstName`

String

Customer's first name.

`middleName`

String

Customer's middle name.

`lastName`

String

Customer's last name.

`address1`

String

Primary address line.

`address2`

String

Secondary address line.

`city`

String

City name.

`state`

String

State or province.

`postal`

String

Postal code.

`country`

String

2-character ISO 3166-1 country code.

`mailPref`

String

Mail preference. `O`: Opt-out, `I`: Opt-in.

`phone`

String

Phone number in the format `+CCC AAA LLL LLL xEEEE`.

`isMobile`

String

`Y`: Yes, `N`: No.

`phonePref`

String

Phone contact preference. `O`: Opt-out, `I`: Opt-in.

`email`

String

Customer's email address.

`emailPref`

String

Email contact preference. `O`: Opt-out, `I`: Opt-in.

`birthday`

String

Customer's birthday in `YYYYMMDD` format.

`anniversary`

String

Customer's anniversary in `YYYYMMDD` format.

`gender`

String

`M`: Male, `F`: Female.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/query#balances-object)

**Balances Object**

This object represents a single type of value held on the card, such as currency or points.

Parameter

Type

Description

`valueCode`

String

The currency code (e.g., "USD") or "Points".

`amount`

Decimal

The total amount of the specified `valueCode`.

`difference`

Decimal

The difference in amount from the previous transaction.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/query#success-response-example)

**Success Response Example**

# Quick Start - Loyalty API | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/quick-start-loyalty-api#factor4-loyalty-api-quick-start)

Factor4 Loyalty API Quick Start


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to the Factor4 Loyalty API Quick Start Guide! This document provides a rapid introduction to integrating prepaid (loyalty/gift) card management functionalities into your application. The Factor4 Loyalty API allows you to programmatically activate, query, top-up, process payments, and manage loyalty points for customer cards.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/quick-start-loyalty-api#id-1.-api-series-overview)

1\. API Series Overview

The Factor4 Loyalty API is designed to offer comprehensive management of gift and loyalty cards. It enables merchants and developers to perform essential operations related to prepaid cards, including card activation, balance inquiries, funds top-ups, processing payments using gift cards, and managing loyalty point issuance and redemption. All API requests are processed via HTTPS POST and require a JSON Web Token (JWT) in the request header, along with a signature for robust authentication and request verification.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/quick-start-loyalty-api#id-2.-key-features-and-endpoints)

2\. Key Features & Endpoints

The Factor4 Loyalty API provides various functionalities to manage prepaid (loyalty/gift) cards, primarily through the following API endpoints:

*   **Activate Gift Card**: Used to activate a prepaid card and link it to customer information.
    
    *   (Specific URL not provided in all references, but general capability is listed).
        
    
*   **Query Gift Card**: Used to retrieve the current balance and associated customer details for a specific prepaid card.
    
    *   `POST /ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftInquiry`
        
    
*   **Top-up Gift Card**: Allows adding funds (reloading/topping-up) to an existing prepaid card. This operation can also optionally activate the card or update customer information.
    
    *   (Specific URL for Top-up, sometimes referred to as `giftIssuance`, is implied but not explicitly provided for the "Top-up" name across all references).
        
    
*   **Pay Gift Card**: Used to process payments by using the available balance on a customer's prepaid (loyalty/gift) card.
    
    *   (Specific URL not provided in all references, but general capability is listed).
        
    
*   **Void Gift Card**: This endpoint is used to void a prior prepaid card transaction, such as a payment or a reload. A void typically reverses the original operation before it has been settled.
    
    *   `POST /ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftVoid`
        
    
*   **Issue Points - Gift Card**: This endpoint is used to issue loyalty points to a customer's prepaid card. This specifically adds points, not monetary value.
    
    *   `POST /ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/loyaltyIssuance`
        
    
*   **Redeem Points - Gift Card**: Utilized to consume or redeem loyalty points from a customer's prepaid card, serving as the inverse of the "Issue Points" operation.
    
    *   `POST /ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/loyaltyRedemption`
        
    
*   **Add Tip - Gift Card**: For adding a tip to a prepaid card transaction that has already been completed, common in service industries.
    
    *   `POST /ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftTip`
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/quick-start-loyalty-api#id-3.-authentication-and-security)

3\. Authentication & Security

All requests to the Factor4 Loyalty API must be secured using a JSON Web Token (JWT) and a signature.

*   **Protocol**: HTTPS
    
*   **HTTP Method**: POST
    
*   **Required Headers**:
    
    *   `Content-Type`: Must be `application/json`.
        
    *   `jwt-token`: Your transaction token, obtained using your developer credentials.
        
    *   `sign`: The request signature. Refer to the Signature Generation Guide for detailed instructions on generating this signature.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/quick-start-loyalty-api#id-4.-environments)

4\. Environments

Factor4 Loyalty API provides a `Sandbox` environment for development and testing purposes.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/quick-start-loyalty-api#id-5.-getting-started-steps)

5\. Getting Started Steps

To begin utilizing the Factor4 Loyalty API, follow these fundamental steps:

1.  **Obtain Developer Credentials**: Secure your `clientId` and any other credentials necessary for generating your `jwt-token` and `sign`.
    
2.  **Generate JWT Token**: Create a valid JWT token using your developer credentials.
    
3.  **Generate Request Signature**: Follow the specific instructions in the Signature Generation Guide to produce the required request signature.
    
4.  **Construct Request Body**: Assemble the JSON formatted request body for your chosen API endpoint, including parameters like `clientId`, `loyaltyChannel`, `accountId`, `tranOrderNo`, and others as required.
    
5.  **Send POST Request**: Transmit your POST request, complete with the correct headers and request body, to the relevant API endpoint in the Sandbox environment.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/quick-start-loyalty-api#id-6.-common-request-parameters)

6\. Common Request Parameters

Below are some frequently used parameters found in the Loyalty API request bodies:

*   `clientId` (String, Required): Your unique developer ID.
    
*   `tranOrderNo` (String, Required): A unique order ID generated by your system for the specific transaction (e.g., for points issuance, redemption, top-up, void, tip).
    
*   `loyaltyChannel` (String, Required): The designated prepaid channel provider.
    
*   `accountId` (String, Required): The unique identifier for the prepaid card.
    
*   `entryType` (String, Required): Specifies the method used to input the `accountId`. Valid codes include: `B` (Barcode), `K` (Keyed/Manual), `M` (Magnetic Stripe), `P` (Proximity/NFC/Contactless).
    
*   `oriOrderNo` (String, Required): The `checkoutId` of the original transaction you want to void (for `giftVoid`) or the original payment transaction ID for adding a tip (for `giftTip`).
    
*   `tranCurrency` (String, Required): The 3-letter ISO currency code for the transaction, e.g., "USD" (used for adding tips).
    
*   `amount` (String): The total transaction amount, e.g., "10.50" (used for top-up, void, tips).

# Activate | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/activate#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to activate a prepaid (loyalty/gift) card and associate it with customer information.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/activate#environments)

Environments


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftActivate`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftActivate`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/activate#headers)

**Headers**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guide](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/activate#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`loyaltyChannel`

String

Yes

The prepaid channel provider. See [Prepaid Channelsarrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776425)
 for valid values.

`accountId`

String

Yes

The unique identifier for the prepaid card.

`entryType`

String

Yes

 below.

`activating`

String

Yes

Set to `"Y"` to activate the card or `"N"` to not activate.

`customerInfo`

Object

Yes

A JSON object containing the customer's details. See [CustomerInfo Objectarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23customerinfo-object)
 structure below.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/activate#customerinfo-object)

**CustomerInfo Object**

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`customerType`

String

Yes

`1`: Primary account holder, `2`: Alternate, `3`: Giver of card.

`firstName`

String

Yes

Customer's first name.

`middleName`

String

Yes

Customer's middle name.

`lastName`

String

Yes

Customer's last name.

`address1`

String

Yes

Primary address line.

`address2`

String

Yes

Secondary address line.

`city`

String

Yes

City name.

`state`

String

Yes

State or province.

`postal`

String

Yes

Postal code (must be a valid format for the country).

`country`

String

Yes

2-character ISO 3166-1 country code.

`mailPref`

String

Yes

Mail preference. `O`: Opt-out, `I`: Opt-in.

`phone`

String

Yes

Phone number in the format `+CCC AAA LLL LLL xEEEE`.

`isMobile`

String

Yes

`Y`: Yes, `N`: No.

`phonePref`

String

Yes

Phone contact preference. `O`: Opt-out, `I`: Opt-in.

`email`

String

Yes

Customer's email address.

`emailPref`

String

Yes

Email contact preference. `O`: Opt-out, `I`: Opt-in.

`birthday`

String

Yes

Customer's birthday in `YYYYMMDD` format.

`anniversary`

String

Yes

Customer's anniversary in `YYYYMMDD` format.

`gender`

String

Yes

`M`: Male, `F`: Female.

**Request Example**

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/activate#response-body)

**Response Body**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response returns the card's balance information and confirms the customer data that has been stored.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message. `success` on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.accountId`

String

The unique identifier for the prepaid card.

`data.balances`

Array

An array of [Balances Objectarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23balances-object)
 detailing the card's value.

`data.customerInfo`

Object

The [CustomerInfo Objectarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23customerinfo-object)
 that was saved.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/activate#balances-object)

**Balances Object**

This object represents a single type of value held on the card, such as currency or points.

Parameter

Type

Description

`valueCode`

String

The currency code (e.g., "USD") or "Points".

`amount`

Decimal

The total amount of the specified `valueCode`.

`difference`

Decimal

The difference in amount from the previous transaction.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/activate#success-response-example)

# Top-up | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/top-up#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to add funds (reload/top-up) to an existing prepaid card. You can also optionally activate the card or update the associated customer information within the same request.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/top-up#environments)

Environments


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftIssuance`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftIssuance`

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/top-up#headers)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

String

Yes

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guide](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)
.

**Request Example**

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/top-up#response-body)

**Response Body**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response object contains the status of the reload transaction request.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message. `success` on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.mid`

String

The merchant ID.

`data.paywizardId`

String

The unique platform ID for the transaction.

`data.checkoutId`

String

The unique transaction ID generated by the payment platform.

`data.transIndexCode`

String

A unique transaction reference code.

`data.amount`

String

The transaction amount that was reloaded.

`data.result`

Integer

An integer code representing the status of the transaction. See [Transaction Status Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23transaction-status-codes)
 below.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/top-up#transaction-status-codes)

**Transaction Status Codes**

The `result` field indicates the immediate outcome of the reload request.

Result Code

Description

`0`

Success

`1`

Failure

`2`

Pending / In Progress

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/top-up#success-response-example)

        "timestamp": "2025-07-24 15:52:21",

            "mid": "202507081058",
            "paywizardId": "10020000080",
            "checkoutId": "933434611567034368",
            "transIndexCode": "100200000809631006007",
            "amount": "10000",
            "result": 0
        }
    }

# Issue Points | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/issue-points#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to issue loyalty points to a customer's prepaid card. This operation is for adding points, not for reloading monetary value.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/issue-points#environments)

Environments


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/loyaltyIssuance`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/loyaltyIssuance`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/issue-points#headers)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guide](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)
.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`tranOrderNo`

String

Yes

`loyaltyChannel`

Yes

 for valid values.

Yes

**Response Body**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response object contains the status of the points issuance transaction.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message. `success` on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data. Null on error.

`data.mid`

String

The merchant ID.

`data.paywizardId`

String

The unique platform ID for the transaction.

`data.checkoutId`

String

The unique transaction ID generated by the payment platform.

`data.transIndexCode`

String

A unique transaction reference code.

`data.amount`

String

The number of points that were issued.

`data.result`

Integer

An integer code representing the status of the transaction. See [Transaction Status Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23transaction-status-codes)
 below.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/issue-points#transaction-status-codes)

**Transaction Status Codes**

The `result` field indicates the immediate outcome of the points issuance request.

Result Code

Description

`0`

Success

`1`

Failure

`2`

Pending / In Progress

# Pay | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/pay#overview)

Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint is used to process a payment using the available balance on a customer's prepaid (loyalty/gift) card.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/pay#environments)

Environments


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment

Protocol

HTTP Method

URL

Sandbox

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftTransaction`

Production

HTTPS

`POST`

`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftTransaction`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/pay#headers)

**Headers**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Key

Type

Required

Description

`Content-Type`

String

Yes

Must be `application/json`.

`jwt-token`

String

Yes

The transaction token obtained using your developer credentials.

`sign`

String

Yes

The request signature. See [Signature Generation Guide](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)
.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/pay#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`tranOrderNo`

String

Yes

The unique order ID for this payment transaction, generated by your system.

`loyaltyChannel`

String

Yes

The prepaid channel provider. See [Prepaid Channelsarrow-up-right](https://oversea.hs1c.cn/showdoc/web/#/671575440/155776425)
 for valid values.

`amount`

String

Yes

The total transaction amount. Example: `"10.50"`.

`tranCurrency`

String

Yes

The 3-letter ISO currency code for the transaction. Example: `"USD"`.

`accountId`

String

Yes

The unique identifier for the prepaid card.

`entryType`

String

Yes

The method used to input the `accountId`. See [Entry Type Codesarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23entry-type-codes)
 below.

`nsfAllowed`

Boolean

No

Non-Sufficient Funds Allowed. Set to `true` to permit the transaction to proceed even if the card balance is insufficient to cover the full amount.

# Payment App Integration Protocol | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#id-1.-introduction)

1\. Introduction

This document descripts data exchange protocol between Cashier and WIZARPOS terminal. The Cashier is caller to perform transactions and Terminal will listen to Cashier and execute financial transaction.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#id-2.-transaction-flow)

2\. Transaction Flow

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2631785516-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%252Fuploads%252FOEuu2rTDOIjwhq3BNLft%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26ce8b2&sv=2)

1.  **Cashier shall send Handshake Request at first to confirm connection is ready.**
    
2.  **After Handshake, Cashier shall perform transaction and send Transaction Request which contains payment data.**
    
3.  **POS execute transaction and response the result.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#id-3.-communication-configuration)

3\. Communication Configuration

Serial port

Default Baud Rate: 115200

TCP server

Default port：6031

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#id-4.-data-format)

4\. Data Format

Data package between Cashier and Terminal.

STX

VERSION

CTRL

LEN

CONTENT

ETX

BCC

**0x02**

**0x02**

**(4 bytes)**

**(2 bytes)**

**(LEN bytes)**

**0x03**

**(1 byte)**

**STX** indicate start byte of data package.

**VERSION** indicate protocol version.

**CTRL** indicate control bytes of data package.

**LEN** indicate length bytes of CONTENT. Hex format.

**CONTENT** indicate main content of transaction.

**ETX** indicate end byte, Fixed **0x03**.

**BCC** indicate package check value, from VERSION (contain) to ETX (contain).

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#id-5.-handshake-request-content)

5\. Handshake Request Content

CONTENT

(4 bytes)

**Handshake request content is 4 bytes random value.**

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#id-6.-handshake-response-content)

6\. Handshake Response Content

CONTENT

(4 bytes)

**Handshake response content should be same with the request.**

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#id-7.-transaction-request-content)

7\. Transaction Request Content

**Transaction Request is content is json format as below:**

NAME

FORMAT

MANDATORY

DESCRIPTION

**TransType**

String

check

Indicate transaction type to be performed.

[See A1.1 Transaction Type](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#a1.1_transaction_type)

**TransScheme**

String

Cooperation with TransType，used in specific schemes

[See A1.2 Transaction Scheme](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#a1.2_transaction_type)

**CallerName**

String

Caller name

**TransIndexCode**

String

Indicate Cashier trace number

Should be unique for every transaction

**BusinessNum**

String

Business registration number

**TerminalNum**

String

Terminal number

**TransAmount**

String

\[Mandatory for payment\]

check

Total amount including OtherAmount and TipAmount

“112233” means 1122.33(USD) or 112.233(JOD) depending on CurrencyCode

**OtherAmount**

String

Cash back amount

**TipAmount**

String

Tip amount

**TaxAmount**

String

Tax amount, should be included in TransAmount

**DutyFreeAmount**

String

value of the tax exemption amount, should be included in TransAmount

**CurrencyCode**

String

check

Indicate currency code of transaction

156: RMB

840: USD

400: JOD

**ReqTransDate**

String (YYYYMMDD)

exp. “20201212”

**ReqTransTime**

String (hhmmss)

exp. “1614033”

**OriTransIndexCode**

String

Original request TransIndexCode

**OriTraceNum**

String

**OriInvoiceNum**

String

Original transaction InvoiceNum

**OriTransId**

String

Indicate original transaction id

**OriRrn**

String

Indicate original RRN

**OriTransDate**

String(YYYYMMDD)

Indicate original transaction date

**OriTransTime**

String(hhmmss)

Indicate original transaction time

**EnableReceipt**

boolean

false-Disable Receipt

true-Enable Receipt

**AppendingReceiptInfo**

String

Indicate message to be printed on receipt

**SkipConfirmProcedure**

boolean

false-Don not Skip

true-Skip Confirm Procedure

**EnableCancelInPayment**

boolean

true-Enable user cancel operation

false-Disable user cancel operation

**AdditionalInfo**

String

Request content sample:

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#id-8.-transaction-response-content)

8\. Transaction Response Content

**Transaction Request is content is json format which contain request data as below:**

NAME

FORMAT

MANDATORY

DESCRIPTION

**TransType**

String

check

Indicate transaction type to be performed.

**TransScheme**

String

Cooperation with TransType，used in specific schemes

[See A1.2 Transaction Scheme](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#a1.2_transaction_type)

**CallerName**

String

Caller name

**TransIndexCode**

String

Indicate Cashier trace number

**TransResult**

boolean

check

true: Success

false: Failed

**RespCode**

String

check

Response code from host server

**RespDesc**

String

check

Response message from host server

**ApprovalCode**

String

Approval code from host

**CardNum**

String

**EntryMode**

Int

0x01: Manual Entry

0x02: Swipe Entry(no CVV)

0x05: Contact ICC(with CVV)

0x07: Contactless

0x90: Swipe Entry(with CVV)

0x91: Contactless MSD

0x95: Contact ICC(no CVV)

**ExpiryDate**

String

**CardBrand**

String

exp.

Visa/MasterCard/Amex/Discover

**TransAmount**

String

\[Mandatory for Sale/Refund\]

check

“112233” means

1122.33(USD) 112.233(JOD)

**OtherAmount**

String

Cash back amount

**TipAmount**

String

Tip amount

**Balance**

String

**TaxAmount**

String

Tax amount, should be included in TransAmount

**DutyFreeAmount**

String

value of the tax exemption amount

**CurrencyCode**

String

Indicate currency code of transaction

156: RMB

840: USD

400: JOD

**CountryCode**

String

**DccOriCurrencyCode**

Integer

\[Mandatory when DCC\]

Original Request Currency Code to be converted

**DccOriAmount**

String

\[Mandatory when DCC\]

Original Request Amount

**DccFee**

String

\[Mandatory when DCC\]

DCC Fee of the transaction

**DccExchangeRate**

String

\[Mandatory when DCC\]

DCC exchange rate

**DccMarkUp**

String

\[Mandatory when DCC\]

DCC mark up

**DccFooterText**

String

\[Mandatory when DCC\]

DCC footer text

**TransDate**

String (YYYYMMDD)

check

Transaction date

exp. “20201212”

**TransTime**

String (hhmmss)

check

Transaction time

exp. “1614033”

**MID**

String

Merchant ID

**TID**

String

Terminal ID

**MerchantName**

String

Merchant Name

**MerchantAddress**

String

Merchant Address

**TraceNum**

String

Trace Number of payment app

**TransID**

String

Transaction ID returned from Host Server

**InvoiceNum**

String

Invoice Number of transaction

**RRN**

String

Retrieval Reference number returned from Host Server

**AuthCode**

String

Transaction Auth Code returned from Host Server

**OriTransIndexCode**

String

Original request TransIndexCode

**OriInvoiceNum**

String

Original transaction InvoiceNum

**OriTransId**

String

Indicate original transaction id

**OriRrn**

String

Indicate original RRN

**EmvAid**

String

Indicate EMV AID

**EmvAppName**

String

Indicate EMV app name

**EmvCryptogram**

String

Indicate EMV TC or ARQC

**EmvTVR**

String

Indicate EMV TVR

**AdditionalInfo**

String

**CardUniqueId**

String

Card unique ID is returned only when TransType is ReadCard.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#id-9.-cancel-request-content)

9\. Cancel Request Content

Cancel request content is empty.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#id-10.-cancel-response-content)

10\. Cancel Response Content

**NAME**

**FORMAT**

**DESCRIPTION**

**“cancelled”**

boolean

\[Mandatory\]

true: transaction cancelled.

False: transaction can’t be cancelled

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#annex-1)

Annex 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#a1.1_transaction_type)

A1.1 Transaction Type

TransType

Description

**Purchase**

**PreAuth**

**IncrementalAuth**

**AuthCompletion**

**BalanceInquiry**

**Reversal**

**Refund**

**Settle**

**TipAdjust**

WorldPay only

**ReadCard**

To get card information, simply pass the TransType, and the CardUniqueId will be returned.

_Local transaction_

**QueryTransaction**

Query transaction result by OriTransIndexCode

**PrintLast**

**PrintTotal**

**PrintDetail**

**PrintParameter**

**GetPosInfo**

**VerifyCardPan**

Verify whether card number match original transaction

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/payment-app-integration-protocol#a1.2_transaction_type)

Scheme

Description

**Credit**

Credit card

**Debit**

Debit card

**EBT**

**ECS**

**QR**

QR transaction

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    Fixed 0x02

Copy

    Byte 1: 	
        0x01 indicate data from Cashier
        0x02 indicate data from POS
        0xF1 indicate Handshake Request
        0xF2 indicate Handshake Response
        0xC1 indicate Cancel Request
        0xC2 indicate Cancel Response
    Byte 2: 		
        Reserved. Set to 0x00.
    Byte 3-4:	
        Sequence number, request package set to X, response package set to X+1 exp. 
        Request [01] [0F], Response [01] [10]
    

Copy

    Exp. [01] [0F] means 0x10F (271) bytes.

Copy

    BCC algorithm:
    BCC := [VERSION] xor [CTRL Byte1] xor [CTRL Byte2] xor … xor [ETX]

Copy

    {
    “TransType”: “Purchase”,
    “TransIndexCode”: “112233”,
    “TransAmount”: “10000”,
    “CurrencyCode”: “840”,
    “ReqTransDate”: “20210302”,
    “ReqTransTime”: “144230”,
    “OriTransId”: “”,
    “OriRrn “: “”,
    “EnableReceipt “: true,
    “AppendingReceiptInfo “: “”,
    “SkipConfirmProcedure”: false
    }

# Payment App AIDL Integration Protocol | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/payment-app-aidl-integration-protocol#id-1.-introduction)

1\. Introduction

This document descripts how to use android AIDL to call payment app.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/payment-app-aidl-integration-protocol#id-2.-transaction-flow)

2\. Transaction Flow

a) put the **aidl** and java folders into path **src/main** under app module

b) rebuild your project to build aidl source code

c) bind the service and call payment app

package: **com.wizarpos.opc**

action: **com.wizarpos.payment.aidl.pay**

File you will need in your android project:

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/payment-app-aidl-integration-protocol#id-3.-transaction-request-content)

3\. Transaction Request Content

**Transaction Request is content is json format as below:**

NAME

FORMAT

MANDATORY

DESCRIPTION

**TransType**

String

check

Indicate transaction type to be performed.

[See A1.1 Transaction Type](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/payment-app-aidl-integration-protocol#a1.1_transaction_type)

**TransScheme**

String

Cooperation with TransType，used in specific schemes

[See A1.2 Transaction Scheme](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/payment-app-aidl-integration-protocol#a1.2_transaction_type)

**CallerName**

String

Caller name

**TransIndexCode**

String

Indicate Cashier trace number

Should be unique for every transaction

**BusinessNum**

String

Business registration number

**TerminalNum**

String

Terminal number

**TransAmount**

String

\[Mandatory for payment\]

check

Total amount including OtherAmount and TipAmount

“112233” means 1122.33(USD) or 112.233(JOD) depending on CurrencyCode

**OtherAmount**

String

Cash back amount

**TipAmount**

String

Tip amount

**TaxAmount**

String

Tax amount, should be included in TransAmount

**DutyFreeAmount**

String

value of the tax exemption amount, should be included in TransAmount

**CurrencyCode**

String

check

Indicate currency code of transaction

156: RMB

840: USD

400: JOD

**ReqTransDate**

String (YYYYMMDD)

exp. “20201212”

**ReqTransTime**

String (hhmmss)

exp. “1614033”

**OriTransIndexCode**

String

Original request TransIndexCode

**OriTraceNum**

String

**OriInvoiceNum**

String

Original transaction InvoiceNum

**OriTransId**

String

Indicate original transaction id

**OriRrn**

String

Indicate original RRN

**OriTransDate**

String(YYYYMMDD)

Indicate original transaction date

**OriTransTime**

String(hhmmss)

Indicate original transaction time

**EnableReceipt**

boolean

false-Disable Receipt

true-Enable Receipt

**AppendingReceiptInfo**

String

Indicate message to be printed on receipt

**SkipConfirmProcedure**

boolean

false-Don not Skip

true-Skip Confirm Procedure

**EnableCancelInPayment**

boolean

true-Enable user cancel operation

false-Disable user cancel operation

**AdditionalInfo**

String

4\. Transaction Response Content

**Transaction Request is content is json format which contain request data as below:**

NAME

FORMAT

MANDATORY

DESCRIPTION

**TransType**

check

**CallerName**

String

Caller name

**TransIndexCode**

String

Indicate Cashier trace number

**TransResult**

boolean

check

true: Success

false: Failed

**RespCode**

String

check

Response code from host server

**RespDesc**

String

check

Response message from host server

**ApprovalCode**

String

Approval code from host

**CardNum**

String

**EntryMode**

Int

0x01: Manual Entry

0x02: Swipe Entry(no CVV)

0x05: Contact ICC(with CVV)

0x07: Contactless

0x90: Swipe Entry(with CVV)

0x91: Contactless MSD

0x95: Contact ICC(no CVV)

**ExpiryDate**

String

**CardBrand**

String

exp.

Visa/MasterCard/Amex/Discover

**TransAmount**

String

\[Mandatory for Sale/Refund\]

check

“112233” means

1122.33(USD) 112.233(JOD)

**OtherAmount**

String

Cash back amount

**TipAmount**

String

Tip amount

**Balance**

String

**TaxAmount**

String

Tax amount, should be included in TransAmount

String

value of the tax exemption amount

**CurrencyCode**

String

Indicate currency code of transaction

156: RMB

840: USD

400: JOD

check

check

# Client SDK API | Paywizard Integration

This section details the methods and objects provided by the PayWizard Web Element SDK.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#paywizard-clienttoken-options)

PayWizard(clientToken, options)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Initializes the PayWizard SDK instance.

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientToken`

string

✓

Developer Token, used for authentication

`options`

Object

Optional parameters, currently undefined

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#returns)

**Returns**

SDK instance, providing the `initCheckout` method to create a checkout session.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#example)

**Example**

Copy

    const payWizard = PayWizard("your-client-token");

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#paywizard.initcheckout-params)

payWizard.initCheckout(params)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Creates a new checkout session and returns the checkout object.

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`params.clientId`

string

✓

Unique client identifier

`params.merchantId`

string

✓

Unique merchant identifier

`params.checkoutId`

string

✓

Unique checkout session identifier (obtained from server-side call to "Create Online Payment Order" API)

`params.elementsOptions`

Object

UI configuration options

`params.elementsOptions.appearance`

Object

Appearance-related configuration

`params.elementsOptions.appearance.width`

string | number

iframe width

`params.elementsOptions.appearance.theme`

`"light"` | `"night"`

Interface theme

`params.savePaymentMethods`

boolean

Whether to allow saving the customer's payment methods

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#about-params.checkoutid)

**About** `**params.checkoutId**`

`checkoutId` is the unique identifier for the checkout session, obtained by your server-side through calling the "Create Online Payment Order" API. Brief information about this API is mentioned in the "Core Integration Steps", and detailed information can be found in the Server-side API Details section at the end of the document.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#returns-1)

**Returns**

`Promise<Checkout>` - A Promise that resolves to a `Checkout` object.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#example-1)

**Example**

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#checkout-object)

Checkout Object


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `Checkout` object provides methods for managing the payment process. It is the return value after a successful call to `payWizard.initCheckout()`.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#checkout.session-options)

**checkout.session(options)**

Sets session-related parameters.

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`options.customer`

string

Unique customer identifier, used for payment method storage

`options.card`

string

Saved payment method identifier

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#about-options.card)

**About** `**options.card**`

`options.card` is the identifier of the saved payment method (i.e., `cardToken`). If your user has previously agreed to save payment methods, you can obtain their `cardToken` list by calling the "Retrieve Bank Card Information by UserId" API on your server-side. Detailed information about this API can be found in the Server-side API Details section at the end of the document.

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#returns-2)

**Returns**

None

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#example-2)

**Example**

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#checkout.mount-selector)

**checkout.mount(selector)**

Mounts the payment interface to the specified DOM element.

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`selector`

string

✓

CSS selector specifying the mount point

**Returns**

`Promise<void>` - A Promise that resolves when mounting is complete.

**Example**

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#checkout.unmount)

**checkout.unmount()**

Unmounts the payment interface from the DOM.

**Returns**

None

**Example**

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#checkout.destroy)

**checkout.destroy()**

Destroys the checkout instance and cleans up all resources.

**Returns**

None

**Example**

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/online-card-payment/client-sdk-api#checkout.confirm)

**checkout.confirm()**

Confirms the payment transaction.

**Returns**

`Promise<Object>` - A Promise containing the transaction result.

**Note**

If a `redirectUrl` was provided during initialization (via the server-side call to the "Create Online Payment Order" API), after calling `confirm`, the user may be redirected to that URL. When redirected, the URL will automatically append the following query parameters:

*   `checkoutId`: The ID of this checkout session.
    
*   `result`: The payment result status code (e.g., 0 for success, 1 for failure, 2 for processing).
    
*   `customerId`: (Optional) If applicable, the customer ID will be returned.
    
*   `cardToken`: (Optional) If applicable, the card identifier for subsequent payments will be returned. You need to handle these parameters on your server-side to complete the subsequent process.
    

**Example**
