# Get Access Tokens | Paywizard Integration

circle-check

Once you are onboarded as one of our developers, we will provide you with a semi-permanent token for testing. For merchants in the production environment, we will also provide a semi-permanent token to be used for transactions.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/get-access-tokens#merchant-token-purpose)

**Merchant Token Purpose**:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each merchant is provided with one or more unique tokens, acting as secure keys to interact with our payment gateway. These tokens are crucial for authenticating the merchant's requests and ensuring that only authorized entities can process payments through their account.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/get-access-tokens#two-distinct-token-types-channel-specific)

**Two Distinct Token Types (Channel-Specific)**:


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **E-commerce (ECOMM) Token**: This token is specifically designed for online transactions. Merchants integrating our payment services into their websites or mobile applications for digital sales would use this token. It's tailored for server-to-server or client-to-server API calls originating from an online environment.
    
*   **Terminal Transaction Token**: This token is used for "card-present" transactions, where payments are processed via a physical point-of-sale (POS) terminal. This token is optimized for environments where direct entry by staff or physical card swipes/taps occur.
    

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/get-access-tokens#test-merchant-token-email-sample)

Test Merchant Token Email Sample:


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# API: POS Initiate Transaction | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/api-pos-initiate-transaction#through-this-api-interface-you-will-be-able-to-initiate-a-transaction-from-your-point-of-sale-system)

Through this API interface, you will be able to initiate a transaction from your Point Of Sale system or web platform.

circle-info

This API is for Point of Sale system

circle-info

The payment terminal which receiving the transaction request is the one binded to the POSID which belongs to the merchant.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/api-pos-initiate-transaction#initiate-a-transaction)

Initiate a Transaction


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Test Enviroment:**

`POST` [https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/internetTransarrow-up-right](https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/internetTrans)

**Production Enviroment:**

`POST` [https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/internetTransarrow-up-right](https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/internetTrans)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/api-pos-initiate-transaction#headers)

**Headers**

Name

Value

Content-Type

`application/json`

jwt-token

Merchant Token provided by Paywizard in merchant token email

sign

[PayWizard Open Platform API Signature Guide V3](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/api-pos-initiate-transaction#request-body)

String

check

This is the final total transaction amount.

Tip amount

false: do not print,

true: print.

appendingReceiptInfo

String

skipConfirmProcedure

boolean

`{false,true}`

Skip confirmation step:

false: do not skip.

true: skip

callBackUrl

String

If the POS system is cloud-based, the transaction result can be obtained through this URL.

Please see: Transaction result callback interface

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/api-pos-initiate-transaction#response-sample)

**Response Sample**

200

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/api-pos-initiate-transaction#merchantid-merchant-id)

`**merchantId**` **(Merchant ID)**

*   **What it is:** A unique identifier for your business account.
    
*   **Who provides it:** The Payment Processor.
    
*   **In the Sandbox:** For testing purposes, Paywizard will give you a specific test `merchantId`. This ensures that your test transactions are processed in the sandbox environment and not with real money.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/api-pos-initiate-transaction#terminalid-payment-terminal-id-tid)

`**terminalId**` **(Payment Terminal ID / TID)**

*   **What it is:** A unique identifier for a specific payment terminal (the physical devices that reads the credit/debit card).
    
*   **Who provides it:** Also provided and registered by the Payment Processor. A single merchant can have many terminals, and each one will have its own unique `terminalId`.
    
*   **In the Sandbox:** Since you are not using a real, physical payment terminal during testing, you don't need a real, registered ID. That is why you can use any 8-digit number as a placeholder `terminalId`.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/api-pos-initiate-transaction#posid-point-of-sale-id)

`**posId**` **(Point of Sale ID)**

*   **What it is:** A unique identifier for the device that _initiates_ the payment request. This is your internal ID.
    
*   **Who provides it:** You (the developer or the business) create and manage this ID within your own software system. The Payment Processor does not know or provide this ID.
    
*   **Purpose:** The `posId` identifies the specific point of sale in your system. This could be:
    
    *   A cash register (e.g., `CASH_REGISTER_01`)
        
    *   A self-service kiosk (e.g., `KIOSK_LOBBY_A`)
        
    *   A PC running billing software (e.g., `FRONT_DESK_PC`)
        
    *   Any other device that can start a transaction.
        
    

[PreviousDo Transactionschevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions)
[NextTransaction Request Examplechevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/api-pos-initiate-transaction/transaction-request-example)

# API: Get POS & Terminal Binding List | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/api-get-pos-and-terminal-binding-list#through-this-api-interface-you-will-be-able-to-obtain-a-list-of-pos-under-the-current-merchant-id-al)

# Transaction Type | Paywizard Integration

TransType

Description

**Purchase**

**PreAuth**

**IncrementalAuth**

**AuthCompletion**

**BalanceInquiry**

**Reversal**

**Refund**

**Settle**

**TipAdjust**

**ReadCard**

To get card information, simply pass the TransType, and the CardUniqueId will be returned.

_Local transaction_

**QueryTransaction**

Query transaction result by OriTransIndexCode

**PrintLast**

**PrintTotal**

**PrintDetail**

**PrintParameter**

**GetPosInfo**

**VerifyCardPan**

Verify whether card number match original transaction

# Terminal API: Subscribe Transaction Results | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/terminal-api-subscribe-transaction-results#through-this-api-interface-you-will-be-able-to-let-the-payment-terminal-to-send-transaction-result-t)

Through this API interface, you will be able to let the payment terminal to send transaction result to the Paywizard platform.

triangle-exclamation

This API is for payment terminal use. Not for Point of Sale system.

Most intergration process will not use this API.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/do-transactions/terminal-api-subscribe-transaction-results#subscribe-transaction-results)

Subscribe Transaction Results


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`POST` `https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/subscribeCashierAgentResult`

**Headers**

Name

Value

Content-Type

`application/json`

jwt-token

`The token responesed from Get Access Token`

**Request Body**

Name

Type

Mandatory

Description

clientId

string

check

Developer ID

merchantId

String

check

Merchant ID

terminalId

String

check

Terminal ID

tradeNo

String

check

hird-party POS systems order numbers,

must be unique under the same ISO/ISV.

transType

String

check

See support transaction type

transScheme

String

check

`{Credit,Debit,EBT,ECS}`

CallerName

String

check

Merchant Name

transIndexCode

String

check

Paywizard trans id

transResult

boolean

check

{true,false}

true: Transaction approved false: Transaction denied

respCode

String

check

Payment host response code.

respDesc

String

check

Payment host response message.

cardNum

String

Card Number

entryMode

Integer

check

Card entry mode:

*   `0x01`: Manual entry card number
    
*   `0x02`: Magnetic stripe
    
*   `0x05`: Contact
    
*   `0x07`: Contactless

check

# API: Bind POS & Payment Terminal | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/api-bind-pos-and-payment-terminal#through-this-api-interface-you-will-be-able-to-register-your-own-pos-to-the-platform-and-simultaneou)

Through this API interface, you will be able to register your own POS to the platform and simultaneously bind the payment terminal

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/api-bind-pos-and-payment-terminal#register-pos-and-bind-pos-with-payment-terminal)

Register POS and Bind POS with Payment Terminal


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Test Enviroment:**

`POST` [https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/registerTerminalarrow-up-right](https://oversea.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/registerTerminal)

**Production Enviroment:**

`POST` [https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/registerTerminalarrow-up-right](https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/registerTerminal)

**Headers**

Name

Value

Content-Type

`application/json`

jwt-token

Merchant Token provided by Paywizard

sign

[PayWizard Open Platform API Signature Guide V3](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)

* * *

**Request Body**

Name

Type

Mandatory

Description

clientId

string

check

Developer ID provided by Paywizard

merchantId

String

check

[Merchant ID](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/api-bind-pos-and-payment-terminal#merchantid-merchant-id)

posId

String

check

[Point of Sale ID](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/api-bind-pos-and-payment-terminal#posid-point-of-sale-id)

terminalId

String

check

[Payment Terminal ID](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/api-bind-pos-and-payment-terminal#terminalid-payment-terminal-id-tid)

[(Payment Processor TID)](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/api-bind-pos-and-payment-terminal#terminalid-payment-terminal-id-tid)

terminalSn

String

check

Payment Terminal S/N

(Device S/N)

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/api-bind-pos-and-payment-terminal#merchantid-merchant-id)

`**merchantId**` **(Merchant ID)**

*   **What it is:** A unique identifier for your business account.
    
*   **Who provides it:** The Payment Processor.
    
*   **In the Sandbox:** For testing purposes, Paywizard will give you a specific test `merchantId`. This ensures that your test transactions are processed in the sandbox environment and not with real money.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/api-bind-pos-and-payment-terminal#terminalid-payment-terminal-id-tid)

`**terminalId**` **(Payment Terminal ID / TID)**

*   **What it is:** A unique identifier for a specific payment terminal (the physical devices that reads the credit/debit card).
    
*   **Who provides it:** Also provided and registered by the Payment Processor. A single merchant can have many terminals, and each one will have its own unique `terminalId`.
    
*   **In the Sandbox:** Since you are not using a real, physical payment terminal during testing, you don't need a real, registered ID. That is why you can use any 8-digit number as a placeholder `terminalId`.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/pos-and-payment-terminal-binding-process/api-bind-pos-and-payment-terminal#posid-point-of-sale-id)

`**posId**` **(Point of Sale ID)**

*   **What it is:** A unique identifier for the device that _initiates_ the payment request. This is your internal ID.
    
*   **Who provides it:** You (the developer or the business) create and manage this ID within your own software system. The Payment Processor does not know or provide this ID.
    
*   **Purpose:** The `posId` identifies the specific point of sale in your system. This could be:
    
    *   A cash register (e.g., `CASH_REGISTER_01`)
        
    *   A self-service kiosk (e.g., `KIOSK_LOBBY_A`)
        
    *   A PC running billing software (e.g., `FRONT_DESK_PC`)
        
    *   Any other device that can start a transaction.
        
    
*   **Why it must be unique in your system:** The most important role of the `posId` is to create a one-to-one pairing between your initiating device and a specific payment terminal (`terminalId`). When a cashier at "Checkout 3" (`posId` = `CHECKOUT_3`) presses the "Pay by Card" button, your system knows it must send the payment request to the specific payment terminal paired with that POS (e.g., `terminalId` = `87654321`).
    

**Request Sample**

**Response Body**

Name

Type

Mandatory

Description

code

int

check

Response Code

`(200 Success,`

`Non-200 Failed)`

msg

String

check

Response Message

timestamp

String

check

Date/Time(UTC)

**Response Sample**

200

# Serial Connection Best Practice | Paywizard Integration

Here is the quick debug steps that you might want use an serial connection from your Point of Sale machine or Vending Machine or PC.

1

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/serial-connection-best-practice#install-payment-apps)

Install Payment Apps

Option 1: Install Payment Apps, apps can be installed through ADB, or push by TMS.

[https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/OPC\_V1.7.0-global-release.apkftp.wizarpos.comchevron-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/OPC_V1.7.0-global-release.apk)

[https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/PayWizard\_Demo\_V2.0.0\_2508081.apkftp.wizarpos.comchevron-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/PayWizard_Demo_V2.0.0_2508081.apk)

Option 2: Our tech support team also can help you to download these apk to your terminal.

2

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/serial-connection-best-practice#set-protocal-type-to-serial-or-tms-push-para-to-terminal)

Set Protocal Type to Serial or TMS Push Para to terminal

Option 1: Set terminal connection protocal type to **Serial** in Payment app, refer to PaymentInterfaceAppUserGuide.pdf

# API: Get Merchant Transaction | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/api-get-merchant-transaction#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This endpoint retrieves a paginated list of transaction logs. You can filter the results using various parameters such as a date range, merchant ID, or transaction type.

**Test Enviroment:**

`POST` [https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/open/v3/queryTranLogListarrow-up-right](https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/open/v3/queryTranLogList)

**Production Enviroment:**

`POST` [https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/open/v3/queryTranLogList arrow-up-right](https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/open/queryTranLogList)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/api-get-merchant-transaction#http-header-information)

**HTTP Header Information**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Name

Value

Content-Type

`application/json`

jwt-token

Merchant Token provided by Paywizard

sign

[PayWizard Open Platform API Signature Guide V3](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/api-get-merchant-transaction#request-body-parameters)

**Request Body Parameters**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`clientId`

String

Yes

Your unique developer ID.

`mid`

String

No

The merchant ID to filter results.

`transactionId`

String

No

The specific transaction log ID to retrieve.

`transType`

String

No

The transaction type to filter by (e.g., "Purchase").

`startTime`

String

No

The start of the date range for the query. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`endTime`

String

No

The end of the date range for the query. Format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss`.

`pageNo`

Integer

No

The page number to retrieve.

`pageSize`

Integer

No

The number of records to return per page. Defaults to `100`.

**Request Example**

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/api-get-merchant-transaction#response-body)

**Response Body**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response is a JSON object containing the list of transaction records and pagination details.

Parameter

Type

Description

`code`

Integer

The HTTP status code. `200` indicates a successful request.

`msg`

String

A human-readable message. `success` on successful requests.

`timestamp`

String

The UTC timestamp of the response.

`data`

Object

A container for the successful response data.

`data.records`

Array

An array of [Transaction Record Objectsarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23transaction-record-object)
.

`data.total`

Integer

See [Pagination Metadataarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23pagination-metadata)
.

`data.pages`

Integer

See [Pagination Metadataarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23pagination-metadata)
.

`data.size`

Integer

See [Pagination Metadataarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23pagination-metadata)
.

`data.current`

Integer

See [Pagination Metadataarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=%23pagination-metadata)
.

**Transaction Record Object**

This object represents a single transaction log within the `records` array.

Parameter

Type

Description

`transactionId`

String

The unique ID for the transaction log entry.

`mid`

String

The merchant ID associated with the transaction.

`amount`

Long

The transaction amount represented as an integer in 1/10000th units of the currency. See note below.

`currencyCode`

String

The numeric ISO 4217 currency code.

`tranTime`

String

The timestamp of the transaction.

`tranType`

String

The type of transaction (e.g., "Purchase").

`checkoutId`

String

The unique transaction ID generated by the payment platform.

`thirdOrderId`

String

The unique order ID generated by the third-party (your) system.

circle-exclamation

Note on `amount` format: The amount is provided in ten-thousandths of the major currency unit. For example, for a currency like the US Dollar, a value of `1436200` represents $143.62.

**Pagination Metadata**

These fields provide information about the paginated result set.

Parameter

Type

Description

`total`

String

The total number of records matching the query.

`pages`

String

The total number of pages available.

`size`

String

The number of records per page.

`current`

String

The current page number.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/api-get-merchant-transaction#success-response-example)

**Success Response Example**

# Socket Connection Best Practice | Paywizard Integration

Here is the debug steps that you might want use an serial connection from your Point of Sale machine or Vending Machine or PC.

1

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/socket-connection-best-practice#install-payment-apps)

Install Payment Apps

Option 1: Install Payment Apps, apps can be installed through ADB, or push by TMS.

[https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/OPC\_V1.7.0-global-release.apkftp.wizarpos.comchevron-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/OPC_V1.7.0-global-release.apk)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/local-integration/socket-connection-best-practice#sart-debugging)

Sart debugging

Suitable for scenarios where no application development on the POS terminal is needed. Instead, the Vendor Machine communicates directly with the Payment App. In this case, communication between the POS terminal and the Vendor Machine supports serial port, MDB (Multi-Drop Bus), and Socket protocols.

Reference for data packaging and unpacking of VM：

[https://ftp.wizarpos.com/advanceSDK/PaymentApp/Serial&SocketDemo240910.zipftp.wizarpos.comchevron-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/advanceSDK/PaymentApp/Serial&SocketDemo240910.zip)

# Webhook: Push Transaction Result | Paywizard Integration

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result#description)

**Description**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    The third party provides the request address to push transaction results, requiring signature verification.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result#webhook)

**Webhook**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result#you-create-a-url)

You Create a URL

You need to create a URL on your own server that is capable of receiving incoming POST requests from Paywizard. This is your "webhook link."

2

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result#submit-the-url-to-paywizard)

Submit the URL to Paywizard

You must give this URL to Paywizard support channels.

3

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result#paywizard-binds-the-url)

Paywizard Binds the URL

Paywizard will then link (or "bind") this URL to your specific developer account.

4

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result#automatic-data-pushes)

Automatic Data Pushes

Once bound, every time a transaction happen for any merchant operating under your developer account, Paywizard's server will automatically send a POST request containing the transaction data to your URL.

5

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result#you-process-the-data)

You Process the Data

Your server will receive this data and can then use it to trigger actions in your system, such as updating an order's status, notifying a customer, or recording the transaction in your database.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result#http-header)

**HTTP Header**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Name

Value

Content-Type

`application/json`

sign-version

version of sign

paywizard-sign

[PayWizard Open Platform API Signature Guide V3](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-transaction-result#transaction-result-parameters)

**Transaction Result Parameters**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# API: Get Merchant Infomation | Paywizard Integration

**Enviroment:**

`POST` [https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/getMerchantInfoarrow-up-right](https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/getMerchantInfo)

**Production Enviroment:**

`POST` [https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/getMerchantInfoarrow-up-right](https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/semiOpen/v3/getMerchantInfo)

**HTTP Header Information**

Name

Value

Content-Type

# APM (QR/WALLET) API | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration/apm-qr-wallet-api#post-ovstrade-openpay-micropay)

Quick Pay - Merchant Scan

post

/ovstrade/openPay/microPay

This endpoint processes a payment using a customer-provided authorization code (often from a QR code or barcode on their device). This is typically used in a "merchant-scan" scenario where the merchant's point-of-sale system scans the customer's payment code.

Header parameters

jwt-tokenstringRequiredExample: `{{ecommerceToken}}`

signstringRequiredExample: `signtext`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

clientIdstringRequired

Your unique developer ID.

transIndexCodestring · max: 60Required

The unique order ID generated by your system.

scanChannelstringRequired

The payment channel associated with the auth code.

amountstringRequired

The total transaction amount.

Example: `10.5`

authCodestringRequired

The authorization code scanned from the customer's device.

tranCurrencystringRequired

The 3-letter ISO currency code for the transaction.

Example: `USD`

productDescstringOptional

A brief description of the product(s) or service(s).

payerTypestringOptional

The type of payer identifier. Required when scanChannel is MOMO.

Example: `MSISDN`

notifyUrlstringOptional

The callback URL where you will receive the final transaction result notification.

Responses

chevron-right

200Success

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

post

/ovstrade/openPay/microPay

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

200Success

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration/apm-qr-wallet-api#post-ovstrade-openpay-generateqrcode)

Generate QR Code - Customer Scan

post

/ovstrade/openPay/generateQrCode

This endpoint allows you to generate a QR code for a "customer-scan" payment scenario. The customer scans the generated QR code with their device to complete the payment.

Query parameters

jwt-tokenstringOptionalExample: `{{ecommerceToken}}`

Header parameters

jwt-tokenstringRequiredExample: `{{ecommerceToken}}`

signstringRequiredExample: `signtext`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

clientIdstringRequired

Your unique developer ID.

transIndexCodestring · max: 60Required

The unique order ID generated by your system.

payChannelstringRequired

The payment channel to be used.

amountstringRequired

The total transaction amount.

Example: `10.5`

currencystringRequired

The 3-letter ISO currency code for the transaction amount. For PIX transactions, this must be BRL.

Example: `BRL`

exchangeCurrencystringOptional

The currency code for settlement. Valid values: BRL, USD, EUR. Required for PIX transactions. Currently only BRL is supported.

Example: `BRL`

documentNumberstringOptional

The customer's tax identification number (e.g., CPF or CNPJ). Required for PIX transactions.

socialNamestringOptional

The full name of the customer. Required for PIX transactions.

dynamicPixExpiresAtstringOptional

The expiration timestamp for a dynamic PIX QR code in ISO 8601 format: YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm:ssZ.

productDescstringOptional

A brief description of the product(s) or service(s).

notifyUrlstringOptional

The callback URL where you will receive the transaction result notification.

Responses

chevron-right

200Success

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

post

/ovstrade/openPay/generateQrCode

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

200Success

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration/apm-qr-wallet-api#post-ovstrade-openpay-queryorder)

Query Transaction Status

post

/ovstrade/openPay/queryOrder

This endpoint allows you to query the status and details of a specific transaction using either the platform's checkoutId or your original transIndexCode.

signstringRequiredExample: `signtext`

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration/apm-qr-wallet-api#post-ovstrade-openpay-refundorder)

Refund

post

/ovstrade/openPay/refundOrder

This endpoint is used to issue a full or partial refund for a previously completed transaction.

Note: Partial refunds are not supported by all payment channels. Please check the documentation for your specific channel.

Header parameters

jwt-tokenstringRequiredExample: `{{ecommerceToken}}`

signstringRequiredExample: `signtext`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

clientIdstringRequired

Your unique developer ID.

transIndexCodestring · max: 60Required

A new, unique order ID for this specific refund request, generated by your system.

oriCheckoutIdstringOptional

The original checkoutId of the transaction you want to refund.

oriTransIndexCodestringOptional

The original transIndexCode of the transaction you want to refund.

amountstringRequired

The amount to be refunded.

notifyUrlstringOptional

The callback URL where you will receive the final refund result notification.

Responses

chevron-right

200Success

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

post

/ovstrade/openPay/refundOrder

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

200Success

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/apm-qr-wallet/quick-start-qr-payment-api-integration/apm-qr-wallet-api#post-ovstrade-openpay-reversalorder)

Void

post

/ovstrade/openPay/reversalOrder

This endpoint is used to reverse (or void) a transaction. A reversal is typically used to cancel a transaction on the same day it was made, before the funds have settled.

Note: Partial reversals are not supported by all payment channels.

Header parameters

jwt-tokenstringRequiredExample: `{{ecommerceToken}}`

signstringRequiredExample: `signtext`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

clientIdstringRequired

Your unique developer ID.

transIndexCodestring · max: 60Required

A new, unique order ID for this specific refund request, generated by your system.

oriCheckoutIdstringRequired

The original checkoutId of the transaction you want to refund.

oriTransIndexCodestringRequired

The original transIndexCode of the transaction you want to refund.

amountstringRequired

The amount to be refunded.

notifyUrlstringRequired

The callback URL where you will receive the final refund result notification.

Responses

chevron-right

200Success

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Close Order

post

/ovstrade/openPay/closeOrder

This endpoint is used to close an order that has been created but has not yet been paid. This action prevents the customer from completing the payment for the specified transaction.

# Webhook: Push Settlement Information | Paywizard Integration

This interface is used to push settlement summary and transaction details to a third-party system via a webhook. The system will send a POST request with JSON data when a batch is settled.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-settlement-information#request-information)

Request Information


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Method: `POST`
    
*   Content-Type: `application/json`
    

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-settlement-information#http-header)

**HTTP Header**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Name

Value

Content-Type

`application/json`

sign-version

version of sign

paywizard-sign

[PayWizard Open Platform API Signature Guide V3](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/paywizard-open-platform-api-signature-guide-v3)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-settlement-information#request-parameters)

Request Parameters


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-settlement-information#root-object)

**Root Object**

Variable Name

Type

Required

Description

`sn`

String

Yes

The terminal serial number (e.g., WP20031Q21000000).

`packageName`

String

Yes

The package name of the payment application.

`summary`

Object

Yes

Settlement summary information (see Summary Object below).

`settlementList`

Array

Yes

List of settlement transactions (see Settlement Item below).

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-settlement-information#summary-object-summary)

**Summary Object (**`**summary**`**)**

**Variable Name**

**Type**

**Required**

**Description**

`mid`

String

Yes

Merchant ID.

`tid`

String

Yes

Terminal ID.

`batchId`

String

Yes

The batch number associated with this settlement.

`currencyCode`

String

Yes

ISO 4217 Currency Code (e.g., `840` for USD).

`debitTotalCount`

Long

Yes

Total count of debit (sale/positive) transactions.

`debitTotalAmount`

Long

Yes

Total amount of debit transactions (in lowest currency unit, e.g., cents).

`creditTotalCount`

Long

Yes

Total count of credit (refund/negative) transactions.

`creditTotalAmount`

Long

Yes

Total amount of credit transactions (in lowest currency unit).

`settleStatus`

String

Yes

Status of the settlement (e.g., `CLOSED`).

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-settlement-information#settlement-item-object-settlementlist)

**Settlement Item Object (**`**settlementList**`**)**

**Variable Name**

**Type**

**Required**

**Description**

`amount`

Long

Yes

Transaction amount

`transId`

String

Yes

Transaction ID / Trace Number.

`batchId`

String

Yes

The batch number for this specific transaction.

`tranTime`

String

Yes

Transaction time. Format: `yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss`.

`transType`

String

No

Transaction type (e.g., `SALE`, `REFUND`).

`cardType`

String

No

Card brand/type (e.g., `VISA`, `MASTERCARD`).

* * *

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-settlement-information#request-example)

Request Example


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

JSON

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/get-transaction-result/webhook-push-settlement-information#response)

Response


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The receiving server should return an HTTP status code to acknowledge receipt.

*   Success: `200 OK`
    
*   Failure: `4xx` or `5xx` (The sender may retry based on internal retry policies).

# Terminal API : Upload Settlement Info | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/e-receipt-intro/terminal-api-upload-settlement-info#the-payment-application-reports-back-settlement-information-using-this-api)

The payment application reports back settlement information using this API.

circle-exclamation

This API is for Payment Application

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/e-receipt-intro/terminal-api-upload-settlement-info#upload-settlement-info)

Upload Settlement Info


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Test Enviroment:**

`POST`[`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/mrtSettlementReport/settlementReport`arrow-up-right](https://oversea.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/mrtSettlementReport/settlementReport)

**Production Enviroment:**

`POST`[`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/mrtSettlementReport/settlementReport`arrow-up-right](https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/mrtSettlementReport/settlementReport)

**Headers**

Name

Value

Content-Type

`application/json`

**Request Body**

Name

Type

Mandatory

Description

mid

String

check

Merchant ID

tid

String

check

Terminal ID

merchantName

String

check

merchantAddr

String

packageName

String

check

Payment Application Package Name

sn

String

check

Terminal S/N

reportTime

String

check

currencyCode

String

check

batchNumber

String

paymentTypes

List<Object>

check

{credit,debit,debit\_master\_visa,extra}

\-paymentType

String

check

\-paymentNumber

String

check

\-payTypeBatchNumber

String

\-settlementLogs

List<Object>

check

\--tradeType

String

check

{sale,void,total}

\--paymentNumber

String

check

\--currencyCode

# AIDL Integration Best Practice | Paywizard Integration

Here is the debug steps that you might want use an serial connection from your Point of Sale machine or Vending Machine or PC.

1

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/aidl-integration-best-practice#install-payment-apps)

Install Payment Apps

Option 1: Install Payment Apps, apps can be installed through ADB, or push by TMS.

[https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/PayWizard\_Demo\_V2.0.0\_2508081.apkftp.wizarpos.comchevron-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/PayWizard_Demo_V2.0.0_2508081.apk)

[https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/OPC\_V1.7.0-global-release.apkftp.wizarpos.comchevron-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/OPC_V1.7.0-global-release.apk)

Option 2: Our tech support team also can help you to download these apk to your terminal. [arrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/payment/OPC_V1.7.0-global-release.apk)

2

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/aidl-integration-best-practice#set-protocal-type-to-default-or-tms-push-para-to-terminal)

Set Protocal Type to DEFAULT or TMS Push Para to terminal

Option 1: Set terminal connection protocal type to **Default** in Payment app, refer to PaymentInterfaceAppUserGuide.pdf

file-pdf

296KB

[PaymentInterfaceAppUserGuide.pdf](https://2631785516-files.gitbook.io/~/files/v0/b/gitbook-x-prod.appspot.com/o/spaces%2FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%2Fuploads%2FnkmPX31oU8SowcD1VXUz%2FPaymentInterfaceAppUserGuide.pdf?alt=media&token=04fa0569-9838-41d0-94c2-fdd364e7729b)

PDF

downloadDownload[arrow-up-right-from-squareOpen](https://2631785516-files.gitbook.io/~/files/v0/b/gitbook-x-prod.appspot.com/o/spaces%2FY7FuzH91SaNfvhwFA9Ic%2Fuploads%2FnkmPX31oU8SowcD1VXUz%2FPaymentInterfaceAppUserGuide.pdf?alt=media&token=04fa0569-9838-41d0-94c2-fdd364e7729b)

Option 2: Our tech support team also can help you to push parameter to your terminal to modify this settings.

3

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/aidl-integration-best-practice#connect-payment-terminal-to-pc-anroid-studio)

Connect Payment Terminal to PC Anroid Studio

With usb cable

4

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/aidl-integration-best-practice#start-debug-in-your-pc-anroid-studio)

[![Logo](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2420409429-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Forganizations%252FSE7LtGg9ZjnRTksgOj5H%252Fsites%252Fsite_xbsrk%252Ficon%252FolYTTY3ddZEWDoR3Qwzs%252Fpaywizard.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4236902e-08b1-4fe1-b071-2963fa337129&width=48&height=48&sign=c51abe8&sv=2)Payment App AIDL Integration Protocol | Paywizard Integrationsmartpossdk.gitbook.iochevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/semi-integration/internal-integration/payment-app-aidl-integration)

# Terminal API : Upload Transaction Info | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/e-receipt-intro/terminal-api-upload-transaction-info#the-payment-application-reports-back-transaction-information-using-this-api)

The payment application reports back transaction information using this API.

circle-exclamation

This API is for Payment Application

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/cloud-api/e-receipt-intro/terminal-api-upload-transaction-info#upload-transaction-info)

Upload Transaction Info


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Test Enviroment:**

`POST` [`https://uat.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/sysTransLog/updateTransInfo`arrow-up-right](https://oversea.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/sysTransLog/updateTransInfo)

**Production Enviroment:**

`POST` [`https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/sysTransLog/updateTransInfo`arrow-up-right](https://portal.paywizard.biz/ovstrade/sysTransLog/updateTransInfo)

**Headers**

Name

Value

Content-Type

`application/json`

**Request Body**

Name

Type

Mandatory

Description

invoice

string

check

trace

String

Trace No.

mid

String

check

Merchant ID

tid

String

check

Terminal ID

merchantName

String

packageName

String

check

Payment Application Package Name

batch

String

check

Batch No.

cardPan

String

check

**Masked Card Number**

sn

String

check

Terminal S/N

dateTime

String

check

yyyyMMddHHmmss

storeName

String

email

String

phone

String

type

String

check

Transaction Type:

`Purchase` `PreAuth` `AuthCompletion` `Reversal` `Refund`

oriDate

String

amount

Long

check

String

Reference Number

approvalCode

String

APPR Code

tsi

String

TSI

atc

String

ATC

tvr

String

TVR

apsn

String

APSN

appName

String

EMV APP Name

String

AID

expDate

String

Card Expire Date

String

check

Currency Name

check

# LOYALTY API | Paywizard Integration

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/quick-start-loyalty-api/loyalty-api#post-ovstrade-openloyaltypay-giftactivate)

Activate

post

/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftActivate

Header parameters

jwt-tokenstringRequiredExample: `{{ecommerceToken}}`

signstringRequiredExample: `signtext`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

clientIdstringRequired

Your unique developer ID.

loyaltyChannelstringRequired

The prepaid channel provider.

accountIdstringRequired

The unique identifier for the prepaid card.

entryTypestringRequired

The method used to input the accountId. “B”:barcode ”K”:keyed ”M”:magnetic ”P”:proximity

Example: `B`

activatingstringRequired

Set to "Y" to activate the card or "N" to not activate.

Example: `Y`

customerInfoobjectRequired

A JSON object containing the customer's details.

Show propertiesplus

Responses

chevron-right

200Success

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/paywizard-open-api/loyalty/quick-start-loyalty-api/loyalty-api#post-ovstrade-openloyaltypay-gifttransaction)

Pay

post

/ovstrade/openLoyaltyPay/giftTransaction

Header parameters

jwt-tokenstringRequiredExample: `{{ecommerceToken}}`

signstringRequiredExample: `signtext`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

clientIdstringRequired

Your unique developer ID.

tranOrderNostring · max: 60Required

The unique order ID for this payment transaction, generated by your system.

loyaltyChannelstringRequired

The prepaid channel provider.

amountstringRequired

The total transaction amount.

Example: `10.5`

tranCurrencystringRequired

The 3-letter ISO currency code for the transaction.

Example: `USD`

accountIdstringRequired

The unique identifier for the prepaid card.

entryTypestringRequired

The method used to input the accountId. “B”:barcode ”K”:keyed ”M”:magnetic ”P”:proximity

Example: `B`

nsfAllowedbooleanOptional

Non-Sufficient Funds Allowed. Set to true to permit the transaction to proceed even if the card balance is insufficient to cover the full amount.

Responses

chevron-right

200Success

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

post
